#Difficulty Beginner
BEGINNER DIFFICULTY
This difficulty level is recommended for first-time players. Players receive very large economy bonuses, while opponents play significantly worse than usual. It's recommended to use this together with the Easy Lairs, Targeting Aid, and Leave Me Alone score modifiers for an even more beginner-friendly experience.
#Difficulty Easy
EASY DIFFICULTY
Players receive economy bonuses, while opponents play worse than usual. It is recommended to use the Easy Lairs, Targeting Aid, and Leave Me Alone score modifiers to further reduce difficulty if necessary.
#Difficulty Normal
NORMAL DIFFICULTY
Opponents are subject to restrictions on the strategies they can use and do not receive either a bonus or penalty to resources.
#Difficulty Fair
FAIR (HARD) DIFFICULTY
Opponents play to their full potential, ensuring fairness, but they do not receive any resource advantages.
#Difficulty Advanced
ADVANCED DIFFICULTY
Opponents get a small resource advantage and may employ dirty tricks, playing to their full potential. This difficulty level is not recommended for new Caster of Magic players!
#Difficulty Expert
EXPERT DIFFICULTY
The player suffers a penalty of +5% city Unrest, while opponents receive a medium resource advantage and may employ dirty tricks, playing to their full potential. This level of difficulty poses a fair and beatable challenge for veteran players.
#Difficulty Master
MASTER DIFFICULTY
The player suffers penalties of +10% city Unrest and -10% Food/Gold/Production/Research output from the city, while opponents receive a medium resource advantage and play to their full potential, including dirty tricks. This level is very difficult but can still be consistently beaten using the best strategies.
#Difficulty Lunatic
LUNATIC DIFFICULTY
For an extreme challenge, the player suffers penalties of +15% city Unrest and -20% Food/Gold/Production/Research output from the city, while opponents receive a medium resource advantage and play to their full potential, including dirty tricks. Winning requires a very good strategy and at least average luck.
PHANTASM DIFFICULTY
Use at your own risk. The player suffers penalties of +20% city Unrest and -25% Food/Gold/Production/Research output from the city, while opponents receive a significant resource advantage and play to their full potential, including dirty tricks. Losing is almost guaranteed. You have been warned!
#Landsize Minimal
MINIMAL LAND
The number of land tiles is determined by the number of players on each plane.
The number of land tiles is set to 30% of normal.
 
Overland spells' cost changes per opponent more than 6:
- Rare/Very Rare summons decrease by 0.66%.
- Spells targeting terrain/cities/units decrease by 0.66%.
- Spells targeting globally increase by 3.33%.
- Uncommon/Rare/Very Rare Global Enchantments increase by 3.33%.
 
Changing this setting can significantly alter game balance, favoring different strategies, so use it at your own risk.
#Landsize Tiny
TINY LAND
The number of land tiles is determined by the number of players on each plane.
The number of land tiles is set to 50% of normal.
 
Overland spells' cost changes per opponent more than 6:
- Rare/Very Rare summons decrease by 0.66%.
- Spells targeting terrain/cities/units decrease by 0.66%.
- Spells targeting globally increase by 3.33%.
- Uncommon/Rare/Very Rare Global Enchantments increase by 3.33%.
 
Changing this setting can significantly alter game balance, favoring different strategies, so use it at your own risk.
#Landsize Small
SMALL LAND
The number of land tiles is determined by the number of players on each plane.
The number of land tiles is set to 70% of normal.
 
Overland spells' cost changes per opponent more than 6:
- Rare/Very Rare summons decrease by 0.66%.
- Spells targeting terrain/cities/units decrease by 0.66%.
- Spells targeting globally increase by 3.33%.
- Uncommon/Rare/Very Rare Global Enchantments increase by 3.33%.
 
Changing this setting can significantly alter game balance, favoring different strategies, so use it at your own risk.
#Landsize Normal
NORMAL LAND
The number of land tiles is determined by the number of players on each plane.
The number of land tiles is set to the default.
 
Overland spells' cost changes per opponent more than 6:
- Rare/Very Rare summons decrease by 0.66%.
- Spells targeting terrain/cities/units decrease by 0.66%.
- Spells targeting globally increase by 3.33%.
- Uncommon/Rare/Very Rare Global Enchantments increase by 3.33%.
 
Changing this setting can significantly alter game balance, favoring different strategies, so use it at your own risk.
#Landsize Large
LARGE LAND
The number of land tiles is determined by the number of players on each plane.
The number of land tiles is set to 133% of normal.
 
Overland spells' cost changes per opponent more than 6:
- Rare/Very Rare summons decrease by 1.33%.
- Spells targeting terrain/cities/units decrease by 1.33%.
- Spells targeting globally increase by 6.66%.
- Uncommon/Rare/Very Rare Global Enchantments increase by 6.66%.
 
Changing this setting can significantly alter game balance, favoring different strategies, so use it at your own risk.
#Landsize Huge
HUGE LAND
The number of land tiles is determined by the number of players on each plane.
The number of land tiles is set to 166% of normal.
 
Overland spells' cost changes per opponent more than 6:
- Rare/Very Rare summons decrease by 2%.
- Spells targeting terrain/cities/units decrease by 2%.
- Spells targeting globally increase by 10%.
- Uncommon/Rare/Very Rare Global Enchantments increase by 10%.
 
Changing this setting can significantly alter game balance, favoring different strategies, so use it at your own risk.
#Landsize Maximal
MAXIMAL LAND
The number of land tiles is determined by the number of players on each plane.
The number of land tiles is set to 200% of normal.
 
Overland spells' cost changes per opponent more than 6:
- Rare/Very Rare summons decrease by 2.66%.
- Spells targeting terrain/cities/units decrease by 2.66%.
- Spells targeting globally increase by 13.33%.
- Uncommon/Rare/Very Rare Global Enchantments increase by 13.33%.
 
Changing this setting can significantly alter game balance, favoring different strategies, so use it at your own risk.
#Landsize Random
RANDOM
The amount of land will be randomly chosen between 30% and 200%, with the more extreme values having the lowest chance.
#Continentsize Islands
ISLANDS
Many smaller land areas are created with extensive oceans separating them.
#Continentsize Small
SMALL CONTINENTS
Most continents are smaller than average but too large to be classified as islands.
#Continentsize Average
AVERAGE CONTINENTS
The continents are of medium size.
#Continentsize Large
LARGE CONTINENTS
The continents are larger than usual.
#Continentsize Mixed
MIXED CONTINENTS
Continent sizes vary from the smallest to the largest.
#Continentsize Random
RANDOM
One of the other options will be chosen randomly.
#Realm Nature
*SBNature.png
 NATURE REALM
 
Nature is the essence of the physical living world, driven by instinct and empowered by symbiosis, fostering harmony between creatures and their environment.
 
Nature spells harness the elemental forces of earth and water, capable of nurturing or causing destruction. Nature books shift the wizard's alignment towards good.
 
Knowledge in the Nature realm enhances skills in managing population health. The first Nature book provides an additional 4% population growth from cities, with subsequent books adding 1% each. Each Nature book also increases maximum population by +0.125.
#Realm Sorcery
*SBSorcery.png
 SORCERY REALM
 
Sorcery is the philosophy of mastering the universe through pure magic, controlled by intellect and understanding. Sorcerers aim to comprehend and perfect magic beyond the physical realm, focusing on its non-material essence.
 
Sorcery spells harness elemental forces like air, illusion, and time. They also include meta-magic spells to resist and control other wizards' spells. Sorcery books do not affect a wizard's alignment.
 
Knowledge in the Sorcery realm enhances skills in managing the academic sector. The first Sorcery book provides an additional 4% research points from cities, with subsequent books adding 1% each.
#Realm Chaos
*SBChaos.png
 CHAOS REALM
 
Chaos is the force of constant change and entropy, from primordial void to ultimate entropy. The Primordial Void, also known as the realm of Chaos, was first unleashed by a flawed Spell of Mastery. It consumed the realm of fire and corrupted everything it touched with chaos and unpredictable madness.
 
Chaos spells focus on corruption and destruction, harnessing elemental forces of change. Chaos books shift the wizard's alignment towards evil.
 
Knowledge in the Chaos realm enhances skills in managing power generation. The first Chaos book provides an additional 4% power from cities, with subsequent books adding 1% each.
#Realm Death
*SBDeath.png
 DEATH REALM
 
Death studies the left-hand aspect of the Primal Forces, guiding beings to rest and deeply tied to night and the underworld. Balanced, it stabilizes and preserves existence; excessive, it causes stagnation and decay. The Death realm's negative reputation stems from its association with dark practices.
 
Death spells control the dead, harness forces of darkness, and bring disease and misfortune upon enemies. Death books shift the wizard's alignment towards evil.
 
Knowledge in the Death realm enhances skills in managing material wealth. The first Death book provides an additional 4% gold from cities, with subsequent books adding 1% each.
#Realm Life
*SBLife.png
 LIFE REALM
 
Life studies the right-hand aspect of the Primal Forces, guiding beings towards consciousness, activity, and creation. Balanced, it brings vitality, love, and inspiration; excessive, it can become dogmatic and totalitarian. Deities of Life are often self-centered and claim sole authority.
 
Life spells focus on healing, protection, and inspirational enchantments. Life books shift the wizard's alignment towards good.
 
Knowledge in the Life realm enhances skills in managing productivity. The first Life book provides an additional 4% production from cities, with subsequent books adding 1% each.
#Retort Alchemist
*ux53.png
 ALCHEMIST
The wizard is an expert in the art of Alchemy.
- Allows the wizard to convert gold to mana and mana to gold at a rate of 1:1.
- All non-summoned units trained by the wizard from non-Barbarian cities gain magic weapons.
- Alchemist's Guild cost 15% cheaper.
- Costs 2 picks.
#Retort Warlord
*ux53.png
 WARLORD
The wizard is a renowned militarist.
- All non-summoned units under the wizard's control have their veterancy level increased by one.
- Allows non-summoned units to exceed their normal veterancy limit by one level.
- Barracks, War College, Armory, Fighter's Guild, Armorer's Guild, City Wall, Fortification, Hillfort, and Warlord's Hold cost 15% cheaper.
- Warlord could utilize global ability of Warlord's Hold regardless of home race.
- Costs 2 picks.
- Mutually exclusive with the Tactician retort at the start of the game.
#Retort Channeler
*ux53.png
 CHANNELER
The wizard has mastered the art of channeling spellcraft.
- Allows the wizard to cast spells without range penalties.
- Reduces spell range penalties during banishment by half.
- Reduces overall spell upkeep by 50%.
- Reduces the cost of casting spells in combat by 12%.
- Costs 2 picks.
#Retort Archmage
*ux53.png
 ARCHMAGE
The wizard is a renowned master in teaching and training spell casting.
- Increases both already acquired and newly produced skill points (SP) by 50%.
#Retort Artificer
*ux53.png
 ARTIFICER
The wizard is a master craftsman who is an expert in magical engineering.
- Reduces the cost of making items/artifacts by 50%.
- Starts the game with the "Enchant Item" spell already researched.
- The "Create Artifact" spell will be the first researchable Rare level spell.
- All mechanical units trained by the wizard gain +1 Melee/Range Attack, +1 Armor, +1 Resistance, +1 Movement Point, and magic weapons.
#Retort Conjurer
*ux53.png
 CONJURER
The wizard is an expert in conjuring magical creatures.
- Reduces the casting costs of all summoning spells by 25%.
- Reduces the research costs of all summoning spells by 25%.
- Reduces the total upkeep cost of Fantastic creatures by 25%.
- Starts the game with the "Summoning Circle" spell already researched.
#Retort Sage Master
*ux53.png
 SAGE MASTER
The wizard is a renowned scholar.
- Increases total research points generated each turn by 33%.
- Increases research points by 15 RP each turn.
- Library, University, Sage's Guild, Academy, and Ludus Agoge cost 15% cheaper.
#Retort Myrran
*ux53.png
 MYRRAN
The wizard is native to the plane of Myrror.
- Starts the game with a fortress on the plane of Myrror.
- Allows the player to choose Myrran races as their home race.
- Adjusts the starting positions of AI wizards accordingly.
#Retort Guardian
*ux53.png
 GUARDIAN
The wizard is respected as the guardian protector of his people.
- Increases the maximum population of the home race's city by 6 units.
- In combat, all units controlled by the wizard gain +10% To-Hit, +10% To-Defend, and +1 Resistance when defending the city controlled by the wizard.
- Costs 2 picks.
#Retort Benefactor
*ux53.png
 BENEFACTOR
The wizard is well-known as a benefactor who willingly lends a hand to those who serve under them.
- Starts the game with 30 fame, and the "Heroic Heart" spell already researched.
- All heroes controlled by the wizard gain +2 Melee/Range Attack, +1 Armor, and +1 Resistance.
- 2x chance for artifact merchants, and 4x chance for mercenaries offer.
- If have enough gold, a hero is guaranteed to appear for hire in January, an item merchant appears in July and mercenaries always show up in April and October starting in 1502. 
- Heroes and mercenaries offering to join will be at a 1 level higher than usual and hiring cost of them do not increase by their level.
#Retort Runemaster
*ux53.png
 RUNEMASTER
The wizard has mastered the power of rune language.
- Reduces research costs of Arcane spells by 50%.
- Reduces casting costs of overland spells (except Arcane, summons, and enchantments) by 25%.
- Reduces casting costs of overland Arcane spells (except item creation, and summons) by 50%.
- Reduces casting costs of combat Arcane spells by 25%.
- The effects of dispel-type spells cast by the wizard are 100% more effective.
- Starts the game with the "Dispel Magic" spell already researched.
#Retort Charismatic
*ux53.png
 CHARISMATIC
The wizard possesses an unnatural presence that dramatically improves his dealings with others.
- Reduces the costs for hiring heroes, mercenaries, and purchasing magical items by half.
- Reduces the unrest level in all cities owned by the wizard by 1.
- Halves all diplomatic penalties from negative actions.
- Doubles all positive diplomatic effects.
- Offers made by the wizard are significantly more likely to be accepted.
#Retort Specialist
*ux53.png
 SPECIALIST
The wizard invests their skill and effort into mastering their primary realm.
- Reduces the casting costs for spells in the wizard's primary realm by 12%.
- Reduces the research costs for spells in the wizard's primary realm by 12%.
- Increases dispel resistance for spells in the wizard's primary realm by 50%.
(Primary realm is determined by the realm with the highest number of books. In case of a tie, specialist realms are prioritized in this order: Nature, Sorcery, Chaos, Life, and Death.)
#Retort Tactician
*ux53.png
 TACTICIAN
The wizard is renowned for their skill in maneuvering troops in combat.
- The wizard can sneak attack, making defenders lose their first action unless it's another wizard's fortress, they have Tactician, or Supernatural Primal power protects them.
- All the wizard's units gain +1 Armor.
- The wizard's teleporting units gain First Strike.
- The wizard's Non-Corporeal units gain Negate First Strike.
- The wizard's units with a terrain bonus gain double the bonus, First Strike, and Negate First Strike.
- Gets a bonus in strategic combat.
- Costs 2 picks.
- Mutually exclusive with the Warlord retort at the start of the game.
#Retort Procurator
*ux53.png
 PROCURATOR
The wizard is an expert in managerial and statecraft.
- Reduces "Indirect Control" and "Banished" city penalties by 25%.
- Triples the "Administrative Skill" bonus.
#Retort Cult Leader
*ux53.png
 CULT LEADER
The Wizard is the leader of a religion/cult with strong influence over the believers.
- Increases the power generated by religious buildings by 100%.
- Increases the unrest reduction by religious buildings by 50% (rounded down).
(Religious buildings include the Shrine, Monastery, Witches' Convent, Cathedral, and Temple. Certain buildings and city enchantments may be sanctified into religious buildings through certain spells.)
#Retort Astrologer
*ux53.png
 ASTROLOGER
The wizard is an expert in predicting and manipulating destiny by reading stars.
- Nodes controlled by the wizard produce +2 power for each year passed since the start of the game.
- Immune to spell-countering effects from nodes.
- Costs 2 picks.
#Retort Enchanter
*ux53.png
 ENCHANTER
The wizard is an expert in the art of enchantment.
- Reduces the cost of enchantment/curse spells cast by the wizard by 25%.
- Increases dispel resistance of all enchantments/curses cast by the wizard by 150%.
- Costs 2 picks.
#Race Barbarian
*worker0.png
 BARBARIAN
Barbarians are proud warriors, known for their martial skill and provoking little hostility, except from the most arrogant races.
 
Barbarian cities grow quickly but cannot build the Armorer's Guild, Fantastic Stable, Alchemist's Guild, Monastery, Mechanician's Guild, or Bank.
 
Barbarian units excel with thrown weapons, have higher accuracy, pathfinding abilities, and a unique, fast naval unit.
 
Barbarian's racial Unrest: Dark Elves+2, Draconians+2, High Elves+2, High Men+2, Klackons+3, Nomads+1, Orcs+2, Xuanyuan+1, Goblins+3.
#Race Beastmen
*worker1.png
 BEASTMEN
Born from the fusion of humans and magic crystals, Beastmen have a beast-like appearance. They are cautious of less humanoid races but strive for closer ties with humanoid ones.
 
Beastman cities generate 0.5 Power per Population but cannot build the Maritime Guild, Hangar, Brewery, Hillfort, Warlord's Hold, Witches' Convent, or Cathedral.
 
Beastmen military units gain +1 Health and Attack.
 
Beastman's racial Unrest: Draconians+2, Gnolls+2, High Men+1, Klacklons+3, Orcs+2, Trolls+2, Xuanyuan+1, Rakhshasa+3, Goblins+3.
#Race Dark Elf
*worker2.png
 DARK ELF
Dark Elves originated from the Elven Civil War of ancient past, their society emphasis and pride on magical supremacy over their Arcanian kin.
 
Dark Elf cities grow slowly but generate 1 Power per Population and cannot build the Maritime Guild, Hangar, Brewery, Hillfort, Warlord's Hold, Witches' Convent, or Cathedral.
 
Dark Elf units gain +2 Resistance, and all their military units have Magical Ranged Attacks.
 
Dark Elf's racial Unrest: Barbarians+2, Dwarves+2, Gnolls+2, High Men+1, Klackons+3, Lizardmen+2, Orcs+2, Xuanyuan+1, Rakhshasa+2, Goblins+3.
#Race Draconian
*worker3.png
 DRACONIAN
Draconians, descendants of drakes, value strength and often clash with other proud races for dominance.
 
Draconian cities generate 0.5 Power per Population but cannot build the Fantastic Stable, Fortification, Brewery, Hillfort, Warlord's Hold, Witches' Convent, or Temple.
 
Draconian units have +1 Resistance, and non-mechanical units gain +1 Armor, Fire Breath, and Flying abilities.
 
Draconian's racial Unrest: Barbarians+2, Beastmen+2, Gnolls+2, High Men+1, Klackons+3, Trolls+2, Xuanyuan+1, Rakhshasa+2, Hawkmen+3, Goblins+3.
#Race Dwarf
*worker4.png
 DWARF
Dwarves are diligent, materialistic, and highly skilled in mining and engineering. While not inherently magical, they have strong resistance to magic.
 
Dwarf cities generate 50% more tax revenue, 100% more from minerals, and have 50% higher worker productivity but grow very slowly and cannot build the Stable, Magic Market, Sage's Guild, Merchant's Guild, Hillfort, Warlord's Hold, Temple, or Monument.
 
Dwarf units gain +2 Resistance, +1 Health for infantry units, and +3 Armor for mechanical units.
 
Dwarf's racial Unrest: Dark Elves+2, High Elves+2, High Men+1, Klackons+3, Xuanyuan+1, Hawkmen+2, Goblins+3.
#Race Gnoll
*worker5.png
 GNOLL
Gnolls are natural predators, feared among humanoid races for their headhunting skills. However, they value honor and respect individuals from other races with strong martial traditions.
 
Gnoll cities cannot build the Fantastic Stable, Maritime Guild, Monastery, University, Cathedral, or Temple.
 
Gnoll units exhibit greater physical strength, with each unit possesses +2 Attack and +1 Movement.
 
Gnoll's racial Unrest: Beastmen+2, Dark Elves+2, Draconians+2, High Elves+2, High Men+3, Klackons+3, Nomads+2, Orcs+2, Xuanyuan+2, Goblins+3.
#Race Halfling
*worker6.png
 HALFLING
Halflings are a peaceful, carefree race, thriving without specific adversaries. They excel in farming and labor but shy away from military pursuits.
 
Halflings are curious and open-minded, generating 1 Research per Population, and their Farmers produce +2 Food. However, their cities cannot build the Monument, Brewery, Hangar, Barracks, Armorer's Guild, Hillfort, Warlord's Hold, Witches' Convent, or Temple.
 
Halfling units, though weak, possess supernatural luck, enhancing their resilience and accuracy.
 
Halfling's racial Unrest: Klackons+1, Goblins+1.
#Race High Elf
*worker7.png
 HIGH ELF
High Elves are long-lived forest dwellers skilled in archery and magic. They see themselves as the first civilized race of Arcanus and often look down on less magically advanced races.
 
High Elf cities generate 0.5 Power per Population but grow slowly and cannot build the Maritime Guild, Hangar, Brewery, Hillfort, Warlord's Hold, Witches' Convent, or Temple.
 
High Elf units have the Forester ability, +1 Resistance, and +10% To-Hit.
 
High Elf's racial Unrest: Barbarians+2, Dwarves+2, Gnolls+2, High Men+1, Klackons+3, Lizardmen+2, Orcs+2, Xuanyuan+1, Rakhshasa+2, Goblins+3.
#Race High Men
*worker8.png
 HIGH MEN
High Men are a culturally advanced human race with strong religious beliefs, known for their affinity for miracles and magic, excellence in architecture, and low regard for other races.
 
High Man cities have a -15% building and mechanical unit costs but cannot build the Fantastic Stable, Hillfort, Warlord's Hold, Brewery, Hangar, Witches' Convent, or Temple.
 
High Man units suffer -1 Resistance, and their religious and racial persecution causes significant tension.
 
High Man's racial Unrest: Rakhshasa+3, Gnolls+3, Halfling+1, High Men+1, Klacklon+4, Lizardmen+3, Trolls+3, Goblins+4, all others+2.
#Race Klackon
*worker9.png
 KLACKONS
Klackons, an insectoid race brought to Arcanus by a mysterious "flying castle," are enigmatic and often distrusted by other races.
 
Klackon cities grow quickly, with Workers are producing 50% faster, but they cannot build the Fantastic Stable, Hangar, Brewery, Coliseum, Hillfort, Warlord's Hold, Witches' Convent, Monastery, Cathedral, Temple, or Merchant's Guild.
 
Klackon units gain +2 Defense from their natural exoskeletal carapace.
 
Klackon's racial Unrest: Halfling+1, High Men+4, Klackons-3, all others+3.
#Race Lizardmen
*worker10.png
 LIZARDMEN
Lizardmen are natural amphibic reptilian with strong piety, often regarded as less advanced by more civilized races.
 
Lizardman cities gain +0.25 Max Population per swamp tile but cannot build the Miner's Guild, Warlord's Hold, Witches' Convent, Cathedral, Brewery, Bank, Fantastic Stable, or Shipyard.
 
Lizardman units can move in water, settlers move faster, and have +1 Health but suffer -1 Resistance.
 
Lizardman's racial Unrest: Beastmen+2, Dark Elves+2, High Elves+1, High Men+3, Klackons+3, Nomads+2, Orcs+2, Xuanyuan+1, Hawkmen+3, Goblins+3.
#Race Nomad
*worker11.png
 NOMAD
Nomads, a human race roaming Arcanian wasteland, have a refined culture built on caravan trading. Their children excel in archery, horse riding, and resisting magical manipulation from an early age.
 
Nomad cities receive a +50% Trade Bonus, gain +1 Food per desert/tundra and +2 Food per grassland tile, and +0.5 Max Population per desert tile but cannot build Granary, Hillfort, Warlord's Hold, Witches' Convent, Cathedral, Fortification, or Hangar.
 
Nomad units gain +3 Resistance, and most are equipped with bows by default.
 
Nomad's racial Unrest: Goblins+3, Gnolls+2, Klackons+3, Lizardmen+2, Trolls+2, Rakhshasa+2, High Men+1, Barbarians+1.
#Race Orc
*worker12.png
 ORC
Orcs are a civilized porcine race with an ancient rivalry with the Elves. Driven by strong desires and high ambitions, they pursue their goals without restraint, though they lack exceptional skill in any area.
 
Orc cities grow quickly but cannot build the Hangar, Brewery, Hillfort, Warlord's Hold, or Cathedral.
 
Orc regular units have reduced Upkeep costs. Their mechanical units could perform tactical retreat.
 
Orc's racial Unrest: Barbarians+2, Beastmen+2, Dark Elves+2, High Elves+2, High Men+1, Klackons+3, Lizardmen+2, Trolls+2, Rakhshasa+2, Hawkmen+2, Goblins+3.
#Race Troll
*worker13.png
 TROLL
Trolls, savage descendants of Nature spirits stranded on Myrror, are powerful warriors with immense strength and extraordinary regeneration, requiring complete destruction of their bodies to prevent their revival.
 
Troll cities gain +0.25 Max Population per tundra tile but cannot build the Maritime Guild, University, Monastery, or Fantastic Stable.
 
Troll units boast exceptional strength, toughness, and regeneration but have fewer Figures and higher Upkeep costs.
 
Troll's racial Unrest: Beastmen+2, Dark Elves+2, Draconian+2, High Elves+2, High Men+3, Klackons+3, Nomads+2, Orcs+2, Xuanyuan+1, Goblins+3.
#Race Xuanyuan
*worker22.png
 XUANYUAN
Xuanyuan, an advanced human race that once cultivating immortality on Arcanus, now resides in Myrror after being exiled for resisting an ancient magical empire.
 
Xuanyuan farmers produce +1 Food, cities have +25% Max Population, but cannot build the Hangar, Brewery, Witches' Convent, Temple, Cathedral, Hillfort, or Warlord's Hold.
 
Xuanyuan units suffer -1 Armor. Their regular units have +2 figures while their mechanical units have +5 Health.
 
Xuanyuan's racial Unrest: Barbarian+1, Beastmen+1, Dark Elves+1, Draconian+1, Dwarves+1, Gnolls+2, High Elves+1, High Men+2, Klackons+3, Lizardmen+1, Trolls+2, Rakhshasa+2, Hawkmen+2, Goblins+3.
#Race Rakhshasa
*worker23.png
 RAKHSHASA
Rakhshasas are deeply spiritual yet formidable carnivorous forest guardians. Their practice of consuming defeated enemies unsettles other races.
 
Rakhshasa cities gain 0.5 Power per Population, and +0.25 Max Population per forest tile but cannot build Mechanician's Guild, Maritime Guild, Brewery, Witches' Convent, Cathedral, Hillfort, or Warlord's Hold.
 
Rakhshasa units have -20% cost, +1 Armor, +1 Movement, and the Forester ability.
 
Rakhshasa's racial Unrest: Beastmen+3, Dark Elves+2, Draconians+2, High Elves+2, High Men+3, Klacklons+3, Nomads+2, Orcs+2, Xuanyuan+2, Goblins+3.
#Race Hawkmen
*worker24.png
 HAWKMEN
Hawkmen are a winged humanoid race with a mysterious origin. Some believe they are children of the Primal Forces, while others think they are magical bird-human hybrids.
 
Hawkman cities grow slowly but gain +0.25 Max Population per mountain tile, and 0.5 Power per Population. They cannot build Dock, Shipyard, Stable, Bank, Brewery, Warlord's Hold, or City Wall.
 
Hawkman units can fly, have the First Strike ability, but include one less Figure.
 
Hawkman's racial Unrest: Draconians+3, Dwarves+2, High Men+2, Klackons+3, Lizardmen+3, Orcs+2, Xuanyuan+2, Goblins+3.
#Race Goblin
*worker25.png
 GOBLIN
Goblins are child-sized humanoid fungi, notorious for their cunning and cruelty. Most races view them as troublesome pests rather than a race to engage with.
 
Goblin cities grow very quickly but face high Unrest, tax avoidance, and cannot build the Armorer's Guild, Animist's Guild, Maritime Guild, Fantastic Stable, Oracle, Wizard's Guild, Monastery, Merchant's Guild, Farmer's Market, or Fortification.
 
Goblin regular units have +2 Figures, -20% cost, -1 Food upkeep, and most melee units can bud clones, but they suffer -10% To-Defend. Mechanical units also gain +2 Figures but -50% Health and -33% Attack.
 
Goblin's racial Unrest: Halfling+1, High Men+4, Goblins+2, all others+3.
#Patrolbutton
PATROL
Sets the selected units to Patrol state. They will remain stationary and will not request orders for the remainder of the game, unless manually canceled using the hotkey "Esc".
#Waitbutton
WAIT
Skip issuing orders for this stack until all others are processed. Use the hotkey "W". Pressing "Back" auto-selects units that have already moved.
 
Pressing "Space" centers on the selected unit. If no units are selected, it centers on your Fortress city.
 
You can use "Ctrl" + "1" to "9" to save a map location, and "1" to "9" to reset the view to that location.
#Donebutton
DONE
The selected units will do nothing else for the turn, and their remaining Movement is set to zero. Use the hotkey "d".
#GAME
GAME
The game button and the hotkey "G" bring up the game options screen. This screen allows you to load and save games, change settings, and surrender to return to the main menu.
#OVERLANDSPELLS
SPELLS
The spells button and the hotkey "S" open your spell book, which lists only the spells that can be cast overland.
#ARMIES
ARMIES
The army list button and the hotkey "A" bring up a complete list of all armies under your control. From this screen, you can equip your heroes, manage your artifacts, and dismiss units.
#MAGIC
MAGIC
The magic button and the hotkey "M" bring you to the magic income screen, where sources of magic power are detailed. From here, you can distribute your power between research, mana crystal production, and improving casting skill.
#OVERLANDCITIES
CITIES
Shows a list of the wizard's cities and income of various resources in each city.
#OVERLANDINFO
INFO
The Info button and the hotkey "I" open a menu listing the available advisors in your empire.
#PLANE
PLANE
The Plane button and the hotkey "P" change your map view to the other plane. Please note that the two planes can differ in size, so the same objects might have different distances between them after switching planes.
#OVERLANDWIZARDS
WIZARDS
The Wizards button and the hotkey "Z" open the Wizards screen, where you can see all other wizards you have contacted, request an audience with them, and view all global enchantments.
#OTHERBUTTON
SPECIAL ACTION
The "Other Action" button and the hotkey "E" allow your units to use their special abilities:
- Spirits can meld with nodes to draw magical power from them.
- Settlers can found new outposts.
- Shamans and Priests can "Purify" corrupted land.
- Engineers can build roads.
#NEXTTURN
NEXT MONTH BUTTON
Clicking this button or pressing the hotkey "N" ends your turn and allows other players to move.
Maintenance costs are paid when clicking the button, but these costs will be covered entirely by your income if possible.
Any remaining income will be added to your treasury after all other players have ended their turns.
#MINIMAP
MINIMAP
The reduced map displays the entire plane in a condensed form. Clicking on it will change your current view. The white box corresponds to your normal viewing window.
#GOLD
TOTAL GOLD
This is the total amount of Gold in your treasury.
#MANA
TOTAL MANA CRYSTALS
This is the total number of Mana Crystals in your reserve that you can draw from to cast spells.
#GOLDINCOME
GOLD INCOME
The amount of Gold you gain or lose each turn from taxes, maintenance, etc.
#FOODINCOME
FOOD INCOME
The amount of excess or deficit Food produced to feed your troops and citizens.
If negative, units will starve to death or desert your army.
If positive, every 2 excess Food is sold for 1 Gold, which is added to your Gold income.
#MANAINCOME
MANA INCOME
The amount of Mana Crystals obtained from Power, minus the amount spent on spell and creature maintenance.
#OVERLANDMOVES
COLLECTIVE MOVEMENT
The total amount and type of Movement available for the selected units when moved together as a group.
Please note that all units in the group will use the displayed Movement Type, even if they have different Movement Types available. They will spend Movement points according to that displayed movement type, which can result in the unit moving slower or faster than it would if moving alone.
#ARMYUPKEEP
TOTAL ARMY UPKEEP
This is the total amount that you are spending on Food, Gold, and Mana Crystal each turn to support your armies.
#ANVIL
ANVIL
Allows you to destroy unwanted magical items, gaining back half of the original cost of the item in Mana crystals.
#ALCHEMYBUTTON
ALCHEMY
The Alchemy button or pressing "A" allows you to convert Gold to Mana crystals or vice versa. You can also use the "Space" key to reverse the amounts of Gold and Mana on the slider.
#SORT
SORT
The Sort button allows cycling through sorting the displayed city data based on each column.
The selected column to sort by is displayed in a different color.
#MSPOWERINCOME
POWER INCOME
This area shows all sources that produce magic Power, RP, or SP.
The total magic Power income can be distributed between producing MP, SP, and RP using the wands below.
#MSRESWAND
RESEARCH WAND
This wand determines how much of your total Power income is spent on producing Research (RP).
If the wand is full, all the power is allocated to researching spells. If the wand is empty, no RP is produced.
Clicking on the tip of the wand can lock it, preventing the amount from changing.
#MSMANAWAND
MANA WAND
This wand determines how much of your total Power income is converted to Mana crystals (MP).
If the wand is full, all the power is distilled into raw Mana crystals. If the wand is empty, no MP is produced.
Clicking on the tip of the wand can lock it, preventing the amount from changing.
#MSSKILLWAND
SKILL WAND
This wand determines how much of your total Power income is used to improve your Spellcasting ability (SP).
If the wand is full, all the power is transferred to your Skill pool. If the wand is empty, no SP is produced.
Clicking on the tip of the wand can lock it, preventing the amount from changing.
#MSMANA
MANA SPENDING
This area displays all recurring Mana costs to maintain spells and creatures, along with the remaining Mana income.
#MSSKILL
CASTING SKILL
This area shows how much casting skill is improved each turn and the total casting skill available in each overland turn or combat.
- All SP produced is stored permanently in the Skill Pool.
- Your casting skill is the square root of all SP in the Skill Pool.
- Combat and Overland Casting Skill are usually the same, but buildings can contribute to increasing only one or the other.
- Hero skill is the skill contributed by Caster Heroes stationed in your fortress, which is 1/5th of their total Caster ability and will be used to progress your overland spell at the end of your turn.
#MSRES
SPELL RESEARCH
This area shows the spell currently being researched and the number of turns left until completion.
Left-clicking in this area will open the Apprentice book.
#WRELATION
RELATION, TREATIES
This area shows all of the wizard's treaties with other wizards and your relations with them.
- Relation levels range from Hate (-100), then Troubled, Tense, Restless, Unease, Neutral, Relaxed, Calm, Peaceful, Friendly, to Harmony (+100).
- Treaties can be War, Wizard's Pact, or Alliance.
- A Wizard's Pact is an agreement where you agree not to enter within 2 tiles of any of that player's cities, and in exchange, they can't attack you or use hostile spells against your empire.
- An Alliance is an agreement of mutual military aid and allows you to enter their territory at any time you want.
#CITYPEOPLE
CITIZENS
This area shows the city population. Each icon represents 1000 people. Citizens are displayed in the order of Mandatory Farmers, Additional Farmers, Workers, and Rebels.
- Farmers produce 4 Food and 0.5 production each. Mandatory Farmers are responsible for producing the Food required by the citizens and cannot be changed to other jobs.
- Workers produce 2 Production.
- Rebels produce nothing and pay no taxes.
#CITYRES
CITY RESOURCES
This section details city resources:
- Food icons represent consumption and surplus for armies. Shortages (grey icons) shrink city's population.
- Production icons display points for buildings or unit training.
- Gold icons show maintenance and surplus for use. Shortages (grey icons) draw from empire income or treasury. Maintenance is prioritized, potentially disbanding troops to balance.
- Power icons show generated magic. Deficits (grey icons) deduct from overall Power pool or Mana reserves.
- Research icons show generated spell research. Deficits (grey icons) deduct from overall Research pool.
Small icon represents 1 resource unit, large icon represents 10 resource units.
#CITYPRODUCING
CURRENT PRODUCTION
This area shows what is currently being produced in the city, the total Production cost, the current progress, and the turns remaining until completion.
#CITYRALLY
RALLY BUTTON
The rally button allows you to order all troops produced in the city to move to a selected location.
#CITYRAZE
RAZE BUTTON
The raze button allows you to destroy this city.
Razing duration is proportional to the number of buildings and city population and earns gold equal to one-third of the production cost of the buildings being sold.
Up to 4 buildings and 2500 people can be "removed" each turn.
#CITYBUY
BUY BUTTON
Allows spending gold to instantly complete the current production. The cost is 2 gold for each point of production still needed to complete the item.
#CITYCHANGE
CHANGE BUTTON
Opens the production screen where you can select which buildings and units to produce and assign them to a production queue.
#SPELLBOOKS
SPELL BOOKS
The spell books in the various realms represent the rank of spells the wizard can understand and the number of spells they can research:
- 1 book allows learning common spells.
- 2 books allow learning uncommon spells.
- 3 books allow learning rare spells.
- 4 books allow learning very rare spells.
- More than 5 books allow research spells of that realm 5% faster for each additional book.
- More than 6 books allow the casting cost of spells of that realm to be 3% cheaper for each additional book.
Wizards can research one spell that is one rank higher than what they can normally comprehend.
 
For more detailed information, please refer to the manual.
#FAME
FAME
Fame increases the chance of mercenaries and merchants showing up, boosts the likelihood of higher-tier heroes appearing for hire, and reduces the Gold maintenance of your army by one for each point of Fame.
#MRELATION
RELATION
Relation levels range from Hate (-100), progressing through Troubled, Tense, Restless, Unease, Neutral, Relaxed, Calm, Peaceful, Friendly, and culminating in Harmony (+100).
#TREATY NONE
NO TREATY
You haven't formed any agreement with this wizard.
Unless they are Lawful or Peaceful, they might decide to attack you or cast hostile spells against you to "test the waters," even without formally declaring war.
#TREATY WIZARD'S PACT
WIZARD'S PACT
You agreed not to send any military troops within a range of two tiles of this wizard's city.
In exchange, this wizard will not attack your units and will not cast any hostile spells against you. Relations improve over time as long as the treaty stays in effect.
They might also cancel any hostile spells they have already cast on your cities over time.
If you break this rule on three consecutive turns, the treaty becomes void, but otherwise, it doesn't expire unless formally cancelled by one of the players involved.
#TREATY ALLIANCE
ALLIANCE
You agreed to aid each other in need by providing military support.
You can send troops into this wizard's territory without penalty, and relations improve at a fast rate.
This wizard will accept any requests to declare war on other wizards you are already at war with but might ask you to declare war on their enemies as well.
#TREATY WAR
WAR
You are at war with this wizard. They will actively attack your troops and cast hostile spells against you.
#PERSONALITY MANIACAL
MANIACAL
Maniacal wizards are afraid of everyone, reducing positive diplomatic effects by 25% and increasing negative ones by 50%. There are absolutely no positive effects from this personality on diplomacy, and they are most inclined to cast Overland spells that bring harm to others.
#PERSONALITY RUTHLESS
RUTHLESS
Ruthless wizards are difficult to deal with, adding only +10 points to each diplomatic decision. These wizards don't prioritize dispelling city curses or defending their empire but enjoy bringing harm to others.
#PERSONALITY AGGRESSIVE
AGGRESSIVE
Aggressive wizards are more inclined to go to war compared to peaceful or lawful wizards, but less likely than chaotic, maniacal, or ruthless ones. You can still reason with them through diplomacy and treaties, adding a moderate +20 points to their diplomatic decisions.
#PERSONALITY CHAOTIC
CHAOTIC
Chaotic wizards are entirely unpredictable. One turn they may be peaceful and non-violent, while the next they might go to war over any minor excuse. Unlike other personalities, Chaotic wizards have a random diplomacy modifier that is re-rolled every turn, ranging from +1 to +50.
#PERSONALITY LAWFUL
LAWFUL
Lawful wizards will never attack without a formal declaration of war unless they are attacked first. Negative diplomatic actions, however, have double effectiveness against them. Any diplomatic decision they make is affected by a +40 modifier, making it much more likely for the wizard to understand the good intentions of others. These wizards don't tolerate city curses and will dispel them as soon as possible.
#PERSONALITY PEACEFUL
PEACEFUL
Peaceful wizards are eager to maintain peaceful relations and will never attack without a declaration of war unless they are first attacked. Diplomatic decisions made by this wizard benefit from a +65 positive modifier, making it quite easy to manipulate such wizards in your favor. However, this modifier has a reversed effect when requesting negative actions from them, such as breaking their treaties.
#OBJECTIVE PRAGMATIST
PRAGMATIST
The pragmatist seeks a balance between military build up, expansion, and spell research.
#OBJECTIVE MILITARIST
MILITARIST
The militarist seeks to build great and powerful armies. They prioritize building and maintaining large, powerful armies and are likely to declare war on wizards weaker than themselves without provocation. Their preferred types of spells are summoning and unit enchantments. Militarist wizards might declare war on players with weak armies, seeing them as unfit for ruling an empire.
#OBJECTIVE THEURGIST
THEURGIST
The theurgist focuses resources on spell research. They prefer casting global and city enchantments more frequently than other wizards.
#OBJECTIVE PERFECTIONIST
PERFECTIONIST
The perfectionist wishes to develop and maintain huge, prosperous cities. They concentrate on creating new buildings and city improvements. The perfectionist prefers casting city and unit enchantments most and does not tolerate curses affecting their cities.
#OBJECTIVE EXPANSIONIST
EXPANSIONIST
The expansionist is primarily interested in expanding controlled territory. They prioritize building naval buildings and are likely to declare war on weaker wizards without provocation. Their preferred types of spells are summoning, and they equally dislike casting curses on enemy cities and wasting resources on dispelling city curses from their own, preferring conquest instead.
#OBJECTIVE NARCISSIST
NARCISSIST
A narcissist wizard wants to be the center of attention at all times. They prefer to invest resources into boosting their own casting skill and dislike employing heroes, creating artifacts, or training their normal soldiers. Narcissist wizards enjoy demonstrating their power by casting curses on others and also put effort into dispelling such curses from their own empire.
#HISTORIAN
HISTORIAN
The historian graph shows the total power of each wizard's empire. Click the button in the top left corner to cycle between statistics:
- Overall: A sum of Army, Power Income, and Population.
- Army: The total strength of the wizard's armies, including both regular units and summoned creatures.
- Power Income: The amount of raw magical power the wizard obtains each turn.
- Spell Power: The amount of casting skill and research progress the wizard has.
- Population: The total population from all cities in the wizard's empire.
#UNITBUILD
UNITS / BUILDINGS
Toggle between the list of available units and buildings on the left side.
#LASTFIRST
LAST / FIRST BUTTON
Toggle between adding new items to the end or the beginning of the queue.
Please note that adding anything to the beginning of the queue that has a requirement already in the queue is not possible.
#HOUSINGTRADE
HOUSING/TRADE/REPEAT
This button toggles between three possible options for the town's production when it's not building a unit or structure. These options always appear at the end of the queue:
- Trade Goods: Produces 1 Gold for every 2 Production hammers.
- Housing: Increases population growth based on the following formula:
  (170*(Max Pop+Racial Growth/10 - 8) / 13) * (1.3-0.1*Population), with a minimum of 40.
  This amount is reduced proportionally by non-mandatory Farmers or Rebels.
- Repeat: Continuously repeats the last item in the queue if it was a unit.
#CLEAR
CLEAR BUTTON
Removes everything from the building queue on the right side.
#UVMELEE
MELEE ATTACK
Each icon represents a chance to deal 1 point of damage in Melee combat. A gold icon represents a bonus due to spells or special abilities. A darkened icon represents a penalty. The chance "To-Hit" is displayed in the upper right corner.
Sword inside the icon represents weapon upgrade.
Dim swords represent normal weapons without upgrade.
Blue swords represent magical weapons upgrade.
White swords represent Mithril weapons upgrade.
Purple swords represent Adamantium weapons upgrade.
#UVRANGED
RANGED ATTACK
Each icon represents a chance to deal 1 point of damage by a Ranged attack. A gold icon represents a bonus due to spells or special abilities. A darkened icon represents a penalty. The chance "To-Hit" is displayed in the upper right corner but is further penalized by 10% if the target is at least 4 tiles away, and another 3% for each tile beyond that unless the Ranged attack is Magical or performed by a hero.
#UVARMOR
ARMOR
Armor, also referred to as Defense icons, each represent a chance to reduce incoming damage by 1 point. A gold icon represents a bonus due to spells or special abilities. A darkened icon represents a penalty. The chance "To-Defend" is displayed in the upper right corner.
#UVRESIST
RESISTANCE
Each icon represents a Resistance value of one. A gold icon represents a bonus due to spells or special abilities. A darkened icon represents a penalty. Each point of Resistance represents a 10% chance to avoid being affected by a hostile spell effect or Poison. Resistance does not reduce the damage taken from Magical sources.
#UVHITS
HEALTH
Each icon represents one Health Point. A gold icon represents a bonus due to spells or special abilities. A darkened icon represents damage already taken.
 
If the unit suffers irrecoverable damage, that damage can't be healed until the end of combat. Additionally, if at least half of the damage on the unit was irrecoverable when it died, it cannot be raised from the dead by any spell or ability.
If at least half of the damage on the unit was Undead-Creating damage when it died, it will become undead to serve the opponent's side if the combat was lost.
#UVHITCHANCE
CHANCE TO-HIT, TO-DEFEND
This is the percentage chance of each point of Attack, Ranged, Thrown, Breath, or Defense resulting in 1 damage dealt or blocked.
- To-Hit represents the chance that applies to all attacks not otherwise mentioned
- To-Range/Melee/Thorwn/Breath represents the hit chance for specific type of attacks
- To-Defend represents the block chance for each damage. Please note that the chance To-Defend affects the first 15 defense rolls a figure makes only; the 16th defense icon and beyond always have a 30% chance of blocking damage.
#SORCERY CONJUNCTION
SORCERY CONJUNCTION
The rising triad of blue stars aligns, reducing the cost of Sorcery and Global Enchantment spells by 33%. All spells have double the normal resistance to being dispelled, and SP generated from power is doubled.
#CHAOS CONJUNCTION
CHAOS CONJUNCTION
The alignment of the rising triad of red stars reduces the cost of Chaos, Combat, and Special spells by 33%. All single-target combat attack spells are 33% stronger, and research generation from power is doubled.
#NATURE CONJUNCTION
NATURE CONJUNCTION
The alignment of the rising triad of green stars reduces the cost of Nature and Summoning spells by 33%. All Fantastic creatures gain +2 Attack, Defense, and Resistance, and mana generation from power is doubled.
#AETHER FLUX
AETHER FLUX
The fabric of magic overflows, reducing the cost of all spells by 33%, except the Spell of Mastery.
#GOOD MOON
GOOD MOON
The power of light peaks, boosting power from divine cult religious buildings by 50% while reducing power from infernal cult religious buildings by 33%. Life and Unit Enchantment spells cost 33% less to cast, and all regular units gain +1 Attack, Defense, and Movement.
#BAD MOON
BAD MOON
The power of darkness peaks, increasing power from infernal cult religious buildings by 50% and reducing power from divine cult religious buildings by 33%. Death and City Enchantment spells cost 33% less to cast, and all regular units lose 3 Resistance in combat.
#VOLCANIC TOXIC SMOG
VOLCANIC TOXIC SMOG
This region is blanketed in dense, noxious smog caused by ongoing volcanic activity. Any unit without Flying or Mountaineer traits that end its turn in an area affected by this thick smog suffers the following effects at the end of turn:
- 1 Non-Magical Poison Doom damage per figure.
- 10 Non-Magical Fire damage.
#FAIRY MAZE
FAIRY MAZE
The Nature Node is home to an anomalous phenomenon known as the Fairy Maze. Any unit without Flying, or Forester trait, or not Nature realm creature that ends its turn on a woodland tile has a 25% chance to become trapped within the ever-shifting forest. While trapped, the unit has a 25% chance to escape at the beginning of each of its turns.
If the trapped creature gains Forester or Flying traits while inside the Fairy Maze, it will automatically escape from Fairy Maze at the beginning of its next turn, bypassing the random chance mechanic.
#PHANTASMAL TERRAIN
PHANTASMAL TERRAIN
The Sorcery Node harbors an anomalous phenomenon known as Phantasmal Terrain. The land surrounding it is warped by unstable spacetime, constantly shifting between three unpredictable states:
- Flat Grassland – deceptively calm, but ever transient
- Bogging Swamp – slow-moving and perilous for traversal
- Impassable Sorcery Well – a void of arcane energy that blocks all passage
Regardless of its current form, the entire area feels as if it lies deep beneath an abyssal sea—distorted, weightless, and haunted by unseen forces.
#COMBATSPELL
SPELL BUTTON
The Spell button opens your spell book and allows you or your selected unit to cast a spell. You can only cast one spell during each combat turn. Your units can cast additional spells, but casting a spell will end the turn for the casting unit.
#COMBATWAIT
WAIT BUTTON
The Wait button selects the next unit without passing the turn for the currently selected one.
#COMBATDONE
DONE BUTTON
The Done button orders the selected unit to end their turn without further action.
#COMBATINFO
INFO BUTTON
The Info button displays information about global abilities or spell effects affecting the current battle.
#COMBATFLEE
FLEE BUTTON
The Flee button orders all of your units to retreat.
Each unit compares their Movement Speed with the fastest enemy unit.
- If they are at least 2 points slower, they are killed while fleeing.
- If they have equal or slower speed, they have a 50% chance to die.
- If they are faster than the enemy, they have a chance to survive calculated as:
  (1 + speed difference) / (2 + speed difference)
When the Flee button turns green, fleeing is guaranteed to be successful with no units dying.
#COMBATAUTO
AUTO BUTTON
Order your Field Commander to take command of the battle. You can allow them to do so for one turn, or for the duration of the entire combat. In either case, you can take back command by clicking anywhere or pressing the "Esc" or "A" hotkeys.
#COMBATSKILL
COMBAT SKILL
This is the amount of casting capacity you have left for the current battle. It refills between each battle.
#COMBATMANA
MANA
The amount of Mana crystals in the Mana reserves.
#COMBATRANGE
RANGE PENALTY
Range is a multiplier that effects the Mana Cost of a spell. The farther away the combat is from your Fortress, the greater the multiplier.
While Banished, you can still cast spells, but the range penalty to do so is 4.
#NODE AURA
NODE AURA
All units that shared the same realm with the Node's realm receive +2 Melee/Ranged Attack, Armor and Resistance.
#COUNTER OTHER REALMS
COUNTER OTHER REALMS
All spells that are from a different realm than the Node have (base casting cost/60) chance to succeed, otherwise they are countered by the Node.
#CONTINUE
CONTINUE
Loads the latest autosave file on the disk.
#WINLOSE
WIN / LOSE BUTTON
Pressing this button allows you to surrender and proceed to the scoring screen, then return to the main menu.
However, when you are already the dominating force in both worlds, the button will change to a "Win" button, allowing you to win the game if all other players surrender instead.
#MAGICPOWERSETTING
MAGIC POWER
Each node produces 8 times this amount of power, plus this amount of power for each tile under its influence.
#CLIMATE
CLIMATE
Choose the predominant climate:
- Fair: Default setting.
- Frozen: More snowy tundra extending further towards the equator. More icy and snow tiles appear in combat, including sea rife with iceburgs.
- Volcanic: More hills, mountains, and volcanoes. Each mountain tiles have chance 1% per erupt into volcanoes without effect on resource of the tile.
- Dry: More deserts, but fewer rivers and swamps. Each turn, each cities have chance for Drought 1% for each nearby desert, or 9% chance of recovery.
- Wet: More swamps and rivers, but fewer deserts. In combat, more wetland tiles occur along rivers and in forest. Sea combat has chance 20% for Hurricane and 4% for Lightning Storm, and half of the chances on land.
#MINERALS
MINERALS
Choose the minerals richness in the game worlds:
- Poor lands: Fewer mineral veins of generally lower quality. Arcanus lacks Mithril.
- Fair lands: Average amount of various minerals. Arcanus can have Mithril but not Adamantium.
- Rich lands: More mineral veins of generally higher quality. Arcanus can contain Adamantium.
#SET SOUND
SOUND
Enables sound effects
#SET MUSIC
MUSIC
Enables background music
#SET COMBAT ANIMATIONS
COMBAT ANIMATIONS
Enables combat attack and movement animations. When disabled, animations are played at a faster speed. You can toggle this setting with the "Q" button during combat.
#SET MORE RANDOM ITEMS
MORE RANDOM ITEMS
When this option is enabled, each generated item has a 50% chance to be a predefined item if possible, or a 50% chance to be randomly generated. If this option is off, items will always be predefined unless no unused predefined item exists within the appropriate cost range.
#SET REQUEUE ALL
REQUEUE ALL
When this option is enabled, any building destroyed in your cities will automatically be added to the front of the building queue.
#SET REBUILD PROMPT
REBUILD PROMPT
When this option is enabled, the game will always bring you to the city screen at the start of your turn if any building was destroyed in cities.
#SET RANDOM EVENTS
RANDOM EVENTS
When this option is enabled, random events may occur.
#SET SHOW ENEMY MOVES
SHOW ENEMY MOVES
When this option is enabled, the overland map view will focus on enemy and neutral players' movements. Moves by friendly players are never shown this way (Alliance, Wizards' Pact).
#SET SPELL ANIMATIONS
SPELL ANIMATIONS
When this option is disabled, overland spell animations will be hidden.
#SET SORT BY REALM
SORT BY REALM
When this option is enabled, your spellbook will be sorted by spell realm and rarity. When disabled, spells are sorted by their type: Summoning, Special, Combat, Unit Enchantment, City Enchantment, and Global Enchantment.
#SET BACKUP SAVES
BACKUP SAVES
When this option is enabled, each turn creates a numbered save file in addition to the normal autosave, which is replaced after each turn.
#SET SHOW NEUTRAL NODE AURAS
NEUTRAL NODE AURAS
When this option is enabled, nodes not belonging to any wizard display their influence area using the neutral flag color.
#SET ANTI-ALIASING
ANTI-ALIASING
When this option is enabled, the game fonts will use anti-aliasing where applicable. Otherwise, fonts will always be displayed without anti-aliasing.
#SET SHOW ENEMY SPELLS
SHOW ENEMY SPELLS
When this option is enabled, animations for enemy Overland spells that are visible will be displayed. If disabled, these animations will not be shown.
#SET LOCK WINDOW SIZE
LOCK WINDOW SIZE
When this option is enabled, the game window cannot be resized. The game window size is saved in the 'Window.ini' file. Delete the file to restore the default size, or edit the file manually to set the desired window size in pixels.
#SET LEGACY TILESET
LEGACY TILESET
When this option is enabled, the game uses the original Master of Magic tile set for overland tiles.
When this option is disabled, overland tiles use new, procedurally generated art.
Note that the original game lacks art for some River Mouth/Shore configurations. In these cases, the missing part of the river is procedurally generated on top of the original Shore tile of the matching shape.
It's possible to enable the use of original River Mouth tiles where available through modding.ini.
#SET LEGACY SELECTION
LEGACY SELECTION
When this option is enabled, clicking a unit in the overland selection window for the first time unselects all other units and selects only the clicked unit.
When this option is disabled, clicking a unit the first time behaves normally (inverts the selection).
Note that the selection for the entire stack can be inverted using the "SHIFT" hotkey.
#SET REMOVE TREES
REMOVE TREES
When this option is enabled, the combat map will render only one tree per tile, reducing the density of trees displayed.
Pressing "T" during combat enables this feature until the end of the battle.
#SET SHOW GRID
SHOW GRID
When this option is enabled, both the combat and overland maps display a grid. You can toggle this feature by pressing the "R" button.
#SET COMBAT SHADOW
COMBAT SHADOW
When this option is disabled, combat shadows will not be displayed.
#SET MOVE TOGETHER
MOVE TOGETHER
When this option is enabled, units with remaining movement will not be prompted to move if they have already moved during this turn, and their movement ended with at least one unit in their stack running out of moves.
#SET 30 FPS MODE
30 FPS MODE
When this option is enabled, Reduces the frame rate to 30 FPS.
When this option is disabled, the game runs at 60 FPS.
#SET SHOW FOG OF WAR
SHOW FOG OF WAR
When this option is enabled, darkening of tiles outside the vision range of your units and cities.
#SET RANDOM BGM
RANDOM BGM
By default, the background music track played depends on the game state — winning, neutral, and losing.
When this option is enabled, a different track is played each turn.
#SET UNIT COUNTER
UNIT COUNTER
When this option is enabled, displaying the number of units on top of stacks on the Overland map.
#SET INVERT MOUSE BUTTONS
INVERT MOUSE BUTTONS
Swaps the effect of left and right clicks on the mouse globally.
These are the defaults when this option is turned off:
Left Click (Action): Move unit, Activate buttons, etc.
Right Click (Information): Select unit, Scroll map, View unit, Help
For more detailed settings, please use Keys.INI.
#INFO SURVEYOR
SURVEYOR
This advisor displays terrain quality suitable for settling cities, descriptions of terrain tiles, and information on monsters in scouted lairs, nodes, and towers.
#INFO CARTOGRAPHER
CARTOGRAPHER
This advisor displays the known map of both worlds.
#INFO APPRENTICE
APPRENTICE
This advisor allows you to browse your known spells, view available research options, and change the ongoing research to another spell. When you change your active research, any progress made on the previous spell will be saved, allowing you to continue from where you left off once you return to researching it.
#INFO HISTORIAN
HISTORIAN
This advisor displays the overall empire strength, army strength, spell power, power income, and empire population of all known wizards, including your own.
#INFO SPY MASTER
SPY MASTER
This advisor provides a history of relationships between all known wizards.
#INFO CHANCELLOR
CHANCELLOR
This advisor displays the previous monthly report.
#INFO TAX COLLECTOR
TAX COLLECTOR
This advisor allows you to adjust your tax rates.
#INFO GRAND VIZIER
GRAND VIZIER
The Grand Vizier can manage the construction of buildings in your cities.
#INFO MIRROR
MIRROR
You can view your selected books and retorts here.
#INFO GOVERNOR
GOVERNOR
Opens the "Cities" sub-screen, equivalent to clicking on the "Cities" button.
#INFO GEOMANCER
GEOMANCER
This advisor displays special terrain information, including details like the owner of Volcano tiles and the amount of Power generated by each Node. It also shows the combat casting Cost Multiplier based on the distance from your Fortress.
#INFO FAMILIAR
FAMILIAR
Your Familiar can reveal the hidden truth about the world, displaying the initial game settings such as map size and number of opponents you selected at the beginning of the game.
#IT SWORD
SWORDS
Swords are versatile weapons well-suited for both defense and offense, and they conduct magic effectively.
Touch abilities, Attack strength, and To-Hit bonuses enchanted into swords affect Melee attacks only.
This item type has no inherent bonus ability.
#IT MACE
MACES
Maces are versatile weapons that offer better resistance than swords but are less suitable for defense.
Touch abilities, Attack strength, and To-Hit bonuses enchanted into maces affect Melee attacks only.
This item type has no inherent bonus ability.
#IT AXE
AXES
Axes are weapons specialized for offensive strength.
Touch abilities, Attack strength, and To-Hit bonuses enchanted into axes affect Melee attacks only.
Any bonus attack strength enchanted into an Axe will increase the wielder's Thrown attack strength by the same amount.
#IT BOW
BOWS
Ranged weapons that shoot arrows at the target.
Touch abilities, Attack strength, and To-Hit bonuses enchanted into bows affect Ranged attacks only.
This item type has no inherent bonus ability.
#IT WAND
WANDS
Ranged weapons with less offensive and defensive power than staves but higher accuracy.
Touch abilities, Attack strength, and To-Hit bonuses enchanted into wands affect Ranged attacks only.
This item type has no inherent bonus ability.
#IT STAFF
STAVES
Ranged weapons with high offensive and defensive power but poor accuracy.
Touch abilities, Attack strength, and To-Hit bonuses enchanted into staves affect Ranged attacks only.
This item type has no inherent bonus ability.
#IT SHIELD
SHIELDS
Shields offer effective protection from attacks and magic spells.
Equipping a shield grants the Large Shield ability, which adds +3 Defense against ranged attacks.
#IT CHAIN
CHAIN MAILS
Chain mails offer less protection than plate mails but are easier to enchant.
Equipping a Chain Mail grants an additional +1 Defense on top of any Defense enchantment included in the item.
#IT PLATE
PLATE MAILS
Plate mails offer the highest protection from damage possible, but due to their large size and weight, they are very difficult to create.
Plate mails have a very high base cost of enchanting, costing 300 more than other types defensive item.
Equipping a Plate Mail grants an additional +2 Defense on top of any Defense enchantment included in the item.
#IT OTHER
ACCESSORIES
Accessories are versatile magical items that can contain a wide variety of enchantments.
This item type has no inherent bonus ability.
#OPT NO OVERLAP
NO OVERLAP
Score Modifier: 0.70x
All cities have to be built at least 5 tiles apart instead of 4.
#OPT AUTOMATIC COMBAT
AUTOMATIC COMBAT
Score Modifier: 1.00x
All combat results are determined by the same calculation process the AI uses to resolve their battles against other AI players or neutral targets. As the result is calculated using complex formulas, it will be usually accurate but might be slightly different from the outcome when playing the same battle manually.
Enabling this option uses the same calculation process the AI uses to resolve battles against other AI players or neutral targets. The result is determined by complex formulas, typically accurate but potentially different from manual play outcomes. This speeds up large-scale games with many opponents but prevents use of combat spells and unit special abilities.
#OPT AGAINST THE WORLDS
AGAINST THE WORLDS
Score Modifier: 2.00x
All other wizards are in a permanent alliance with each other and at war with you. Diplomacy is disabled.
Note: This setup is mutually exclusive with "Sandbox Mode", "Final War", and disables "No Trading".
#OPT WORLD EQUALIZER
WORLD EQUALIZER
Score Modifier: 1.00x
Players are evenly divided between the two planes, instead of the player's starting plane having more opponents while the other plane has fewer.
Note: This setup is mutually exclusive with "Race to the Unknown", "I Am the Boss", and "Inverted Worlds".
#OPT INVERTED WORLDS
INVERTED WORLDS
Score Modifier: 0.40x
Inverts the number of wizards between the two planes - the player's starting plane will have fewer wizards while the other plane has more.
Note: This setup is mutually exclusive with "Race to the Unknown", "World Equalizer", and "I Am the Boss".
#OPT RACE TO THE UNKNOWN
RACE TO THE UNKNOWN
Score Modifier: 0.80x
All players start on the same plane as you. Towers have halved monster budgets. Plane Shift appears for research as if it were an uncommon spell and has halved casting cost. Opponents will prioritize breaking towers and researching Plane Shift higher than usual.
Note: This setup is mutually exclusive with "World Equalizer", "Inverted Worlds", and "I Am the Boss".
#OPT EASY LAIRS
EASY LAIRS
Score Modifier: 0.90x
Lair monster and treasure budgets are halved, and monsters with a cost of 300 or higher are never included. Available high-quality treasure is also reduced.
#OPT DUMB NEUTRALS
DUMB NEUTRALS
Score Modifier: 0.85x
Neutral armies are not allowed to use stalling strategies.
When "Automatic Combat" is enabled, neutral units lose the benefits of "Flying" and "Invisibility" during battle result calculations.
#OPT MONSTERS GONE WILD
MONSTERS GONE WILD
Score Modifier: 1.35x
The overall strength of all rampaging monster groups is increased by 50%, but the maximum strength of each individual monster in the stack remains unchanged. Additionally, neutral cities will send larger raider armies than usual.
#OPT TARGETING AID
TARGETING AID
Score Modifier: 0.95x
When enabled, during combat, attempting to cast a single target spell on an enemy unit that is unaffected due to immunity or other abilities will display a warning message. The spell will not be cast, allowing the player to reconsider.
If this option is disabled, casting spells on targets immune to them is possible, but they will have no effect.
It's important to note that enemies might still resist a spell if their Armor or Resistance is high enough to block the entire effect, but no warning will be given in such cases.
#OPT STANDARDIZED
STANDARDIZED
Score Modifier: 1.00x
Enemy wizards are restricted to using the default book and retort picks without customization options.
Mandatory on Easy difficulty.
#OPT PLANE OF WATER
PLANE OF WATER
Score Modifier: 1.15x
The land to sea ratio is adjusted to 1:9 instead of the usual 1:5.
This option is mutually exclusive with the "Plane of Earth".
#OPT PLANE OF EARTH
PLANE OF EARTH
Score Modifier: 0.80x
The land to sea ratio is adjusted to 1:3 instead of the usual 1:5.
This option is mutually exclusive with the "Plane of Water".
#OPT LEAVE ME ALONE
LEAVE ME ALONE
Score Modifier: 0.75x
AI wizards will treat land tiles within a 6-tile radius around the human player's settlements as unavailable for building cities.
#OPT SANDBOX MODE
SANDBOX MODE
Score Modifier: 0.50x
AI wizards will never turn hostile towards the human player and will never declare war unless provoked by a warning or attacked by the player.
This option is mutually exclusive with the "Against the Worlds".
#OPT ORDER PLEASE
ORDER PLEASE
Score Modifier: 1.00x
AI wizards cannot have "Chaotic" personality.
#OPT SMART FAMILIAR
SMART FAMILIAR
Score Modifier: 0.95x
When approaching a lair, node, or tower, your familiar will predict battle results for you.
#OPT NO TRADING
NO TRADING
Score Modifier: 1.25x
Neither the AI nor the human player is allowed to trade spells.
#OPT CONTINENTAL LORD
CONTINENTAL LORD
Score Modifier: 0.85x
When this option is enabled, your starting location will be on the largest landmass on your plane.
#OPT TREE MASTERY
BUILDING TREE MASTERY
Score Modifier: 1.00x
When this option is enabled, all players start the game with Tree of Knowledge already researched and casted, allowing the construction of Armorer's Guild, Wizard's Guild, Maritime Guild, Fantastic Stable, Amplifying Tower, and Linking Tower.
#OPT UNDEVELOPED START
UNDEVELOPED START
Score Modifier: 1.00x
All players start the game with halved Casting Skill and power generated from their Fortress city. The Fortress cities have 1000 less population, and players aren't given any Settler units at the beginning.
Enabling this option will delay various in-game features that depend on turn count by 20, such as the appearance of rampaging monsters or the amount of power generated by the Astrologer retort.
#OPT DISCONNECTED
DISCONNECTED
Score Modifier: 0.95x
Reduces the number of Towers of Wizardry that connect the two planes to 40% of the normal amount, with a minimum of 2 towers.
#OPT EVERYTHING NICE
EVERYTHING NICE
Score Modifier: 0.90x
Land and city destruction spells are banned. No player can obtain any of the following spells:
Nature Realm: Earthquake, Planetary Mastery
Chaos Realm: Corruption, Raise Volcano, Chaos Rift, Call the Void, Doomsday, Armageddon, Meteor Storm
Death Realm: Warp Node, Evil Presence, Drought, Pestilence
Please note that even if you selected to start the game with any of these spells, you will not have access to them.
#OPT I AM THE BOSS
I AM THE BOSS
Score Modifier: 0.30x
The player starts alone on their plane, while all other wizards begin on the other plane.
Opponents will prioritize breaking towers and researching Plane Shift more than usual.
This option is mutually exclusive with the "World Equalizer", "Race to the Unknown", and "Inverted Worlds".
#OPT TREASURE IMPACT
TREASURE IMPACT
Score Modifier: 0.75x
High-quality treasure available in lairs, nodes, and towers is drastically increased.
AI players will prioritize hunting for treasure more and will customize their wizards accordingly.
#OPT CORRUPT LEADERS
CORRUPT LEADERS
Score Modifier: 0.94x
Offering tribute to enemy wizards outside of war has the same effect as an ongoing Peace Treaty. The wizard can't perform hostile actions or declare war.
The duration depends on the amount of Gold or Spell rarity, and multiple offers have a cumulative effect.
Please be aware that hostile actions you take against the wizard can decrease the duration of the Peace Treaty effect, similar to a normal Peace Treaty.
This modifier has no effect on opponents you are already at war with.
#OPT MINOR PARANOIA
MINOR PARANOIA
Score Modifier: 1.15x
AI Wizards generated cannot have a Peaceful personality, and there is a -12 modifier in the generic war declaration formula against the human player.
This option is mutually exclusive with the "Major Hostility", and "Against the Worlds".
#OPT MAJOR HOSTILITY
MAJOR HOSTILITY
Score Modifier: 1.30x
AI Wizards generated cannot have a Peaceful or Lawful personality, and there is a -24 modifier in the generic war declaration formula against the human player.
This option is mutually exclusive with the "Minor Paranoia", and "Against the Worlds".
#OPT FINAL WAR
FINAL WAR
Score Modifier: 1.40x
When a domination rate of 75% or higher is reached, all wizards declare war on the human player and ally with each other.
This option is mutually exclusive with the "Against the Worlds".
#OPT BOOK COLLECTORS
BOOK COLLECTORS
Score Modifier: 0.75x
Each time a wizard is banished or defeated, there is a chance that one of their spell books will become the winner's possession. If wizard's fortress is their last city, gaining of a book is guerenteed. The acquired book has all the benefits of a normal spell book but does not contain new researchable spells. The wizard who loses the book does not lose any spells.
#OPT UNSTOPPABLE STAMPEDE
UNSTOPPABLE STAMPEDE
Score Modifier: 1.25x
In combat, all neutral Fantastic creatures gain Regeneration 0.
#OPT ADAMANTIUM FORTRESS
ADAMANTIUM FORTRESS
Score Modifier: 0.60x
The Human player starts the game with an old Adamantium mine located right below their Fortress. Their starting units are equipped with Adamantium equipment left over from the previous owner.
#OPT NODEBORNE SOULS
NODEBORNE SOULS
Score Modifier: 1.25x
Nodes have souls and will be more active in defending themselves in combat. All nodes have combat enchantment attached to them. Nodes also grant Common or Uncommon unit enchantments from the same realm as the node to all defending neutral creatures.
#OPT COSMIC CHESSBOARD
COSMIC CHESSBOARD
Score Modifier: 1.25x
Divine and Infernal gods freely intervene in events on both planes. Any combat involving neutral Life or Death Fantastic creatures will trigger intervention from gods of their side, granting common or uncommon combat enchantments and unit enchantments to support their minions.
#OPT UPHILL BATTLE
UPHILL BATTLE
Score Modifier: 1.50x
Whenever AI units are in combat against the human player, those units gain +10% To-Hit, +10% To-Defend, and +1 Resistance.
#OPT GODS PLAY DICES
GODS PLAY DICES
Score Modifier: 1.50x
Gods gamble with the fate of mortals....
At the start of combat, each unit rolls for resistance penalties:
- 10% for -2
- 20% for -1
- 20% for +1
- 10% for +2
AI's units also roll for resistance penalties, but with only half the chance for each penalty level when facing the human player.
#OPT KHAN THE CONQUEROR
KHAN THE CONQUEROR
Score Modifier: 1.25x
Neutral units will fight as if their commander has the Warlord and Tactician retorts.
#OPT <STARTING SITUATION>
STARTING SITUATION:
Score modifiers below change how the game starts, influencing the types of opponent wizards faced, their starting positions, and the map layout.
#OPT <ACCESSIBILITY OPTIONS>
ACCESSIBILITY OPTIONS:
Score modifiers below determine how much the game engine assists and guides you throughout your journey. These modifiers include options for accessibility to help beginners learn the game or settings that favor the human player. While these generally make the game easier, they can also be used in conjunction with game-changing modifiers on the next page to adjust difficulty and create interesting role-play scenarios.
#OPT <ADVANCED OPTIONS>
ADVANCED OPTIONS:
Score modifiers below significantly alter gameplay, often leading to more challenging settings to play with.
#OPT YOU TOO, ADAMANTIUM?
YOU TOO, ADAMANTIUM?
Score Modifier: 1.25x
Opponent wizards starts the game with an old Adamantium mine located right below their Fortress and free Alchemist's Guild in the city. Their starting units are equipped with Adamantium equipment.

#OPT PLEASANTVILLE

All wizards' empires operate with perfect administrative efficiency, distance-based waste/Corruption and Siege penalties do not apply to city administration.
Settlers' cost is nolonger scale with number of city own by the wizard.
#OPT <FORTRESS OPTIONS>
FORTRESS OPTIONS:
Score modifiers below allows player to customized their starting fortress location as well as some unique buildings that hard to come by.
#OPT FORTRESS ON THE HILL
FORTRESS ON THE HILL
Score Modifier: 0.90x
Your starting fortress location is situate on an elevated beautiful hill, raised yourself for some fresh air in your study!
If original fortress location is actually on the river, hill tile would be raised nearby instead.
This scoring option is mutually exclusive with the "Mountain King", the "Mount Doom", the "Sand Pit", the "Everglade", the "Disney on Ice", and the "Magic Garden".
#OPT MOUNTAIN KING
MOUNTAIN KING
Score Modifier: 0.90x
Your starting fortress location is situate on a great majestic mountain, raised yourself to show how great you are!
If original fortress location is actually on the river, mountain tile would be raised nearby instead.
This scoring option is mutually exclusive with the "Fortress on the Hill", the "Mount Doom", the "Sand Pit", the "Everglade", the "Disney on Ice", and the "Magic Garden".
#OPT MOUNT DOOM
MOUNT DOOM
Score Modifier: 0.90x
Your starting fortress location is situate on an active volcano, raised yourself as stove in the kitchen is not dignify enough for master wizard like you!
If original fortress location is actually on the river, volcano tile would be raised nearby instead.
This scoring option is mutually exclusive with the "Fortress on the Hill", the "Mountain King", the "Sand Pit", the "Everglade", the "Disney on Ice", and the "Magic Garden".
#OPT SAND PIT
SAND PIT
Score Modifier: 0.90x
Your starting fortress location is situate on a personal exclusive desert, properly of your own making as sandbox is not big enough for you!
If original fortress location is actually on the river, desert tile would be raised nearby instead.
This scoring option is mutually exclusive with the "Fortress on the Hill", the "Mountain King", the "Mount Doom", the "Everglade", the "Disney on Ice", and the "Magic Garden".
#OPT EVERGLADE
EVERGLADE
Score Modifier: 0.90x
Your starting fortress location is situate on a mysterious majestic swampland, suit dignity of proper master wizard like you!
If original fortress location is actually on the river, swamp tile would be raised nearby instead.
This scoring option is mutually exclusive with the "Fortress on the Hill", the "Mountain King", the "Mount Doom", the "Sand Pit", the "Disney on Ice", and the "Magic Garden".

#OPT DEMON KING'S CASTLE
DEMON KING'S CASTLE
Score Modifier: 1.25x
All opponent wizards start the game with City Wall, Hillfort, Fortification, Baray, Undercity Hive Network, and Tree of Life in the fortress. Although all of these buildings are destructable, these buildings would be built along with new fortress every time those opponents cast Spell of Return!
The tile beneath the fortress of opponent will convert into volcano unless the tile is a river.
Opponent fortress would receive upkeep refund from these buildings as long as it last.
#OPT ZERO BOOK RULE
ZERO BOOK RULE
