Play by old Warlord mod's rule before version 1.5.10 with each wizard get 1 researchable Common spell of that realm at random if the wizard does not start with any book in that realm.
#OPT MORE THAN RETORT
MORE THAN RETORT
Score Modifier: 1.00x
Each retort accompanies with unique researchable spells and reforms.
#FORTRESS
*Fortress_0.png
 FORTRESS
A wizard's Fortress is their base of operations. If it's lost, the wizard gets banished and must cast the Spell of Return or loses the game.
The fortress conducts raw magical energy, casting a lightning bolt with a strength calculated as (18 + Skill/8) / 2 for the first (3 + Skill/20) turns of combat. Both values are scaled by the Difficulty setting for AI players. The strength of the bolts cannot exceed 60.
The fortress also produces 10 power and an additional 1.5 for each book owned in realms where the wizard has at least 4 books, rounded down.
#B BARRACKS
*Building3_0.png
 BARRACKS
Maintenance: 1 gold/turn
Barracks allow a city to train and organize regular military units. Without barracks, a city cannot train regular military units. All units created in the town gain +1 Level.
#B COLISEUM
*Building4_0.png
 COLISEUM
Maintenance: none
A Coliseum entertains the population, reducing Unrest by 1 and increasing Fame by 5.
#B FIGHTER'S GUILD
*Building5_0.png
 FIGHTER'S GUILD
Maintenance: 4 gold/turn
The Fighter's Guild trains soldiers and unlocks superior unit types. Advancing beyond this tier requires casting the Tree of Knowledge spell.
#B ARMORER'S GUILD
*Building6_0.png
 ARMORER'S GUILD
Maintenance: 4 gold/turn
The Armorer's Guild is the height of military technology, training troops in advanced fighting techniques and basic battle tactics, and enabling the construction of more sophisticated units.
#B WAR COLLEGE
*Building7_0.png
 WAR COLLEGE
Maintenance: 3 gold/turn
A War College serves as a center for teaching battle strategy, tactics, and advanced fighting techniques. All new troops start as Veterans.
#B SMITHY
*Building8_0.png
 SMITHY
Maintenance: None
A Smithy specializes in producing high-quality weaponry and tools, serving as a key building in any town. It generates 3 Production and is essential for producing most military units.
#B STABLES
*Building9_0.png

#B LAVA SMELTER
*Building45_0.png
 LAVA SMELTER
Maintenance: 20 gold/turn
Dwarf race's unique building.
The Lava Smelter extracts rare minerals by smelting lava from deep beneath the cave. It generates 15 Power and +1 level of magic weapon upgrades. The city also gains the Wall of Fire.
Level 1: Magic -> Mithril
Level 2: Mithril -> Adamantium
Level 3: Adamantium -> +Orihalcon
Mineral Effect:
 Mithril + Adamantium -> Weapon Immunity
 Mithril + Crysx -> Missile Immunity
 Mithril + Orihalcon -> Resist Element
 Adamantium + Orihalcon -> Elemental Armor
 Adamantium + Crysx -> Flame Blade
This building must be built in rocky area.

#B HILLFORT
*Building50_0.png
 HILLFORT
Maintenance: 3 gold/turn
A Hillfort is a defensive structure built on an elevated location, offering a strategic advantage.
In Strategic Combat, the city garrison gains +3 Armor and Missile Immunity.
In Tactical Combat, on low elevation overland location, a Hillfort surrounds the city with steep ramp that difficult for units without Mountaineer, or Flying, or Non-Corpereal ability to move across. On high elevation overland location (hill, mountain, or volcano), a Hillfort prevent Corpereal units from move in and out of the city except a few entry points with impassable cliff face. A Hillfort also grants Missile Immunity to friendly units inside the city.

#Spell CRACKS CALL
*CracksCall_9.png
 CRACKS CALL
Nature Uncommon - Instant Combat
Target: combat tile
Casting Cost: 30 mana
Rends the earth, creating a fissure. Any non-Flying, Corporeal creature over the fissure has a 4% chance per Defense stat to become "Buried" for the remainder of the combat. Buried creatures cannot move or attack, suffer -10% To-Defend, take Irrecoverable Damage from all attacks, and are irrecoverably destroyed if their side loses the battle. Any Wall on the tile is also destroyed.
A unit affected by Cracks Call must take four penalty rolls, each with a 25% chance of suffering 4 Irrecoverable Damage from falling into the fissure. If the unit is already Buried, it must take two additional penalty rolls.

For caster units with spells and abilities that have a recharge time of more than four turns during combat, one spell is automatically recharged every four turns.

#UA INVISIBLE
*ux19.png
 INVISIBLE
Invisibility makes the unit impossible to target with ranged attacks. The unit becomes visible when adjacent to an enemy unit, but there is still a 20% chance for each hit to miss the target, as if Blur was in effect. If Blur is also in effect, the cumulative chance becomes 40%.
#UA CREATE UNDEAD
*ux20.png
 CREATE UNDEAD
Create Undead allows the unit to create new Undead of the same type from any units it has eliminated in combat. This can't be used on heroes. If the unit possesses Death Immunity or Magic Immunity, the ability will have no effect. Units that are raised as Undead can't recover their Health point normally, but are killed if you lose the battle and can't retain control of them. Units affected by Black Sleep can't be raised as Undead.
#UA LONG RANGE
*ux126.png
 LONG RANGE

#UA QUICK CASTING
*ux22.png
 QUICK CASTING
When the unit casts a spell, it uses only 2 Movement points instead of all of them.
#UA MELD
 MELD WITH NODE
Meld with Nodes allows spirits to merge with a magical node and begin to channel the power of the node to you. The process of melding destroys the spirit.
When a Guardian Spirit melds a node, the node produces an additional +3 power and all of the owner's units defending the node receive the benefit of a Heavenly Light spell.
#UA NONCORPOREAL
*ux23.png
 NON-CORPOREAL
Non-Corporeal allows the unit to pass through any land square at a cost of 1 Movement point and allows it to move through walls unimpeded. Non-Corporeal units don't turn to Undead from Undead creating damage.
#UA WIND WALKING
*ux24.png
 WIND WALKING
Allows the unit and all units in its stack to fly on the overland map and participate in naval combat. The minimal overland Movement Speed of the unit becomes 3. Carried units can't drop below 0.5 Movement points unless the Windwalker runs out of Movement points.
#UA REGENERATION
*ux25.png
 REGENERATION
Regeneration allows the unit to heal a set number of Health Points per combat turn and be completely healed at the end of a combat. If the unit was destroyed but its side was victorious, the unit will come back to life, completely healed. Units killed by irrecoverable or undead creating damage can't regenerate.
#UA PURIFY
*ux26.png
 PURIFY
Purify allows a unit to clean corruption from a square. Corrupted map square has 3% chance each turn to decay; from forest becomes swamp, hill becomes mountain, and grassland becomes desert. So recommended to purify the land in your territory as soon as possible.
#UA NEGATE FIRST STRIKE
*ux47.png
 NEGATE FIRST STRIKE
Negate First Strike allows the unit to nullify the First Strike ability of attackers. This special ability has no effect on Thrown, Breath, or Gaze attacks.
#UA LUCKY
*ux124.png
 LUCKY
Lucky grants +10% To-Hit, +10% To-Defend, and +1 Resistance.
#UA JINX
*ux164.png
 JINX
The enchanted unit brings bad luck to its allies. All regular units on their side lose 1 Attack, Armor, and Resistance. Multiple instances of Jinx are not cumulative.
#UA POISON IMMUNITY
*ux6.png
 POISON IMMUNITY
Poison Immunity makes the unit immune to all forms of poison attacks.
#UA FIRE IMMUNITY
*ux7.png
 FIRE IMMUNITY
Fire Immunity makes units immune to Fire attacks. (Magical Ranged attacks are not Fire attacks, regardless of the animation.)
#UA STONING IMMUNITY
*ux8.png
 STONING IMMUNITY
Stoning Immunity makes the unit immune to all forms of stoning.
#UA WEAPON IMMUNITY
*ux9.png
 WEAPON IMMUNITY
Weapon Immunity makes the unit nearly impervious to attacks from non-hero regular units that do not have Mithril, Adamantium, Magical, holy, or flaming weapons, increasing the unit's Armor by +10 against those attacks. Weapon Immunity does not protect against Fantastic creatures, heroes, and spells.
#UA MISSILE IMMUNITY
*ux10.png
 MISSILE IMMUNITY
Missile Immunity makes the unit immune to small physical projectile (sling, arrow, and small bullet) ranged attacks. Missile Immunity does not protect unit from Touch type effects that coming along with ranged attack such as Poison, Stoning Touch, Death Touch, or Life Steal abilities. Doom and Illusion type damage ignore or circumvent Missile Immunity entirely.
#UA ILLUSION IMMUNITY
*ux11.png
 ILLUSION IMMUNITY
Illusion Immunity negates the illusionary bonus of illusionary attacks and prevents Confusion, Vertigo, and Mind Storm. In addition, invisible units are revealed, and this unit can use ranged attacks to attack them, as well as use ranged attacks through Wall of Darkness.
#UA COLD IMMUNITY
*ux12.png
COLD IMMUNITY
 Cold Immunity makes the unit impervious to cold spells.
#UA MAGIC IMMUNITY
*ux13.png
 MAGIC IMMUNITY
Magic Immunity makes a unit immune to all forms of magic, including ranged magical attacks and all spell effects, regardless of realm.
Although Magic Immunity prevents the unit from effect of Illuion or Doom type direct attack spells, it does not protect the unit from Doom or Illusion type damage from Magical Ranged Attacks from other units. It also does not prevent damage from Poison attack attached to Magical Ranged Attacks.
#UA DEATH IMMUNITY
*ux48.png
 DEATH IMMUNITY
Death Immunity makes the unit immune to most spells in the Death realm.
#UA SUMMONDEMON
*ux136.png
 SUMMON DEMON
Summons Lesser Demons in battle. Unlike the Summon Demon spell, these demons do not have the ability to cast spells.
#UA IMMOLATION
*ux33.png
 IMMOLATION
This unit is surrounded by a burning, fiery aura that prevent unit from being Frozen, and inflicts a strength 10 Magic Fire attack on all enemies engaged in Melee combat with the target unit. This Magic attack is in addition to the unit's normal attacks. Immolation also burns away Webs on the unit at a faster than normal rate.
#UA FEAR
*ux129.png
 FEAR
Each individual enemy figure engaging this unit in melee must resist at -3 or stand frozen in terror, unable to attack, even if swung upon. Note: Thrown, Breath, and Gaze attacks are not Melee attacks.
#UA RESISTANCE TO ALL
*ux34.png
 RESISTANCE TO ALL
Resistance to All increases the Resistance of all friendly units on the same overland tile by the listed bonus level. The bonus is not cumulative with other units that have the same ability - the highest bonus will be used only.
#UA HOLY BONUS
*ux35.png
 HOLY BONUS
Holy Bonus increases the Melee and Ranged Attack strength, Armor, and Resistance of all friendly units on the same overland tile by the bonus level of the Holy Bonus. The bonus is not cumulative, if multiple units have this ability, only the highest will apply.
#UA ARMOR PIERCING
*ux29.png
ARMOR PIERCING
Armor Piercing allows attacks from this unit to ignore half of the defending unit's armor. If this ability is granted by a weapon, it only applies to attacks performed by that type of weapon.
#UA FIRST STRIKE
*ux30.png
 FIRST STRIKE
First Strike allows the unit to deal its damage before hand-to-hand attacks, but after Breath, Thrown, and Gaze attacks when the unit is attacking.
#UA POISON
*ux31.png
 POISON
Poison attacks force the attacked unit to resist for each level of the poison or suffer one hit for each failure. These resistance rolls always have a -1 save modifier.
#UA LIFE STEAL
*ux32.png
 LIFE STEAL
Life-stealing attacks force the attack target to make a resistance roll for each attacking figure. For each point the Resistance is failed, the defending unit loses one hit, while the attacker gains one. Units killed mainly by Life-Steal return as Undead under the control of their destroyer. If this ability is granted by a weapon, it only applies to attacks performed by that type of weapon.
#UA DOOM
*ux137.png
 DOOM
The unit always deals exactly 1 damage for each 2 Attack strength, ignoring all defensive effects or To-Hit chances. If this ability is granted by a weapon, it only applies to attacks performed by that type of weapon.
#UA DESTRUCTION
*ux113.png
 DESTRUCTION
The ability causes attacked units to make a resistance roll or be disintegrated. It affects the entire unit. If this ability is granted by a weapon, it only applies to attacks performed by that type of weapon.
#UA ILLUSION
*ux36.png
 ILLUSION
Illusionary attack allows the attacking unit to ignore the defender's armor entirely. If this ability is granted by a weapon, it only applies to attacks performed by that type of weapon.
#UA STONING TOUCH
*ux28.png
 STONING TOUCH
Stoning touch makes the attacked figure resist or be turned to stone for each attacking figure. This ability does not apply to Magic Ranged attacks. If this ability is granted by a weapon, it only applies to attacks performed by that type of weapon.
#UA DEATH TOUCH
*ux138.png
 DEATH TOUCH
Death touch makes the attacked figure resist or be killed instantly for each attacking figure. This ability does not apply to Magic Ranged attacks. If this ability is granted by a weapon, it only applies to attacks performed by that type of weapon.
#UA EXORCISE
*ux130.png
 EXORCISE
Exorcise makes the attacked Fantastic unit figure resist or be banished from existence for each attacking figure. If this ability is granted by a weapon, it only applies to attacks performed by that type of weapon.
#UA CHAOS ARMOR
*ux59.png
 CHAOS CHANNEL
The unit is transformed into a Fantastic Chaos creature with dragon skin, gaining +3 armor.
This effect can't be dispelled.
#UA CHAOS FLIGHT
*ux60.png
 CHAOS CHANNEL
The unit is transformed into a Fantastic Chaos creature with dragon wings, gaining flight and a minimal Movement Speed of 2.
This effect can't be dispelled.
#UA CHAOS BREATH
*ux61.png
 CHAOS CHANNEL
The unit is transformed into a Fantastic Chaos creature with the ability to breathe fire at strength 4.
This effect can't be dispelled.
#UA FULL CHAOS CHANNEL
*ux285.png
 FULL CHAOS CHANNEL
The unit is transformed into a Fantastic Chaos creature with dragon skin, dragon wings, and the ability to breathe fire at strength 4.
This effect can't be dispelled.
#UA CHAOS CHANNEL
*ux196.png
 CHAOS CHANNEL
The unit is transformed into a Fantastic Chaos creature with either dragon skin, or dragon wings, or the ability to breathe fire at strength 4.
This effect can't be dispelled.
#UA THROWN
*ux127.png
 THROWN
Thrown weapons allow an attacking unit to hurl its thrown weapons before engaging in hand-to-hand combat. The Thrown attack is executed before melee attacks and only for the attacker.
#UA FIRE BREATH
*ux135.png
 FIRE BREATH
Fire breath allows an attacking unit to breathe a fiery blast before engaging in hand-to-hand combat. The Breath attack is executed before melee attacks and only for the attacker.
#UA LIGHTNING BREATH
*ux134.png
 LIGHTNING BREATH
Lightning breath allows an attacking unit to breathe an Armor Piercing blast of lightning before entering hand-to-hand combat. The Breath attack is executed before melee attacks and only for the attacker.
#UA STONING GAZE
*ux27.png
 STONING GAZE
Stoning gaze makes all enemy figures resist or be stoned before engaging in hand-to-hand combat.
#UA DOOM GAZE
*ux131.png
 DOOM GAZE
Doom gaze makes the enemy automatically take damage with no attack or defense rolls before melee, thrown, or breath attacks.
#UA DEATH GAZE
*ux132.png
 DEATH GAZE
Death gaze makes all enemy units resist or die instantly. The gaze takes effect before actual melee is entered. Death gaze could not inflict upon unit with Death Immunity.
#UA GUARDIAN WIND
*ux115.png
 GUARDIAN WIND
Unit enchantment that grants Missile Immunity to the unit.
Missile Immunity makes the unit immune to small physical projectile (sling, arrow, and small bullet) ranged attacks. Missile Immunity does not protect unit from Touch type effects that coming along with ranged attack such as Poison, Stoning Touch, Death Touch, or Life Steal abilities. Doom and Illusion type damage ignore or circumvent Missile Immunity entirely.
#UA BLOOD LUST
*ux125.png
 BLOODLUST
Enchanted unit deals double melee attack power against regular units and heroes. If the spell is cast in combat, the enchanted unit cannot be healed or cast spells until the end of combat.
#UA ANIMATED
*ux64.png
 ANIMATED
The creature is now a vile Undead being with +1 Melee, Ranged, Thrown, Breath Attacks, Armor, +10% To-Hit, and Weapon Immunity. The unit also gains all abilities related to being Undead: they can't heal, are Fantastic, belong to the Death Realm, and possess Illusion Immunity, Death Immunity, and Cold Immunity.
#UA WRAITH FORM
*ux65.png
 WRAITH FORM
The unit has Weapon Immunity and a non-corporeal form. In addition, the unit has the ability to hit units with Weapon Immunity as though it was a Fantastic creature.
#UA PERMA WRAITH FORM
*ux23.png
 WRAITH FORM
The unit has Weapon Immunity and a non-corporeal form. In addition, the unit has the ability to hit units with Weapon Immunity as though it was a Fantastic creature.
#UA SREGENERATION

 REGENERATION
Enchanted unit gains Regeneration 2.
#UA LAND LINKING
*ux67.png
 NATURE LINK
The target unit gains +1 Resistance and endows the target unit (and any units currently stacked with that unit) with the ability to travel over all land terrain at 1 Movement point per tile.
If the unit is Fantastic, it also gains +2 Armor, Melee, and Breath attacks.
#UA WATER WALKING
*ux68.png
 WATER WALKING
Endows the unit with the ability to walk on water, rivers, swamps, and tundra at a speed of 1 Movement point per tile.
#UA ELEMENTAL ARMOR

Improves a unit's Armor against all Spells, Magical Ranged Attacks, and Breath Attacks by 12.
#UA RESIST ELEMENTS

Instills in the target unit increased Resistance (+4) to the elemental magic of Nature and grants improved Armor (+4) against all Spells, Magical Ranged Attacks, and Breath Attacks.
#UA FOCUS MAGIC
*ux71.png
 FOCUS MAGIC
Improves the unit's ability to wield magic:
- +3 strength to Magical Ranged/Doom Gaze/Breath Attack
- Physical Ranged Attack converts to Magical at the same strength or 3
- Thrown Attack converts to Magical Ranged Attack or gains 3 Magical Ranged Attack with 4 Ammo if no Ranged Attack
- +15 MP to spellcasting capacity
- +1 to maximum spell charge
#UA IRON SKIN
*ux72.png
 IRON SKIN
Fuses iron with the unit's skin, making it able to withstand most attacks (+5 Armor).
#UA ENDURANCE
*ux73.png
 ENDURANCE
Increases the target unit's Movement Speed by one and their Health Points by 4, divided evenly between each figure, but at least 1 per figure.
#UA SPELL LOCK
*ux116.png
 SPELL LOCK
As long as the Spell Lock is in effect, no friendly enchantment on the unit may be dispelled. If the unit is Fantastic, it can't be banished from existence by spells and effects such as Exorcise, or Banish. The Spell Lock resists being dispelled as if it had a strength of 150.
#UA FLIGHT
*ux77.png
 FLIGHT
Bestows the power of flight upon the unit and increases its Movement Speed to a minimum of 3.
#UA RESIST MAGIC
*ux146.png
 RESIST MAGIC
Endows the unit with a tremendously improved Resistance (+5 crosses) against all magical effects.
#UA FLAME BLADE
*ux80.png
 FLAME BLADE
Adds +3 Melee Attack strength, +2 Missile-type Ranged and Thrown Attacks, and fire breath +1. Flaming weapons can hit creatures with Weapon Immunity.
The bonus, except for Fire Breath, is not cumulative with Fiery Fury.
#UA MYSTIC SURGE
*ux81.png
 MYSTIC SURGE
This unit gains +3 Movement, and +2 Armor bonuses, but also suffers -2 Resistance, and -10% To-Defend penalties.
This enchantment can't be dispelled but fade away on its own along with most of remaining Health point (only 1 Health Point left) at the end of combat.
#UA TRUE SIGHT
*ux82.png
 TRUE SIGHT
The unit does not suffer from the ignores-armor effect of illusionary attacks, always succeeds resistance rolls for Sorcery spells, and can see invisible units and through Walls of Darkness.
#UA HOLY WEAPON
*ux83.png
 HOLY WEAPON
Blesses the unit's weapons, allowing them to hit creatures which possess Weapon Immunity and giving a +10% To-Hit bonus in combat.
#UA HEROISM
*ux84.png
 HEROISM
The entire unit becomes elite. This spell will automatically be dispelled when the unit becomes elite naturally.
#UA BLESS
*ux85.png
 BLESS
Adds 4 to the enchanted unit's Resistance against all Chaos and Death realm Spells, Death Gaze, Death Touch, Cause Fear, and Life-Steal. 
Adds 7 to the enchanted unit's Armor against all attacks with Fire or Lightning damage types and any damage-dealing spells from Chaos and Death realms.
#UA LIONHEART
*ux86.png
 LIONHEART
Adds +3 to the unit's Melee and Missile Attack strength, and Resistance. Adds +8 Health Points to the unit, divided evenly between figures. For example, a 4-figure unit will gain 2 Health Points per figure, but a hero would gain a full 8 Health Points.
#UA ORIHALCON
*ux161.png
 ORIHALCON
The unit wears armor decorated with Orihalcon crystals, which makes them more resistant to spells (+1 Resistance). Furthermore, if the unit can use Magical Ranged Attacks, the orihalcon amplifies the strength of those attacks by +2.
#UA SANCTIFY
*ux88.png
 SANCTIFIED
This unit produces 3 Power and requires no Gold to maintain. In combat, the enchanted unit becomes a Life creature (but not a Fantastic creature unless it was already a Fantastic creature) as long as this enchantment is still in effect on the unit.
If the unit is a Cleric, it gains 2 Casting Skills for each of its own base Resistance points, becomes a Fantastic creature, and can cast all Life realm spells.
#UA HOLY ARMOR
*ux89.png
HOLY ARMOR
The enchanted unit has a +10% higher chance To-Defend. However, units that have 5 or lower Armor receive +2 Armor instead.
#UA INVULNERABILITY

 INVULNERABILITY
The unit gains Weapon Immunity, and the first two hits sustained by the unit from any attack are ignored.
#UA VERTIGO
*ux98.png
 VERTIGO
This unit has suffered a -25% To-Hit and a -7% To-Defend.
(Please note that neither chance can drop below 10%.)
#UA CONFUSION
*ux108.png
 CONFUSION
At the beginning of each turn, the effects of this spell will be determined randomly from this list:
1) unit stands confused
2) unit moves randomly
3) unit is controlled by opponent
4) no effect.
When the combat ends, the unit, if still alive, will desert the owner's army and can't regenerate.
#UA MIND STORM
*ux110.png
 MIND STORM
The affected  unit suffers -5 of its Ranged Attacks, Thrown, Armor, and Resistance as well as -3 Melee Attack strength.
#UA SHATTER

 SHATTER
All Attack strengths are reduced to 1.
#UA WEAKNESS
*ux93.png
 WEAKNESS
Saps the strength out of a target unit's creatures, who suffer a penalty of 3 to their Melee, Thrown, and Ranged Attack strengths.
#UA BLACK SLEEP
*ux111.png
 BLACK SLEEP
The affected unit sleeps through the remainder of combat, providing a defenseless target for enemies. If attacked by an enemy unit while in this condition, a sleeping unit takes the full force of the attack in damage but can't be raised as an Undead.
#UA WARP WEAPON

 WARP CREATURE
Reduces the Attack strength of the unit by half for all attack types.

 WARP CREATURE

#UA WARP CREATURE
*ux289.png
 WARP CREATURE
As the unit was affected by Chaos Rift, it has 10% chance to suffer from one of these effects.
- Reduces the Attack strength of the unit by half for all attack types.
- Reduces the Armor strength of the unit to one third.
- Reduces the magical Resistance of the unit to zero.
#UA HASTE
*ux74.png
 HASTE
Doubles the unit's Movement and number of attacks in combat.
#UA WEB

 WEB
Web entangles an enemy unit in a web which traps the unit where it stands until it destroys the web and prevents flight even afterward.
#UA CREATURE BINDING
*ux97.png
 CREATURE BINDING
The affected Fantastic creature is bound to fight for the casting wizard until the end of combat. The bound creature disappears after combat ends.
This effect can't be dispelled!
#UA POSSESSION
*ux95.png
 POSSESSION
The possessed unit fights for the casting wizard until combat ends, then deserts and disappears permanently. Fantastic creatures and heroes may not be possessed.
This effect can't be dispelled!
#UA LEADERSHIP
*ux43.png
 LEADERSHIP
Leadership increases the Melee Attack strength of all regular units on the same map tile by one per 3 levels of the hero, and the Missile Ranged Attack by one per 6 levels. Super leadership (*) increases this bonus by 50%.
#UA LEGENDARY
*ux44.png
 LEGENDARY
Legendary represents the hero's reputation and increases the frequency and strength of mercenaries approaching the wizard for hire, as well as decreases the initial hiring cost. The hero adds +5 fame per level of the hero directly to the controlling wizard's fame total. Super legendary (*) increases this bonus by 50%.
#UA BLADEMASTER
*ux46.png
 BLADEMASTER
Blademaster increases the hero's chance To-Hit by 3.33% per level of experience. Super Blademaster (*) increases this bonus by 50%.
#UA ARMSMASTER
*ux45.png
 ARMSMASTER
Armsmaster adds +2 experience to all regular units stacked with the hero at the end of each turn, per level of experience. Super Armsmaster (*) increases this bonus by 50%.
Multiple sources of Armsmaster are not cumulative and heroes can gain at most 2 experience this way each turn.
#UA CONSTITUTION
*ux49.png
 CONSTITUTION
Constitution increases the hero's Health beyond human norms, adding +1/level to the hero's Health point. Super constitution (*) increases this bonus by 50%.
#UA MIGHT
*ux50.png
 MIGHT
Might increases the hero's Melee Attack by +1 per level of experience. Super might (*) increases this bonus by 50%.
#UA ARCANE POWER
*ux51.png
ARCANE POWER

#UA POWERSHOT

 POWERSHOT

#UA SAGE

 SAGE

#UA PRAYERMASTER

#UA CHARMED

#UA UNITLEVEL
 LEVELS FOR REGULAR UNITS
- Level 1 (0 ep) Recruit:
- Level 2 (30 ep) Regular:
  +1 Melee/Ranged, +1 Resistance
  +1 Casting Skill
- Level 3 (80 ep) Veteran:
  +1 Melee/Ranged, +1 Armor
  +1 Casting Skill, +1 Special Attack
- Level 4 (180 ep) Elite:
  +1 Armor, +1 Resistance, +1 Health
  +1 Casting Skill
----(Below required Warlord/Crusade)----
- Level 5 Ultra Elite:
  +1 Melee/Ranged, +1 Armor, +5% To-Hit
  +1 Casting Skill, +1 Special Attack
- Level 6 Champion:
  +1 Melee/Ranged, +2 Armor, +5% To-Hit
  +1 Casting Skill
#UA HEROLEVEL
 LEVELS FOR HEROES
- Level 1 (0 ep) Hero:
- Level 2 (30 ep) Myrmidon:
  +1 Melee/Ranged, +1 Resistance, +1 Health
- Level 3 (80 ep) Captain:
  +1 Melee, +1 Armor, +1 Health, +5% To-Hit
- Level 4 (180 ep) Commander:
  +1 Melee/Ranged, +1 Resistance, +1 Health
- Level 5 (300 ep) Champion:
  +1 Melee, +1 Health, +5% To-Hit
- Level 6 (550 ep) Lord:
  +1 Melee/Ranged, +1 Resistance, +1 Health
- Level 7 (900 ep) Grand Lord:
  +1 Melee, +1 Armor, +1 Health, +5% To-Hit
- Level 8 (1400 ep) Super Hero:
  +1 Melee/Ranged, +1 Resistance, +1 Health
- Level 9 (2000 ep) Demigod:
  +1 Melee, +1 Health, +5% To-Hit
#UA AMMO
*ux133.png
 AMMO
The amount of times remaining the unit can launch a Ranged attack this battle. Ammo is refilled after each battle.
#UA ROAD BUILDING
*ux37.png
 ROAD BUILDING
Construction allows units to build roads.
#UA SCOUTING
*ux38.png
 SCOUTING
Scouting increases the range a unit can see on the overland map to the scouting level.
#UA MERGING
*ux147.png
 MERGING
The unit has the ability to merge with the earth, pass through it, and reform itself at its destination, moving to any tile in combat for 1 Movement point. The unit is unaffected by Cracks Call.
#UA TELEPORTING
*ux1.png
 TELEPORTING
Teleporting allows a unit to move anywhere on the combat map for a cost of 1 Movement point.
#UA PATHFINDING
*ux21.png
 PATHFINDING
Pathfinding allows the unit and all units stacked with it to move across any land square at the cost of 1 Movement point, and allows the unit to move on any land square in combat for 1 Movement point as well.
In combat, the unit gains a terrain bonus of +5% To-Hit and +1 Armor if it fights and stays on rocky or forest terrain.
#UA MOUNTAINEER
*ux3.png
 MOUNTAINEER
Mountaineer allows all units stacked to cross mountains and hills at a cost of one Movement point per square.
In combat, the unit gains a terrain bonus of +5% To-Hit and +1 Armor if it fights and stays on rocky terrain and can move through rocky terrain at a cost of 1 Movement point.
#UA FORESTER
*ux2.png
 FORESTER
Forester allows all units stacked to pass through forest tiles at a cost of one Movement point per square.
In combat, the unit gains a terrain bonus of +5% To-Hit and +1 Armor if it fights and stays on forest terrain and can move through forest terrain at a cost of 1 Movement point.
#UA SUMMONDEMON
*ux136.png
 SUMMON LESSER DEMON
This unit can summon lesser demons in battle, as if it were casting the Summon Demon spell. However, the lesser demons will not have the ability to cast spells.
#UA UNDEAD
*ux117.png
 UNDEAD
An undead unit has returned from dead by certain Death spells or powers. The resulting unit is now considered a Fantastic unit of the Death realm with Cold Immunity, Death Immunity, and Illusion Immunity. Undead creatures can't heal normally and no longer gain experience.
The Undead also loses ability to cast Healing spell on their own, charges of Healing spell are converted into charges of Revenant spell.
#UA STASIS OVERLAND
*ux90.png
 STASIS (OVERLAND)
This unit skips the next overland turn. As long as it fails to resist at -5, the effect carries over to the next month.
#UA STASIS COMBAT
*ux90.png
 STASIS (COMBAT)
This unit can't act. (It can still counterattack when attacked.)
#UA CASTER
*ux52.png
 CASTER
Caster allows the unit to cast spells like a wizard in combat, without using mana points from the wizard's mana reserve. Furthermore, any hero with the Caster ability ending the turn in the wizard's fortress will contribute 1/5 of their casting ability to progress the wizard's overland spell.
 
Spells cast by units are not affected by effects which modify casting costs for wizards, such as retorts or conjunctions.
#UA NECROMANCY
*ux158.png
 NECROMANCY
After battle, raise fallen friendly units as Undead. Up to a total cost of 140 per hero level will be raised.
#UA ITEM SLOT
 ITEM SLOT
An empty slot that can be used to equip an item to this hero.
- A Sword slot allows equipping a sword, mace, or axe.
- A Bow slot allows equipping a bow, sword, mace, or axe.
- A Staff slot allows equipping a staff or wand.
- A Sword/Staff slot allows equipping any weapon except bows.
- A Shield slot allows equipping a Shield, Chain Mail, or Plate Mail.
- A Ring slot allows equipping any accessory: Gloves, Orbs, Helmets, Amulets, etc.
#UA AGILITY
*ux140.png
 AGILITY
Increases the Armor of the unit by +1 per level of experience. Super Agility (*) increases this bonus by 50%.
#UA CAPACITY
*ux139.png
 CAPACITY
This unit gets an additional Ammo for every 2 experience levels. Super Capacity (*) increases this bonus by 50%.
#UA AETHER MASTER
*ux63.png
 AETHER MASTER
The hero warps the fabric of AEther to be less resistant to the controlling wizard's spellcasting attempts. Produces 8 SP per experience level each turn. Super AEther Master (*) increases this bonus by 50%.
#UA GUIDING BEACON
*ux87.png
 GUIDING BEACON
The hero supports the Ranged Attacks of friendly units on the same map tile, increasing the Ranged Attack strength of units by 1 per 3 levels of experience. Super Guiding Beacon (*) increases this effect by 50%.
#UA SOUL LINKER
*ux141.png
 SOUL LINKER
The hero has an extraordinary talent for commanding Fantastic creatures, boosting their To-Hit and To-Defend chances by 2.5% for each experience level. Super Soul Linker (*) increases this effect by 50%.
#UA RITUAL MASTER
*ux52.png
 RITUAL MASTER
The hero regularly performs rituals for their master, generating raw Magical Power equal to her experience level times 6 every turn. Super Ritual Master (*) increases this effect by 50%.
#UA BATTLEMAGE
*ux109.png
 BATTLEMAGE
The hero is able to tap the forces of physical combat and convert some of the energy into magic. The hero gains MP equal to the experience level every time they perform a Melee Attack or counterattack. The MP gained this way can't exceed the maximum MP capacity of the hero. Super Battlemage (*) increases this effect by 50%.
#UA SUPPLY COMMANDER
*ux112.png
 SUPPLY COMMANDER
The hero organizes and maintains a military-grade supply network, boosting the total Ammo of all troops in combat by 2 where they are present. Multiple instances of this ability are not cumulative, but the bonus is added on top of any bonus received from Capacity.
#UA DIVINE BARRIER
*ux14.png
 DIVINE BARRIER
The hero casts and maintains a protective force field that softens enemy blows hitting friendly soldiers. All friendly units gain +1 Armor per 3 experience levels. Super Divine Barrier (*) increases this bonus by 50%.
#UA LOGISTICS
*ux118.png
 LOGISTICS
The hero has an above-average understanding of battlefield terrain and effective ways of moving across them. Each friendly unit in combat gains an additional +0.5 Movement per two experience levels. Super Logistics (*) increases this bonus by 50%.
#UA PRIMAL FORCE
*ux157.png
 PRIMAL FORCE
This unit is under influence and guidance of force and will that beyond mortal comprehension. The unit produces 12 power each turn for the controlling wizard! The army with this unit could not suffer sneaked attack by mundane tricks from any tactician.
#UA PRIMAL LORD
*ux157.png
 PRIMAL LORD
This unit serves the will of one of aspect of the power that be directly. The unit produces 24 power each turn for the controlling wizard! The army with this unit could not suffer sneaked attack by mundane tricks from any tactician.
#UA SUPERNATURAL
*ux142.png
 SUPERNATURAL
Attacks from figures of this unit surpass the laws of physics. Any attack dealing 7 or more damage before damage reduction effects will deal a minimum of (base damage-5)/2 damage, even if it would be reduced below that amount by armor or spell effects. This creature can't be raised as Undead by wizards who have below 200 base casting skill, not counting any contributed by city buildings.
#UA TRANSPORT
*ux155.png
 TRANSPORT
All non-transport units stacked with this unit move without consuming Movement points and can move even if they don't have any.
A unit can't be transported by a new transport during the same turn it was already transported by another.
#UA HEADS
*ux156.png
 MULTI-COMPARTMENTS
This unit has multiple compartments. Each compartment acts as if they were separate figures.
#UA PANDORA
*ux159.png
 PANDORA'S BOX
At the start of each player's combat turn, this unit has a 50% chance to summon a random Fantastic creature. The available budget depends on the hero level and refills after each battle.
#UA WALL BONUS
*ux160.png
 WALL BONUS
This unit is currently protected by a city wall, receiving an additional +3 Armor when attacked by any units from outside the wall.
#UA HOVERING
 HOVERING
Remains of a dispelled global enchantment, this unit can hover over the water surface until it enters a land tile.
#UA DESTINY
*ux165.png
 DIVINE
This unit has been blessed by the heavens and reborn as a divine being.
It is transformed into a Supernatural Life creature permanently, with doubled base Melee and Ranged attack strength, Health Points, +4 Armor, and Resistance. If the unit is Undead, it loses the "no healing" status and can be healed again like normal.
This effect can't be dispelled.
#UA HEALING AURA
*ux166.png
 HEALING AURA
This unit heals up to 10 damage on friendly (base type) regular units at the end of each combat turn. The healed damage is selected randomly between all possible targets.
#UA BLOODSUCKER
*ux167.png
 BLOODSUCKER
Whenever this unit successfully deals damage to an enemy, it deals an additional 3 damage and recovers 3 Health Points.
#UA DISCIPLINE COMBAT
*ux169.png
 DISCIPLINE
The enchanted unit gains bonus based on level of experience:
- Level 1, Recruit/Hero:
  +1 Armor
- Level 2, Regular/Myrmidon:
  +2 Armor
- Level 3, Veteran/Captain:
  +1 Melee/Physical Ranged, +2 Armor
- Level 4, Elite/Commander or higher:
  +1 Melee/Physical Ranged, +2 Armor
  gains Negate First Strike
#UA DISCIPLINE OL
*ux169.png
 DISCIPLINE
The enchanted unit gains bonus based on level of experience:
- Level 1, Recruit/Hero:
  +1 Armor
- Level 2, Regular/Myrmidon:
  +2 Armor
- Level 3, Veteran/Captain:
  +1 Melee/Physical Ranged, +2 Armor
- Level 4, Elite/Commander or higher:
  +1 Melee/Physical Ranged, +2 Armor
  +1 Movement Rate
#UA BURIED
*ux171.png
 BURIED
This unit fell into a crack and can't attack or move and suffers -10% To-Defend but can still counterattack.
At the end of combat, if their side wins the battle, the effect disappears; otherwise, the unit will be destroyed.
#UA STEALTH
*ux19.png
 STEALTH
- This unit does not trigger Wizard's Pact violations.
- This unit can accurately scout the contents of Lairs, Nodes, or other encounter zones, including the type and exact quantity of all defenders.
- This unit is not shown on the overland map, as if it were invisible. (Note: this does not affect the AI.)
#UA AMPLIFIER
*ux52.png
 AMPLIFIER
All friendly spells deal or heal 1 more damage if they successfully deal any damage. Multiple copies of Amplifier are not cumulative. The spell doesn't need to be cast by the unit with this ability, but the unit has to be present in the battle where the spell takes effect.
#UA LIGHTNING RESISTANCE
*ux163.png
 LIGHTNING RESISTANCE
Lightning attacks lose the Armor Piercing property when affecting this unit.
#UA EGOISM
*ux173.png
 EGOISM
The unit is extremely aware of its own importance and will maximize its effort in improving itself. Doubles EXP gained from all sources.
#UA DARK FORCE
*ux172.png
 DARK FORCE
The forces of darkness empower the unit at the beginning of each combat, restoring its Health to the maximum amount and granting a +10% To-Hit and +10% To-Defend. The evil force stains the body of the wielder, dealing one point of irrecoverable damage to the unit at the beginning of their combat turn.
#UA HEALING IMMUNITY
*ux174.png
 HEALING IMMUNITY
This unit can't heal naturally or by Life magic spells.
If the unit was recently affected by Raise Dead, or Bloodlust, Healing Immunity will disappear at the end of combat.
#UA NO HEALING
*ux174.png
 NO HEALING
Zombies, Skeletons, and Undead units can't heal naturally and can't be healed by Life magic spells.
#UA SHARPSHOOTING
*ux126.png
 SHARPSHOOTING
Hero units are not affected by range penalties when using Ranged Attacks.
#UA GODS PLAY DICES
 GODS PLAY DICES
Gods play dice by betting on the fate of mortals and cheating it too.
At the beginning of combat, each unit rolls for resistance penalties (4% for -3, 8% for -2, 16% for -1, 16% for +1, and 8% for +2).
Non-human players' units also roll for resistance penalties but only at half chance for each penalty level against the human player.
#UA FROZEN
*ux176.png
 FROZEN
This unit is frozen solid and can't act for a turn.
Units with Cold Immunity, Immolation or Non-Corporeal cannot be frozen.
#UA COUNTER IMMUNITY
*ux177.png
 COUNTER IMMUNITY
Spells cast from spell charge on this unit can't be countered.
#UA Hunter

 HUNTER
Game hunting tradition from the city where this unit was trained imprinted skills for living in the wild and fighting at range. Unit permanently gains +1 Ranged Attack and Forester.
#UA Giant Strength
*ux178.png
 GIANT STRENGTH
Coal mining tradition from the city where this unit was trained instilled the value of strength and bodybuilding. Unit permanently gains +1 Melee Attack.
#UA Tough Skin
*ux179.png
 TOUGH SKIN
Tradition of working and beating iron from the city where this unit was trained developed techniques to toughen their skin and make them less vulnerable to weapons. Unit permanently gains +1 Armor.
#UA Natural Resistance
*ux180.png
 NATURAL RESISTANCE
Traditional use of nightshade from the city where this unit was trained improved resistance to magic and poison. Unit permanently gains +1 Resistance.
#UA Immunized Magic
*ux181.png
 IMMUNIZED MAGIC
Long-term exposure to magical ore among the population in the city where this unit was trained developed some degree of resistance to magical effects. Unit permanently gains +1 Resistance for each 10 Powers generated in the city from ore.
#UA Guiled
*ux182.png
 GUILED
Long-term protection of their own wealth from undesirable people imprinted sly and cunning into their fighting style. Unit permanently gains additional To-Defend for each Gold generated in the city from ore.
#UA Poor Vision
*ux183.png
 POOR VISION
Unnatural darkness of Eternal Night impaired the unit's vision. All non-Death creatures get -2 Ranged Attack power as long as Eternal Night is in effect.
#UA Malnourished
*ux184.png
 MALNOURISHED
Youth who grow up and train during food shortage or famine in the city cannot develop to their full potential. The unit permanently suffers -1 Melee Attack and -2 Armor penalties.
#UA HIEROPHANY
*ux186.png
 HIEROPHANY
The afflicted unit loses 50% of its Armor along with its immunities, Lightning Resistance, Negate First Strike, and all mobility perks.
Divine Epiphany is considered an effect from direct interaction with a divine manifestation and is not classified as manipulation by magic. Therefore, it cannot be prevented by Magic Immunity.
#UA ZEAL

 ZEAL

#UA BLAZE OF GLORY
*ux191.png

Enchanted unit gains Armor Piercing along with Melee equal to the unit's Armor and Thrown attack equal to its current Ranged Attack strength, but loses First Strike, all of its original base Armor value (not including Armor as a result of other enchantments), and both Ranged Attack strength and Ammo.
#UA SHADOW STRIKE
*ux192.png
 SHADOW STRIKE
Enchanted unit gains Thrown Attack strength equal to 1 + 33% of its Melee strength (rounded down). If the unit already has a thrown ability, 1 + 33% of its Melee strength is added to Thrown attack strength.
#UA REVENANT

 REVENANT
In combat, enchanted unit gains Death Touch 0 if not already having Death Gaze, as well as Regeneration 1 (if the unit already has Regeneration, +1 to its Regeneration value) until the end of combat.
#UA VAMPIRISM
*ux185.png
 VAMPIRISM
Enchanted unit turns into a lesser vampire with Undead traits, Bloodsucker, and the ability to Create Undead. Half of its Thrown and Breath Attacks strength is transferred to melee, and Thrown/Breath strength that the unit currently has is reduced to no more than 1. Lesser vampires are Death creatures that have Bloodsucker, the ability to Create Undead, and all traits of undead creatures, including Death Immunity, Illusion Immunity, and Cold Immunity, but can no longer gain experience.
This effect can't be dispelled.

#UA FIERY FURY

 FIERY FURY

These bonuses, except for Rock Ranged Attack, do not stack with Flame Blade.

#UA THE CHOSEN

#UA BINDING
*ux116.png
 BINDING
Friendly unit enchantments cannot be dispelled while the binding is in effect. If the hero is Fantastic, it cannot be banished from existence by spells and effects such as Exorcise, Banish, or the Great Unsummoning.  
Binding also hoodwinks opponent wizards into attempting to dispel the enchantment under its protection, regardless of its effectiveness. The urge to dispel the protected enchantment increases with the number of enchantments under its protection.

#UA FIGURE
*ux264.png
 FIGURE
"Figure" refers to the number of soldiers or subunits inside the unit. The unit status always displays attributes for each figure. Each figure has its own Attack Strength and Health Points. The total damage done by the unit is the sum of all figures combined. As the unit receives damage, the number of figures may be reduced, thus decreasing the total attack strength.

If the unit has the innate Thrown ability, its Thrown strength is converted into the strength of Lightning Breath. Lightning Breath power is considered innate and can grow stronger with veterancy levels.

#UA FAIRY MAZE

#UA STRENGTH OF WATER
*ux318.png
 STRENGTH OF WATER
The unit could replenish and increase their strength by absorb excess water in combat environment.
Ocean/Moat/Water Hole tile
- +2 Melee, +2 Range Attack
- Gain Thrown attack strength equal to half of Range attack
- Replenish 4 Health and 1 Ammo at the start of combat turn
- If battlefield is wet Overland tile, replenish another 4 Health and 1 Ammo at the start of combat turn.
Floating/Snow/Swamp tile
- +1 Melee, +1 Range Attack
- Replenish 1 Health at the start of combat turn.
- If battlefield is wet Overland tile, replenish another 1 Health and 1 Ammo at the start of combat turn.

#UA CHOSEN OF GAIA
*ux330.png
 CHOSEN OF GAIA
The hero has been blessed with an extraordinary connection to creatures of the realm of Nature, boosting their To-Hit and To-Defend chances by 3% for each experience level in combat. Super Chosen of Gaia (*) increases this effect by 50%.
If more than one hero has this ability, only bonus from hero that offer the highest bonus would be implemented.
#UA CHOSEN OF AETHER
*ux331.png
 CHOSEN OF AETHER

If more than one hero has this ability, only bonus from hero that offer the highest bonus would be implemented.

#UA MECHANICAL MASTER
*ux335.png
 MECHANICAL MASTER
The hero has an extraordinary talent in mechanical machinary, all Mechanical units on the same side in combat gain +20% To-Hit plus +2% To-Hit per hero level and +10% To-Defend plus +2% To-Defend per hero level in combat.
Super Mechanical Master (*) all Mechanical units on the same side in combat gain +20% To-Hit plus +3% To-Hit per hero level and +10% To-Defend plus +3% To-Defend per hero level in combat and if the Health of a mechanical unit on the same side is lower than 50%, it heals 1 damage at the end of the turn.
If Mechanical Master hero left the combat. Mechanical units still gain +20% To-Hit and +10% To-Defend until the end of the turn.
#UA ELEMENTAL MASTER
*ux336.png
 ELEMENTAL MASTER
The hero has been blessed with an extraordinary connection to elementals and their spirits, boosting their To-Hit and To-Defend chances by 4% for each experience level as well as Resistance and Health Point by 1 for each experience level in combat. Super Elemental Master (*) increases this effect by 50%.
If more than one hero has this ability, only bonus from hero that offer the highest bonus would be implemented.
#UA IRRESISTIBLE CHARGE
*ux337.png
 IRRESISTIBLE CHARGE
The hero has an extraordinary skill in commanding cavalry, especially charge. All regular units gains +1 Melee for each movement point spent in that turn until the end of their movement turn. Super Irresistible Charge (*) increases this effect by 50%.
If more than one hero has this ability, only bonus from hero that offer the highest bonus would be implemented.
#UA PLANAR GUIDE
*ux338.png
 PLANAR GUIDE
The hero has ability to grant nearby friendly units ability to travel across the planes without need of utilize Tower of Wizardary or additional magic from the Wizard until the end of turn.
The hero would allow the wizard to utilize this ability only after the wizard have already known the spell Plane Shift or both plane have already connected through Tower of Wizardary.
#UA CHANNELER'S PUPPET
*ux345.png
 CHANNELER'S PUPPET
This hero is actually life-like doll animated and remoted controlled by will of the Channeler. Melee and Magic Range attack of this hero will be +1 for each 30 points of the owner's Base Casting Skill. Armor will be +1 for each 50 points of the owner's Base Casting Skill. Spell charge and ability would change according to owner's spellbooks.
#UA ASCENDED PUPPET
*ux346.png
 ASCENDED PUPPET
This puppet hero has ascended and gain their own will while still bind with loyalty to their parent Channeler. Their ability is upgraded and changed based on spellbooks and retorts of their parent.
#UA STRAYED PUPPET
*ux369.png
 STRAYED PUPPET
This puppet hero has lost connection to their parent Channeler of the ancient past but keep on animated by the will of their own. They lost access to majority of the power of their parent and have only what their original creator parent left behind.
#UA RIGHTEOUS WARD
*ux370.png
 RIGHTEOUS WARD
The hero is protected by ward of holy miracle bestowed by divinities. The ward gains more permanent unit enchantments as hero level get higher. Super Righteous Ward grows at 50% faster rate.
Ward Level 3: Bless
Ward Level 5: Holy Armor
Ward Level 7: Divine Protection
Ward Level 9: Melee Exorcise -X (X=hero's level)
(Super Righteous Ward only)
Ward Level 10: True Sight, Fire Immunity, becomes Life creature
Ward Level 12: Invulnerability
Ward Level 13: Magic Immunity
#UA ARCANE WARD
*ux371.png
 ARCANE WARD
The hero is protected by ward of protection constructed by arcane power. The ward gains more permanent unit enchantments as hero level get higher. Super Arcane Ward grows at 50% faster rate.
Ward Level 3: Resist Magic
Ward Level 5: Resist Elements
Ward Level 7: Elemental Armor
Ward Level 9: Iron Skin
(Super Arcane Ward only)
Ward Level 10: Insulation
Ward Level 12: Invisibility
Ward Level 13: Magic Immunity
#UA CHAOS BOON

 CHAOS BOON
The hero is the reciever of the gift of Chaos. Their physical body undergoes perpetual mutation and evolution into Chaos mutant. The Boon gains additional permanent enchantments as hero level get higher.

Boon Level 5: Spirit Link
Boon Level 6: Chaos Channel Fire Breath
Boon Level 7: Chaos Channel Armor

Boon Level 9: Insulation
#UA DEATH ASCENSION
*ux373.png
 DEATH ASCENSION
The hero is the reciever of the gift of Death. Their body and soul undergoes transformation into vampiric Death creature. The ascension gains additional permanent enchantments as hero level get higher.
Ascension Level 1: Life Steal -X (X=hero's level)
Ascension Level 2: Bloodsucker, Poison Immunity
Ascension Level 3: Fear, Death Immunity
Ascension Level 4: Spirit Link
Ascension Level 5: Wraith Form, Illusion Immunity
Ascension Level 6: Shadow Strike
Ascension Level 7: Bloodlust
Ascension Level 8: Revenant
Ascension Level 9: Create Undead
#UA ARTIFICIAL AUGMENTATION
