 ARTIFICIAL AUGMENTATION
This unit has been converted into half-mechanical being. The unit gains +2 Melee, +2 Armor, Armor Piercing, Illusion Immunity, Death Immunity, and becomes Mechanical.
#UA ARCHMAGE'S TEACHING
*ux349.png
 ARCHMAGE'S TEACHING
This unit is practicing magic according to teaching and training principles of the Archmage. 
The unit with casting skill, get casting skill +15.
The unit with spell charge, get spell charge +1.
The unit with magic ranged attack, get ammo +2.
#UA ARCHMAGE'S DISCIPLE
*ux350.png
 ARCHMAGE'S DISCIPLE
This hero is studying magic under personal guidance of the Archmage as one of their primary disciples. This hero gains +40 Spell Skill even if this hero originally could not cast any magic.
#UA LUCKY STAR
*ux351.png
 LUCKY STAR
The unit becomes unusually Lucky until the end of combat.
#UA CONJURING PACT
*ux352.png
 CONJURING PACT
If the enchanted unit is Fantastic creature, it would fall under the Conjurer's influence and fight for the Conjurer until the end of combat. If the enchanted unit is regular unit, it would suffer -10% To-Hit and To-Defend from disorientation instead.
#UA SPIRIT LINK
*ux353.png
 SPIRIT LINK
The enchanted unit gains +2 Resistance permanently. If the enchanted unit is Fantastic creature, it gains sentience, able to earn experience. If the unit is regular unit, it could gains bonus as if they are fantastic creature. The enchanted unit enchanted with Spirit Link could not be targeted by spell and ability that affected only on fantastic creature.
#UA POWER OVERWHELMING
*ux368.png
 POWER OVERWHELMING
This creature has already been enchanted with overwhelming power from a single realm. Until the end of combat, the unit has no capacity to be enchanted with anymore of Power of Nature, nor Power of Sorcery, nor Power of Chaos, nor Power of Life, nor Power of Death.
#UA ARTIFICER UPGRADE
*ux230.png
 ARTIFICER UPGRADE
Mechanical units produced by the wizard's city gain +1 Melee/Range Attack, +1 Armor, +1 Resistance, +1 Movement Point, and magic weapons.
#UA MAGICAL WEAPON
*ux286.png
 MAGICAL WEAPON
The unit will be equipped with a magical weapon. The unit equipped with a magical weapon gains +10% to Melee, Physical Range, and Thrown To-Hit, and its attacks will ignore Weapon Immunity.
#UA MITHRIL UPGRADE
*ux287.png
 MITHRIL UPGRADE
The unit will be equipped with equipment made of Mithril. The unit equipped with Mithril equipment gains +1 Melee, Physical Range, and Thrown Attack strength, as well as +1 Armor.
#UA ADAMANTIUM UPGRADE
*ux288.png
 ADAMANTIUM UPGRADE
The unit will be equipped with equipment made of Adamantium. The unit equipped with Adamantium equipment gains +2 Melee, Physical Range, and Thrown Attack strength, as well as +2 Armor.
#UA GENERIC BARBARIAN
*ux290.png
 BARBARIAN SPECIALIZATION
Barbarian crews are skilled fighters, gaining +10% To-Hit, and are adept at wilderness travel, having the Pathfinding skill compared to crews of other races.
#UA GENERIC BEASTMAN
*ux291.png
 BEASTMAN SPECIALIZATION
Beastman crews are aggressive fighters, gaining +1 Melee, and possess more robust endurance, gaining +1 Health compared to crews of other races.
#UA GENERIC DARK ELF
*ux292.png
 DARK ELF SPECIALIZATION
Dark Elf crews possess basic skills in the arcane arts, allowing them to perform a magic range attack instead of a physical range attack. They also have strong resistance to poison and magical effects, gaining +2 Resistance compared to crews of other races.
#UA GENERIC DARK ELF CATAPULT
*ux292.png
 DARK ELF SPECIALIZATION
Dark Elf Catapults launch magical Fireballs toward the target instead of hurling rocks. Their crews possess strong resistance to poison and magical effects, gaining +2 Resistance compared to crews of other races.
#UA GENERIC DRACONIAN
*ux293.png
 DRACONIAN SPECIALIZATION
Draconian crews, due to their dragon blood, have increased magical resistance, gaining +1 Resistance compared to crews of other races.
#UA GENERIC DWARF
*ux294.png
 DWARF SPECIALIZATION
Dwarven ships and war machines have metal plating, granting +3 Armor but at a +25% cost. Their crews possess strong resistance to poison and magical effects, gaining +2 Resistance, and are skilled in mountain hiking, having the Mountaineer skill compared to crews of other races.
#UA GENERIC GNOLL
*ux295.png
 GNOLL SPECIALIZATION
Gnoll crews are more ferocious, gaining +2 Melee, and their vessels move faster, gaining +1 Movement compared to crews and ships of other races.
#UA GENERIC HALFLING
*ux296.png
 HALFLING SPECIALIZATION
Halfling crews lack ferocity, suffering -1 Melee, but possess extraordinary luck, having the Lucky skill compared to crews of other races.
#UA GENERIC HIGH ELF
*ux297.png
 HIGH ELF SPECIALIZATION
High Elf crews are highly skilled, refined over their long lives, gaining +10% To-Hit. They are attuned to forests, possessing the Forester skill, and have higher resistance to poison and curses, gaining +1 Resistance compared to crews of other races.
#UA GENERIC HIGH MAN
*ux298.png
 HIGH MAN SPECIALIZATION
The High Man's skilled craftsmen make their mechanical units 15% cheaper, but their crews are superstitious and easy to fall victim to poison and magical effects (-1 Resistance) due to their ignorance toward the magical threats.
#UA GENERIC KLACKON
*ux299.png
 KLACKON SPECIALIZATION
Klackon vessels and machines are sturdier, gaining +2 Armor, thanks to their light but extremely durable carapace plating on the exterior.
#UA GENERIC LIZARDMAN
*ux300.png
 LIZARDMAN SPECIALIZATION
Lizardman crews possess more robust endurance, gaining +1 Health, but have weaker constitution against poison and magical effects, suffering -1 Resistance compared to crews of other races.
#UA GENERIC NOMAD
*ux301.png
 NOMAD SPECIALIZATION
Nomad crews are more proficient with logistics, gaining +2 Ammo, and land-based mechanical units get +1 Overland Movement. They also possess robust resistance against poison and magical effects, gaining +3 Resistance compared to crews of other races.
#UA GENERIC ORC SHIP
*ux302.png
 ORC SPECIALIZATION
Orc seamen and artillery crews are well-respected profession in Orc society, making artillery corps and naval service prestigious careers. Many well-to-do Orc families eagerly send their members into these military professions. Due to how important they are within Orc hierarchy, they have no taboo about self preserving in combat and could perform tactical retreat.
#UA GENERIC ORC WAR MACHINE
*ux302.png
 ORC SPECIALIZATION
Orc machine operating crews are highly valued and well-paid positions in Orc military, making them a sought-after role for well-to-do Orc families. Many such families send their less successful members into these privileged military positions.
#UA GENERIC TROLL
*ux303.png
 TROLL SPECIALIZATION
Troll ships require special modifications to avoid becoming flotsam in the hands of their crews (+50% cost, +3 Health). Fortunately, Troll crews excel at wrecking enemy vessels, gaining +3 Melee and +1 Resistance. Their love of seafood and fishing skills means no additional food is needed to sustain them.
#UA GENERIC XUANYUAN
*ux304.png
 XUANYUAN SPECIALIZATION
Xuanyuan's ships and artillery corps are known for have more crews in their unit as redundency spare (+5 Health) to compensate their poor battlefield protection (-1 Armor) compared to equivalent ships and artillery corps of other races.
#UA GENERIC RAKHSHASA
*ux305.png
 RAKHSHASA SPECIALIZATION
Due to the Rakhshasa's aversion to water, their ships are designed to be faster and more durable, gaining +1 Armor and +1 Movement. The interiors are filled with potted plants, creating a jungle-like environment that grants the crew the Forester skill, making them feel at home.
#UA GENERIC HAWKMAN
*ux306.png
 HAWKMAN SPECIALIZATION
Hawkman machine crews are experts in alpine warfare, possessing the Mountaineer skill, which enables them to perform better in mountainous environments compared to crews of other races.
#UA GENERIC GOBLIN
*ux307.png
 GOBLIN SPECIALIZATION
Goblin crews operate in flotillas, gaining +2 figures, but their ships are smaller, resulting in -33% Attack strength and -50% Health due to their disregard for safety in design. Additionally, Goblin crews are reckless, suffering -10% To-Defend compared to crews of other races.
#UA POX HOST
*ux308.png
 POX HOST
This unit is a host of highly infectious Goblin Pox, which is strongly virulent for non-Goblins. In combat, all Goblin units suffer -1 Attack, and -1 Armor, while all non-Goblin units suffer -3 Attack, -3 Armor, and -1 Resistance. Once last unit with Pox Host of their in combat destroyed, their Goblin Pox is disappeared from combat.
#UA PLANEWALKING
*ux309.png
 PLANEWALKING
Enchanted unit gains ability to Teleporting and Plane Shifting. Teleporting allows a unit to move to any location on the combat map for a cost of 1 Movement point. Plane Shifting allows unit to instantly shift between the planes at no Movement cost Once the other plane has been discovered by researching the Plane Shift spell, or at least one Tower of Wizardry must be unlocked.
#UA TRANSIENT SHIFTER
*ux309.png
 TRANSIENT SHIFTER
The unit has been temporary granted ability to instantly shift between the planes at no Movement cost until the end of turn. The other plane must have been discovered by researching the Plane Shift spell, or at least one Tower of Wizardry must be unlocked in order to use this ability.
#IP INSULATION
*ux190.png
 INSULATION
Surrounds the target unit with a thin layer of vacuum that protects from electric, fire, and cold attacks.
The equipped unit gains Fire Immunity, Cold Immunity, and Lightning Resistance.
#IP SPELLCHARGE
 SPELL CHARGES
This option allows you to store combat spells in weapons, allowing the hero equipped with the item to cast the stored spell a selected number of times each combat.
#IP SPELL SKILL
 SPELL SKILL
This item power increases the spellcasting capacity (MP) of the equipped hero. It does not enable spellcasting on heroes that do not already have the ability to cast spells.
#IP SPELL SAVE
 SPELL SAVE
This item power increases the Resistance penalty inflicted by spells cast by the hero wielding the item. It does not affect special attacks that might require resistance rolls, only spells.
#IP FLAMING
 FLAMING
Flaming items are more powerful, raising all relevant Attack strengths by an additional 3.
#IP SHADOW PIERCING
 SHADOW PIERCING
A weapon granted with Shadow Piercing can damage opponents by cutting through their shadows.
"Thrown" equals half the base Melee Attack strength of the unit. This ability is different from the Death unit enchantment of "Shadow Strike" and can stack with it.
#IP EXORCIST
 EXORCIST
The Exorcist makes the attacked Fantastic unit figure resist or be banished from existence for each attacking figure. It also grants the Bless enchantment.
#IP DIVINE PROTECTION
*ux222.png
 DIVINE PROTECTION
The wielder of the item becomes "Lucky" and gains Death Immunity.
#IP RECHARGE
*ux245.png
 RECHARGE
The equipped unit starts combat with +4 Ammo.
#IP EGOISM
 EGOISM
The unit wielding this item becomes extremely aware of their own importance and will maximize their effort to improve themselves. It doubles EXP gained from all sources.
#IP DARK FORCE
 DARK FORCE
The forces of darkness empower the unit at the beginning of each combat, restoring their Health to the maximum amount and granting a +10% chance To-Hit and To-Defend. However, the evil force also inflicts one point of irrecoverable damage to the unit at the beginning of their combat turn.
#IP AMPLIFIER
 AMPLIFIER
All friendly spells deal or heal 1 more damage if they successfully deal any damage. Multiple copies of this ability do not stack. The unit wielding the item does not need to cast the spell, but must be present in the battle where the spell takes effect.
#IP STEALTH
 STEALTH
The equipped hero gains Stealth, making them impossible to see, hear, or detect outside combat:
- The hero does not trigger Wizard's Pact violations.
- The hero can accurately scout the contents of Lairs, Nodes, or other encounter zones, including the type and exact quantity of all defenders.
- The hero is not shown on the overland map, appearing as if invisible to others (note: this does not affect the AI).
#IP VAMPIRIC
 VAMPIRIC WEAPON
All damage done by this weapon converts fallen foes into Undead and forces the attacked target to make a resistance roll at a -5 Resistance penalty. For each point the Resistance roll fails by, the defending unit loses one hit point, while the attacker gains one.
#IP MYSTIC POWER
 MYSTIC POWER
The equipped unit receives tremendous mystical enchantment from an artifact of power, gaining +3 Melee Attack strength, +2 Resistance, and +8 Health Points.
This effect can stack with the Life unit enchantment of "Lionheart."
#UA ECHO OF THE DEEP
*ux216.png
 ECHO OF THE DEEP
The Kraken's hunting ground is in the water. This amphibious crustacean will be submerged when staying on sea or lake tiles. A similar effect can also occur magically due to space-time distortion from a Sorcery node.  
If combat occurs on a water map or at a Sorcery node, it becomes invisible, gains +2 Movement points, +10% To-Defend, and possesses Fire Immunity.
#IP COLOSSAL POWER
 COLOSSAL POWER
A hero equipped with this artifact gains the effects of Colossal Strength (additional 1+40% of original Melee, Thrown, and Physical Ranged attack strength) and Iron Skin (+5 Armor).
#UA The Master Engineer
*Units\u0x3_1.png
 THE MASTER ENGINEER
....The Master Engineer is a renowned member of the Mechanician's Guild, a title not easily attained without proven skill and acceptance from his Dwarven peers. Unlike other Dwarven masters who spend most of their time fine-tuning their workshop's creations to perfection, he prefers to see his own inventions in live battlefield situations, using them as a way to improve and gather inspiration for his future inventions.
#UA The Berserker
*Units\u1x3_1.png
 THE BERSERKER
....The Berserker is a warrior of great renown, driven by an insatiable lust for combat and, some say, an unhinged personality. Known for charging into battle with little regard for self-preservation or tactics, he survives to seek out more foes foolish enough to underestimate him. His goals in life are simple: glory in battle, good ale, many women, and a fiery death. He also has an affinity for golden oddities, such as his prized winged helmet.
#UA The Sage
*Units\u2x3_1.png
 THE SAGE
....The Sage has devoted his long life to the academic study of magical arts. He travels far and wide across worlds in search of ever greater knowledge and understanding of arcane theories. His quest has led him here, to the land where the greatest wizards reside. He offers his services for hire, seeking to gain proximity to these powerful wizards and acquire even more knowledge to further his lifelong pursuit.
#UA The Dervish
*Units\u3x3_1.png
 THE DERVISH
....The Dervish is a renowned ascetic from the desert wilderness. His life as a warrior is guided by divine revelation, dedicating all his gains from service to the Wizard whom the divine inspired him to serve. He willingly gives away his gold to his master and prefers a simple, austere life. Despite his calm demeanor, his bow can swiftly become deadly to those he deems enemies, striking with the precision of one who has mastered both discipline and devotion.
#UA The Beastmaster
*Units\u4x3_1.png
 THE BEASTMASTER
....The Beastmaster is more at home in the wild than in the company of men. Considered odd at the best of times, many claim he is a bastard child of the Beastmen. As such, he is rarely welcomed in human abodes and spends more time among his beasts. Perhaps in an effort to understand the people who fear him, he lends his services as a mercenary, offering his unique connection to the wild creatures as both a boon and a mystery to those who dare to work with him.
#UA The Bard
*Units\u5x3_1.png
 THE BARD
....The Bard is a renowned storyteller and musician whose tales are sung throughout the lands, inspiring many hearts. Yet, she is never satisfied with her latest work, always searching for that one true story that will fulfill her ambition. The Bard's origins are not entirely clear; her youthful looks and petite stature suggest innocence, yet her eyes speak of wisdom and age that do not match her face, hinting at a past filled with secrets and untold stories.
#UA The Centurion
*Units\u6x3_1.png
 THE CENTURION
....The Centurion comes from humble beginnings and rose through the ranks from a mere grunt to become the highest-ranked Orc Centurion, commanding the legionaries, rather than being merely a decorative noble-born general. Renowned as a militarist and a skilled tactician, he is a leader any lord would want to train and lead their army, respected by his troops for his experience and fearlessness on the battlefield.
#UA The Healer
*Units\u7x3_1.png
 THE HEALER
....The Healer was a prodigy who studied the healing arts in a prestigious university among High Men. One day, she decided that merely practicing and studying medicine in her university was not enough. Against her professors' objections, she refused to ordain as clergy or join the Medical Guild. Instead, she devoted herself as a traveling healer, wandering the planes to further heal those in need and contribute her skills to the world, seeking to make a tangible difference wherever she went.
#UA The Huntress
*Units\u8x3_1.png
 THE HUNTRESS
....The Huntress is a skilled hunter and accomplished tracker. Despite her friendly demeanor and disheveled appearance, she is tough as nails when it comes to survival. She does not speak of her reasons for constantly traveling the planes, but it is clear she is tracking or searching for someone or something she once lost, a mystery that drives her relentless journey.
#UA The Thief
*Units\u9x3_1.png
 THE THIEF
....The Thief may have begun her career acquiring desirable objects, but she is now known for much more. In battle, her swift reflexes and agile moves make it seem as if she can disappear on the spot. Raised by Halflings, she may even have Halfling blood. She takes pride in her heritage and plans to achieve even greater heights, determined to ensure her people are never underestimated again.
#UA The Druid
*Units\u10x3_1.png
 THE DRUID
....The Druid cultivates the age-old traditions of nature worship among High Elves. Devoted to studying the mystical ways of nature and the energies hidden within the land, he can commune with nature and its creatures, making him an excellent ranger and scout. Always eager to lend his skills and knowledge, he enjoys spreading the power of nature wherever he goes, guiding others to appreciate and respect the forces that shape the world.
#UA The War Monk
*Units\u11x3_1.png
 THE WAR MONK
....The War Monk lives the life of a monk in search of true understanding of the self and the ultimate truth. Believing in balance and peace, he is not averse to violence, which he sees as part of the natural cycle of life. He lends his lightning-fast reflexes and powerful fists to causes he deems worthy or interesting, and once he gives his word, he remains loyal in service, viewing every action as a step toward enlightenment.
#UA The Warrior Mage
*Units\u12x3_1.png
 THE WARRIOR MAGE
....The Warrior Mage believes adaptability is the key to survival and victory. Trained in both magic and combat, he supports his troops against any enemy. Less favorable rumors claim he failed to become a true mage due to his temper and love of the blade. Regardless, he is a valuable soldier to have at your side, using his unique blend of magical and martial prowess to turn the tide of battle.
#UA The Magician
*Units\u13x3_1.png
 THE MAGICIAN
....The Magician is a Dwarven spellcaster, a rarity among a race that typically disdains magic. Possessing great power and a taste for destructive and brutal magics, he is said to be slightly unhinged, with his body clearly twisted by the chaotic power coursing through his arcane veins. His unpredictable nature makes him both a terrifying and fascinating ally, as his volatile magic can turn the battlefield into a storm of destruction.
#UA The Assassin
*Units\u14x3_1.png
 THE ASSASSIN
....The Assassin is known for his mastery of deadly poisons acquired from the most venomous snakes in the land. A whisperer to snakes, rumors claim he is immune to his own poisons, having subjected himself to snakebites regularly. Whether wielding his spear or a simple hairpin, he is always prepared to kill, striking swiftly and silently, leaving only whispers and fear in his wake.
#UA The Wind Mage
*Units\u15x3_1.png
 THE WIND MAGE
....The Wind Mage is a High Elf spellcaster specializing in air and wind magic. Young by elven standards, he would normally remain in his college of magic were it not for his constant thirst for travel. Perhaps his natural affinity for air drives his desire for freedom and change. Despite his aloof personality and terrible attention deficit, he is valuable, albeit challenging, to work with, as his unpredictable nature often leads to unexpected and powerful results.
#UA The Ranger
*Units\u16x3_1.png
 THE RANGER
....The Ranger is sometimes referred to as the Elf in Tights, a moniker he doesn't seem bothered by, as he claims the tights provide better flexibility in all situations. A multi-talented Elf, he excels in wilderness activities, serving as a tracker and scout. He takes great pride in his mastery of the bow, constantly striving to prove his worth above all others, and his sharp eye and quick reflexes make him an invaluable ally in both exploration and battle.
#UA The Draconian
*Units\u17x3_1.png
 THE DRACONIAN
....The Draconian is a formidable warrior of imposing stature, with the blood of ancient dragons coursing through his veins. An intimidating foe and a great ally, he, like his ancestors, has a penchant for treasure, embarking on a life of adventure to amass wealth. Instead of riding horses, he prefers to mount Doom Drakes, reigning fire and fear from the skies as he hunts for fortune and glory. His presence on the battlefield is both awe-inspiring and terrifying, as he combines raw power with a fierce determination to claim what he believes is rightfully his.
#UA The Witch
*Units\u18x3_1.png
 THE WITCH
....The Witch earned her nickname as a practitioner of the dark arts, yet defies stereotypes with her seemingly youthful appearance. Many speculate that if her true visage were revealed, it would reflect deep corruption of body and soul. She enjoys the rumors surrounding her and does not seek to dispel them, delighting in the fear and intrigue she stirs wherever she goes. Her mastery of the dark arts is unquestioned, and those who cross her path quickly learn that appearances can be deceiving.
#UA The Bronze Sentinel
*Units\u19x3_1.png
 THE BRONZE SENTINEL
....The Bronze Sentinel is a humanoid of uncertain origin. Is he a man who fell prey to some alchemical experiment? Or is he a divine creature, or perhaps a construct of some great power? The Bronze Sentinel sheds no light on this mystery and prefers to remain enigmatic. For reasons of his own, he will join a Wizard of good renown, offering his considerable strength and mysterious presence, though his true motivations remain a closely guarded secret.
#UA The Ninja
*Units\u20x3_1.png
 THE NINJA
....The Ninja is a master of infiltration arts, known for their ability to conceal their true identity and gender. Rumors abound regarding the Ninja's origins: some claim they are half-Dark Elf and half-Human of Xuanyuan origin, while others argue that "Ninja" is the title bestowed upon the most powerful members of the Nightblade order. The truth remains obscured by propaganda, carefully perpetuated by the Ninja themselves to conceal their true nature and motives. Always a shadow in the night, they operate with stealth and precision, leaving only whispers in their wake.
#UA The Rogue
*Units\u21x3_1.png
 THE ROGUE
....The Rogue is a dashing, flamboyant figure who leaves an impression wherever he goes. Possessing a silver tongue, he inspires great confidence in the troops he accompanies. An adventurer by trade, his exploits have spread his name across the land, inspiring tales of bravery and cunning. However, he is forever on the run from various parties wounded by his personal misconduct towards the fair ladies of the land, a fact that only adds to his reputation as a charming yet controversial figure.
#UA The Amazon
*Units\u22x3_1.png
 THE AMAZON
....The Amazon is a fierce warrior hailing from the fabled Amazons, a tribe of female-only fighters renowned for their skill and determination. Roaming the frontier between the Nomad and Barbarian lands, she proves without a doubt that women are every bit as capable in battle as men, if not more so! The Amazon now lends her sword as a mercenary to further spread the fame of her warrior sisters, serving only those of considerable renown whom she deems worthy of her service. Her reputation as both a fearsome fighter and a symbol of female strength precedes her, and those who earn her respect find themselves with a powerful ally.
#UA The Warlock
*Units\u23x3_1.png
 THE WARLOCK
....The Warlock might have been one of the Master Wizards were it not for a failed experiment that left him scarred and debilitated. Decades ago, this Dark Elf Warlock mastered the secrets of channeling vast quantities of Mana through the magical arts into destructive and deadly forms, until that fateful day. Though the experiment left its mark, he remains a dangerous and powerful Warlock, wielding great mastery over the deadly force of lightning. His abilities to manipulate energy are unmatched, and while he may appear fractured, his power continues to grow, making him a force to be reckoned with.
#UA The Unknown
*Units\u24x3_1.png
 THE UNKNOWN
....The Unknown is just that an enigma. Nothing is known of this person's background or previous exploits. Emerging into this world seeking employment, their skill and power are unquestionable. However, their true motives and nature remain shrouded in the dark cloak of mystery, with no one able to discern whether they are friend or foe. The only certainty is their effectiveness, making them a compelling, if unpredictable, ally or adversary.
#UA The Illusionist
*Units\u25x3_1.png
 THE ILLUSIONIST
....The Illusionist is practically a child, yet possesses frightfully powerful abilities in mind magic and deception. A natural-born trickster, her playful demeanor belies a highly skilled caster capable of creating terrifying illusions that can break even the sturdiest of foes. Beneath her innocent appearance lies a mind capable of manipulating reality itself, making her both a formidable opponent and a master of misdirection.
#UA The Swordsman
*Units\u26x3_1.png
 THE SWORDSMAN
....The Swordsman is a hardened war veteran respected and feared by soldiers across the lands. Some speculate he was once a lord or even a prince who lost everything in an epic duel, with his eye patch serving as a silent testament to his past. Renowned for his tactical brilliance and mastery of the blade, he commands respect both on and off the battlefield, his reputation forged in the fires of countless battles.
#UA The Priestess
*Units\u27x3_1.png
 THE PRIESTESS
....The Priestess is a cleric devoted to the arts of healing and the cause of goodness. Found as a child outside a temple in the holy city of Hawkman, she was trained rigorously but could not ascend to the role of Holy Mother due to her non-Hawkman lineage. Rumored to possess divine beauty and charm, whispers suggest she may have divine parentage or a potent blessing upon her, her presence bringing an aura of peace and reverence wherever she goes.
#UA The Paladin
*Units\u28x3_1.png
 THE PALADIN
The Paladin is a young warrior of great renown, achieving membership in the esteemed Paladin Order at a remarkably early age. Known for his unwavering devotion to aiding those in need and his courage in confronting even the most formidable foes, he is admired by all who value life and justice. His zeal and loyalty, however, sometimes blind him to the complexities of moral choices, as his single-mindedness in pursuit of righteousness can lead him into difficult or even dangerous situations.
#UA The Black Knight
*Units\u29x3_1.png
 THE BLACK KNIGHT
....The Black Knight instills fear and despair in all who face him. A knight of Death itself, he is relentless and without mercy, driven by a morbid obsession with death as an ultimate reward. Renowned for his combat prowess and brutality, he rides a pitch-black horse, his presence a harbinger of doom. Rumored to be a Death Knight incarnate, he is relentless in his pursuit of bringing death to others, leaving nothing but destruction in his wake.
#UA The Arcane Archer
*Units\u30x3_1.png
 THE ARCANE ARCHER
....The Arcane Archer was raised among high elves and trained rigorously in archery, but her unique affinity for magic sets her apart. Able to conjure magical arrows with her exceptional archery skills, her mysterious appearance hints at a dark elf heritage. She is determined to achieve mastery and fame in the name of her high elven family, fiercely guarding her secrets and lineage, knowing that her true potential lies in blending the ancient traditions of her heritage with the arcane powers she wields.
#UA The Knight
*Units\u31x3_1.png
 THE KNIGHT
....The Knight is an elderly yet noble veteran who lives by a strict code of honor, regardless of the lands he traverses or the lords he serves. Speculated to be on a final, noble quest, he remains reticent about his personal goals. Despite his age, his resolve and skill with the sword are as formidable as ever, making him sought after by wise leaders who value his experience, wisdom, and steadfastness. His presence on the battlefield serves as both a symbol of honor and a reminder of the strength that comes with a lifetime of service.
#UA The Necromancer
*Units\u32x3_1.png
 THE NECROMANCER
....The Necromancer delves into forbidden magics, wielding power over death and the undead. Able to animate corpses and manipulate life energies, his abilities are as unnatural as they are feared. Rumors swirl that he himself is sustained by dark magic, seeking to extend his own life or even reverse his own death through his arcane studies. His presence evokes dread, as he commands the forces of decay and reanimation with a chilling expertise, always in search of greater mastery over life and death.
#UA The Everchosen
*Units\u33x3_1.png
 THE EVERCHOSEN
....The Everchosen is a figure of mystery and awe, shrouded in a cloak and helm that conceal his identity. A skilled swordsman and powerful mage, he is whispered to be chosen by the Chaos domain, mutated and twisted into a force of Chaos. Whether true or not, traces of Chaos corruption linger about him, marking him as both formidable and unpredictable. His power radiates with the chaotic energies that flow through him, making him a dangerous and elusive figure whose true intentions remain hidden beneath layers of dark influence.
#UA The Avatar
*Units\u34x3_1.png
 THE AVATAR
....The Avatar embodies the essence of the Right-hand aspect of the Primal Force itself, possibly a divine incarnation on the mortal plane. Though bound by mortal limitations, his spirit is eternal and cannot be destroyed, only temporarily banished. Believers view his arrival as a sign of deliverance and peace, while skeptics fear it heralds cataclysmic events, such as the return of the fabled Spell of Mastery. His presence is a powerful force, evoking both hope and fear, as his true purpose remains a mystery.
#UA The Warmaster
*Units\u272x3_1.png
 THE WARMASTER
....The Warmaster is the most decorated Gnoll commander in history, renowned for his tactical brilliance and ferocity in battle. Leading his jackal pack across the lands, his mere presence strikes fear into enemies and inspires bloodlust in allies. Only rulers of considerable renown can afford his services, fully aware of the havoc he can wreak upon their foes. His reputation precedes him, making him both a feared adversary and a sought-after ally in times of war.
#UA The Gambler
*Units\u273x3_1.png
 THE GAMBLER
....The Gambler is a notorious Halfling and inveterate gambler, barred from revisiting any gambling den twice due to his penchant for bankrupting their owners. Tales abound of his wagers with mortal and even supernatural beings, including a legendary bet with a Chaos Lord that earned him a dubious blessing. In battle, every move is a gamble, risking his life and those of his allies for victory.
#UA The Dreamwalker

 THE DREAMWALKER

Revered as the master of dreams and nightmares, she embodies both fear and fascination. Known simply as the Dreamwalker, her name is spoken only in hushed tones by those who dare to invoke it, for she has the power to twist the fabric of reality and guide others through the dark recesses of their own minds.
#UA The Steelbreaker

 THE STEELBREAKER

Always seeking battles worthy of his reputation, he relishes the opportunity to prove his strength and skills, convinced that no foe is too great for him to conquer. His name strikes fear in enemies and inspires admiration among those who recognize his unparalleled might.
#UA The Grand Inquisitor

His conviction is absolute, and he will stop at nothing to cleanse the world of corruption, regardless of the cost or the alliances he must forge along the way.
#UA The Crone

#UA The Sagittarius

....The Sagittarius is a wise centaur known for wandering between realms, mentoring countless heroes and unlocking their potential. He was also famous as one of the earliest captains of what is now called the "Chironean Guards," leading with a combination of discipline, strategy, and deep knowledge of both combat and healing. His legacy as a leader and teacher continues to inspire those who seek to rise above their limits.
#UA The Swarm Queen

Her presence signifies a formidable force capable of overwhelming foes through coordinated assault, her strategic mind guiding her warriors with precision and strength. Her leadership is a blend of raw power and psychological dominance, making her a force to be reckoned with.
#UA The Sea Lord
*Units\u281x3_1.png
 THE SEA LORD
....The Sea Lord is a legendary Lizardman who sails the oceans atop an ancient dragon turtle. Known from the sunken ruins of Atlantis, he rises to challenge wrongdoers when the seas are threatened. Stories vary on his appearance, sometimes depicting him as youthful, other times as ancient, yet always accompanied by the same dragon turtle. Some believe he alone knows the location of mythical seaweed that grants eternal youth, while others see him as a guardian of ancient knowledge and power, wielding secrets of the deep to protect the balance of the seas.
#UA The War Chief
*Units\u283x3_1.png
 THE WAR CHIEF
....The War Chief is a controversial troll chieftain known for his unmatched strength and cunning, surpassing even his fellow trolls in both prowess and intellect. Formerly of the Frost Club clan, he transformed it from the weakest to the strongest through relentless warfare. Now bored with peace, he seeks new battles and challenges, particularly those among master wizards whose conflicts promise excitement and worthy adversaries. His insatiable hunger for combat drives him to constantly seek out the fiercest opponents, always aiming to test his abilities against those who would prove a challenge.
#UA The Planewalker
*Units\u284x3_1.png
 THE PLANEWALKER
....The Planewalker is a renowned traveler between planes, an enigmatic figure whose origins and motives remain obscured. Traversing unstable space-time, he roams between realms with ease, often stirring trouble and disseminating knowledge of other planes. Though a trickster and troublemaker, his insights into interdimensional affairs make him both a valuable ally and a dangerous foe. With towers of wizardry now largely inaccessible due to their guardians, public knowledge of other planes in recent times has mostly come from him, further cementing his role as both a source of arcane wisdom and a wild card in the balance of power across realms.
#UA The Elementalist

 THE ELEMENTALIST
....The Elementalist hails from Conflux, where elemental forces converge. Little is known of her, but her ability to summon and command elemental entities suggests she holds considerable influence in her realm. Her presence on the material plane remains a mystery, known only to the wizard she serves and the secrets they share. Her power over the elemental forces is undeniable, and those who encounter her often find themselves caught in the currents of raw magic she wields with ease.

#UA Trireme
*Units\u35x3_1.png
 TRIREME
The Trireme is a basic naval unit, built from floatable softwood using an older design. Powered by sails and three rows of oarsmen, it offers flexibility in combat and features a bronze ram for charging. However, it lacks bowmen or artillery for ranged attacks. While cheaper to produce, the Trireme is outperformed by more modern ship designs.
 
The Trireme and its crews have unique designs and characteristics based on the race. Each race adapts the Trireme to suit their strengths, making them different from one another in appearance and function.

#UA Galley

 GALLEY

Constructed from hardwood, it features both sails and rowers, similar to older designs, but carries more crew equipped with bows and arrows. This design is highly popular across both planes, with nearly every race having its own equivalent of this type of ship.
 
The Galley and its crews of each races have their own unique design and characteristic. This make them difference from each others.

#UA High Elf Galley
*Units\u36x3_1.png
 GALLEY
The Galley is a standard naval unit widely used in contemporary naval combat. Constructed from hardwood, it combines sails and rowers like older designs but carries a larger crew equipped with bows and arrows. This design is highly popular across both planes, with nearly every race having its own version of this ship.
 
High Elf Galley crews are highly skilled, refined over their long lives (+10% To-Hit), attuned to forests (Forester skill), and have higher resistance to poison and curses (+1 Resistance) compared to crews of other races.

Due to their place among Orc's high society, there is no problem for them to self preserving and perform tactical retreat in combat.
#UA Troll Galley
*Units\u36x3_1.png
 GALLEY
The Galley is a standard naval unit widely used in contemporary naval combat. Constructed from hardwood, it combines sails and rowers like older designs but carries a larger crew equipped with bows and arrows. This design is highly popular across both planes, with nearly every race having its own version of this ship.
 
Troll ships require special modifications to avoid becoming flotsam in the hands of their crews (+50% cost, +3 Health). Fortunately, Troll seamen excel at wrecking enemy vessels (+3 Melee, +1 Resistance). Their love of seafood and fishing skills also means no additional food is needed to sustain them.

#UA Rakhshasa Galley
*Units\u36x3_1.png
 GALLEY
The Galley is a standard naval unit widely used in contemporary naval combat. Constructed from hardwood, it combines sails and rowers like older designs but carries a larger crew equipped with bows and arrows. This design is highly popular across both planes, with nearly every race having its own version of this ship.
 
Due to the Rakhshasa's aversion to water, their ships are designed to be faster and more durable (+1 Armor and +1 Movement). The interiors are filled with potted plants, giving the crew a jungle-like environment (Forester skill), making make them feel at home.
#UA Goblin Galleys
*Units\u36x3_1.png
 GALLEYS
The Galley is a standard naval unit widely used in contemporary naval combat. Constructed from hardwood, it combines sails and rowers like older designs but carries a larger crew equipped with bows and arrows. This design is highly popular across both planes, with nearly every race having its own version of this ship.
 
Goblin Galleys are operated in flotillas (+2 figures) but their ships are smaller (-33% Attack strength) and designs are disregard safety (-50% Health) and Goblin crews are also reckless (-10% To-Defend) compared to crews of other races.
#UA Fire Galley
*Units\u257x3_1.png
 FIRE GALLEY
The Fire Galley is an advanced naval unit designed for intense close combat. It upgrades the standard galley with a heavy flamethrower that projects alchemical fire, which water cannot extinguish. The Fire Galley features enhanced propulsion with additional oars and oarsmen for increased maneuverability. Due to the need for extra space and crew for the flamethrower and alchemical fire storage, there is less room for arrow ammunition.
 
The Fire Galley and its crews of each races have their own unique design and characteristic. This make them difference from each others.
#UA Beastman Fire Galley
*Units\u257x3_1.png
 FIRE GALLEY
The Fire Galley is an advanced naval unit built for intense close combat. An upgrade of the standard galley, it is equipped with a heavy flamethrower that unleashes alchemical fire, which cannot be extinguished by water. Enhanced propulsion with additional oars and oarsmen improves maneuverability. However, the space needed for the flamethrower and alchemical fire storage reduces room for arrow ammunition.
 
Beastman Fire Galley crews are aggressive fighters (+1 Melee) and possess more robust endurance (+1 Health) compared to crews of other races.

#UA Warship
*Units\u38x3_1.png
 WARSHIP
The Warship is an elite naval unit, known for its speed and lethality. It features advanced hull construction, making it larger than earlier designs and capable of carrying artillery. Equipped with multiple masts and advanced sails, the Warship also allows for more crew members to serve as marines, providing strong melee combat protection for the vessel.
 
The Warship and its crews of each races have their own unique design and characteristic. This make them difference from each others.

 CATAPULT

#UA Ballista
*Units\u218x3_1.png
 BALLISTA
Ballista is a common siege unit. A heavy siege weapon, this heavy mechanical bolt caster design to thrown javelin-size bolt to impact and piercing the target's armor from far away. Ballista are using widely among different races with relatively advanced knowledge on mechanical works. The ballista works best against heavily armored units. Basic design of the ballista does not included self-propelling mechanism, so mobility might be an issue for army that using it.
 
Ballista was originally an invention of ancient Xuanyuan which later spread to other civilized races on both planes due to banishment of the Xuanyuan from Arcanus to Myrror. This allowed other civilized races to study this contraption.
#UA Beastman Ballista
*Units\u218x3_1.png
 BALLISTA
The Ballista is a siege unit of a heavy mechanical bolt caster designed to launch javelin-sized bolts to pierce enemy armor from a distance. Widely used among races with advanced mechanical knowledge, it excels against heavily armored units but suffers from limited mobility. Originally invented by the ancient Xuanyuan, the Ballista spread to other civilized races after their exile to Myrror.
 
Beastman Ballista crews are aggressive fighters (+1 Melee) and possess more robust endurance (+1 Health) compared to crews of other races.

 BALLISTA
The Ballista is a siege unit of a heavy mechanical bolt caster designed to launch javelin-sized bolts to pierce enemy armor from a distance. Widely used among races with advanced mechanical knowledge, it excels against heavily armored units but suffers from limited mobility. Originally invented by the ancient Xuanyuan, the Ballista spread to other civilized races after their exile to Myrror.
 
High Elf Ballista crews are highly skilled, refined over their long lives (+10% To-Hit), attuned to forests (Forester skill), and have higher resistance to poison and curses (+1 Resistance) compared to crews of other races.
#UA High Man Ballista
*Units\u218x3_1.png
 BALLISTA
The Ballista is a siege unit of a heavy mechanical bolt caster designed to launch javelin-sized bolts to pierce enemy armor from a distance. Widely used among races with advanced mechanical knowledge, it excels against heavily armored units but suffers from limited mobility. Originally invented by the ancient Xuanyuan, the Ballista spread to other civilized races after their exile to Myrror.
 
The High Man's skilled craftsmen make their artillery machines 15% cheaper, but their crews are superstitious and easy to fall victim to poison and magical effects (-1 Resistance) due to their ignorance toward the magical threats.
#UA Klackon Ballista
*Units\u218x3_1.png
 BALLISTA
The Ballista is a siege unit of a heavy mechanical bolt caster designed to launch javelin-sized bolts to pierce enemy armor from a distance. Widely used among races with advanced mechanical knowledge, it excels against heavily armored units but suffers from limited mobility. Originally invented by the ancient Xuanyuan, the Ballista spread to other civilized races after their exile to Myrror.
 
Klackon vessels and machines are sturdier (+2 Armor) thanks to their light but extremely durable carapace plating on the exterior.
#UA Nomad Ballista
*Units\u218x3_1.png
 BALLISTA
The Ballista is a siege unit of a heavy mechanical bolt caster designed to launch javelin-sized bolts to pierce enemy armor from a distance. Widely used among races with advanced mechanical knowledge, it excels against heavily armored units but suffers from limited mobility. Originally invented by the ancient Xuanyuan, the Ballista spread to other civilized races after their exile to Myrror.
 
Nomad Ballista crews are more proficient with logistics (+2 Ammo, +1 Overland Movement) and possess robust resistance against poison and magical effects (+3 Resistance) compared to crews of other races.
#UA Orc Ballista
*Units\u218x3_1.png
 BALLISTA
The Ballista is a siege unit of a heavy mechanical bolt caster designed to launch javelin-sized bolts to pierce enemy armor from a distance. Widely used among races with advanced mechanical knowledge, it excels against heavily armored units but suffers from limited mobility. Originally invented by the ancient Xuanyuan, the Ballista spread to other civilized races after their exile to Myrror.
 
Orc machine operating crews are highly valued and well-paid positions in Orc military, making them a sought-after role for well-to-do Orc families. Due to their place among Orc's high society, there is no problem for them to self preserving and perform tactical retreat in combat.
#UA Xuanyuan Ballista
*Units\u218x3_1.png
 BALLISTA
The Ballista is a siege unit of a heavy mechanical bolt caster designed to launch javelin-sized bolts to pierce enemy armor from a distance. Widely used among races with advanced mechanical knowledge, it excels against heavily armored units but suffers from limited mobility. Originally invented by the ancient Xuanyuan, the Ballista spread to other civilized races after their exile to Myrror.
 
Xuanyuan's artillery corps are known for have more crews in their unit as redundency spare (+5 Health) to compensate their poor battlefield protection (-1 Armor) compared to equivalent artillery corps of other races.
#UA Hawkman Ballista
*Units\u218x3_1.png
 BALLISTA
The Ballista is a siege unit of a heavy mechanical bolt caster designed to launch javelin-sized bolts to pierce enemy armor from a distance. Widely used among races with advanced mechanical knowledge, it excels against heavily armored units but suffers from limited mobility. Originally invented by the ancient Xuanyuan, the Ballista spread to other civilized races after their exile to Myrror.
 
Hawkman machine crews are experts in alpine warfare (Mountaineer skill) that enables them to perform better in mountainous environments compared to crews of other races.
#UA Goblin Ballistas
*Units\u218x3_1.png
 BALLISTAS
The Ballista is a siege unit of a heavy mechanical bolt caster designed to launch javelin-sized bolts to pierce enemy armor from a distance. Widely used among races with advanced mechanical knowledge, it excels against heavily armored units but suffers from limited mobility. Originally invented by the ancient Xuanyuan, the Ballista spread to other civilized races after their exile to Myrror.
 
Goblin Ballista teams operate more machines in each unit (+2 figures) but machine designs are smaller (-33% Attack strength) and disregard safety (-50% Health) and crews themselves also reckless (-10% To-Defend) compared to crews of other races.
#UA Settlers
*Units\u44x3_1.png
 SETTLERS
Settlers are the brave folk who set out onto new land to expand your empire by set up new outpost that could grow to become new town. To train a settler your town must have population at least 2000.
#UA Barbarian Settlers
*Units\u44x3_1.png
 SETTLERS
Settlers are the brave folk who set out onto new land to expand your empire by set up new outpost that could grow to become new town. To train a settler your town must have population at least 2000.
 
Barbarian Settlers are skilled in travel in wilderness (Pathfinding skill) compare to settlers of other races.

#UA Refugees
*Units\u53x3_1.png
 REFUGEES
Refugees are people who have lost their homes, have nowhere to return to, or are fleeing from conflict and seeking protection. Unlike settlers, they consist of the frail, the weak, the elderly, women, and children who cannot protect themselves and require the aid of a powerful wizard for protection. They need a new home to avoid their situation turning into a full-blown humanitarian crisis.
 
Refugees are unable to protect themselves, require more food, and move slower than settlers. Even roads do not help improve their travel speed, making their journey more difficult and perilous as they search for safety.
#UA Beastman Spearmen
*Units\u46x3_1.png
 SPEARMEN
The Spearmen battalion is a basic polearm infantry unit. Spearmen are cheap and easy to train. With polearm weapons, spearmen never fall victim to an enemy's First Strike in melee, making them essential for any fledgling army.
 
Beastman Spearmen are aggressive fighters (+1 Melee) and possess more robust endurance (+1 Health) compared to spearmen of other races.

*Units\u57x3_1.png
 SPEARMEN

#UA Orc Spearmen

 SPEARMEN

Orc Spearmen are poorly paid (if ever get paid at all) compared to spearmen of other races. Although their contracts promise a larger share of loot in Orc armies, often paid in slaves of the opposite sex, such income is never reliable.
#UA Troll Spearmen
*Units\u147x3_1.png
 SPEARMEN
The Spearmen battalion is a basic polearm infantry unit. Spearmen are cheap and easy to train. With polearm weapons, spearmen never fall victim to an enemy's First Strike in melee, making them essential for any fledgling army.
 
For other races, Troll Spearmen are not quite "Spearmen." While they might carry pointy sticks, their sheer brutality (+3 Melee), dumb toughness (+3 Health, +1 Resistance), and their ability to Regenerate set them apart. They are also expensive to train and maintain (+100% training cost, +1 gold Upkeep), despite their small number (-2 Figures).
#UA Rakhshasa Spearmen

Rakhshasa Spearmen are more nimble (+1 Armor, as speed is armor), capable of running very fast (+1 Movement), and are very much at home in the forest (Forester skill) compared to spearmen of other races.
#UA Hawkman Spearmen

 SPEARMEN

Hawkman Spearmen are innate flyers (Flying Movement) capable of reliably strike enemies in melee first before they can retaliate (First Strike skill). However, their battalion size is smaller (-1 Figure) compared to spearmen of other races.

Goblin Spearmen are recklessly disregarding their own safety (-10% To-Defend). They are more numerous (+2 Figures), and are able to bud their clone in combat compared to spearmen of other races.
#UA Beastman Halberdiers
*Units\u48x3_1.png
 HALBERDIERS
The Halberdiers battalion is an advanced polearm infantry unit with decent defense. Halberdiers are well-trained infantry capable of providing strong melee support. With polearm weapons, Halberdiers never fall victim to an enemy's First Strike in melee.
 
Beastman Halberdiers are aggressive fighters (+1 Melee) and possess more robust endurance (+1 Health) compared to halberdiers of other races.

 HALBERDIERS

Halberdiers are well-trained infantry capable of providing strong melee support. With polearm weapons, Halberdiers never fall victim to an enemy's First Strike in melee.
 
Dwarf Halberdiers possess robust endurance (+1 Health), strong resistance to poison and magical effects (+2 Resistance), and are skilled in mountain hiking (Mountaineer skill) compared to halberdiers of other races.

#UA Klackon Halberdiers
*Units\u116x3_1.png
 HALBERDIERS
Klackon Halberdiers are military units organized by bands of feral Klackons who do not serve any hive queen, based on their emulation of their non-hive mind neighbors. They can be found as mercenaries. Halberdiers are well-trained infantry capable of providing strong melee support. With polearm weapons, Halberdiers never fall victim to an enemy's First Strike in melee.
 
Klackon Halberdiers are sturdier (+2 Armor) compared to other races due to their heavy carapace.

 SWORDSMEN

Barbarian Swordsmen are skilled fighters (+10% To-Hit), capable of hurling axes or javelins before engaging in melee (+2 Thrown), and adept at wilderness travel (Pathfinding skill) compared to swordsmen of other races.

 SWORDSMEN
The Swordsmen battalion is a basic blade weapon infantry unit. Equipped with sword and shield, they bravely advance towards enemies despite projectile attacks. Swordsmen are disciplined soldiers and essential for any growing army.
 
Nomad Swordsmen are equipped with bows and arrows (+2 Missile Range Attack, +4 Ammo) and possess robust resistance against poison and magical effects (+3 Resistance) compared to swordsmen of other races.
#UA Orc Swordsmen
*Units\u138x3_1.png
 SWORDSMEN
The Swordsmen battalion is a basic blade weapon infantry unit. Equipped with sword and shield, they bravely advance towards enemies despite projectile attacks. Swordsmen are disciplined soldiers and essential for any growing army.
 
Orc Swordsmen are poorly paid (-1 gold Upkeep cost) compared to swordsmen of other races. Although their contracts promise a larger share of loot in Orc armies, often paid in slaves of the opposite sex, such income is never reliable.
#UA Troll Swordsmen
*Units\u148x3_1.png
 SWORDSMEN
The Swordsmen battalion is a basic blade weapon infantry unit equipped with swords and shields, advancing bravely toward enemies despite incoming projectiles. Swordsmen are the trained soldiers and essential units for any growing army.
 
For other races, Troll Swordsmen are not quite "Swordsmen." While they might wield long iron bars, their sheer brutality (+3 Melee), dumb toughness (+3 Health, +1 Resistance), and their ability to Regenerate set them apart. They are also expensive to train and maintain (+100% training cost, +1 gold Upkeep), despite their small number (-2 Figures).
#UA Xuanyuan Swordsmen
*Units\u289x3_1.png
 SWORDSMEN
The Swordsmen battalion is a basic blade weapon infantry unit equipped with swords and shields, advancing bravely toward enemies despite incoming projectiles. Swordsmen are the trained soldiers and essential units for any growing army.
 
Xuanyuan Swordsmen have more men in their battalion (+2 Figures) but are equipped with mass-produced armors that cuts corners in both quality and production processes (-1 Armor) compared to swordsmen of other races.
#UA Rakhshasa Swordsmen
*Units\u309x3_1.png
 SWORDSMEN
The Swordsmen battalion is a basic blade weapon infantry unit equipped with swords and shields, advancing bravely toward enemies despite incoming projectiles. Swordsmen are the trained soldiers and essential units for any growing army.
 
Rakhshasa Swordsmen are more nimble (+1 Armor, as speed is armor), capable of running very fast (+1 Movement), and are very much at home in the forest (Forester skill) compared to swordsmen of other races.
#UA Hawkman Swordsmen
*Units\u319x3_1.png
 SWORDSMEN
The Swordsmen battalion is a basic blade weapon infantry unit equipped with swords and shields, advancing bravely toward enemies despite incoming projectiles. Swordsmen are the trained soldiers and essential units for any growing army.
 
Hawkman Swordsmen are innate flyers (Flying Movement), capable of reliably striking enemies in melee first before they can retaliate (First strike skill). However, their battalion size is smaller (-1 Figure) compared to swordsmen of other races.
#UA Goblin Swordsmen
*Units\u347x3_1.png
 SWORDSMEN
The Swordsmen warband is a basic blade weapon infantry unit equipped with swords and shields, advancing bravely toward enemies despite incoming projectiles. Swordsmen are the trained soldiers and essential units for any growing army.
 
Goblin Swordsmen are recklessly disregarding their own safety (-10% To-Defend). They are more numerous (+2 Figures), and are able to bud their clone in combat compared to swordsmen of other races.
#UA Beastman Shieldbearers
*Units\u223x3_1.png
 SHIELDBEARERS
The Shieldbearers battalion is an advanced blade weapon infantry unit. Equipped with sword, armor, and shield, they advance swiftly towards enemies amid a hail of projectiles. Shieldbearers are well-trained soldiers capable of providing strong melee support.
 
Beastman Shieldbearers are aggressive fighters (+1 Melee) and possess more robust endurance (+1 Health) compared to shieldbearers of other races.
#UA Draconian Shieldbearers
*Units\u224x3_1.png
 SHIELDBEARERS
The Shieldbearers battalion is an advanced blade weapon infantry unit. Equipped with sword, armor, and shield, they advance swiftly towards enemies amid a hail of projectiles. Shieldbearers are well-trained soldiers capable of providing strong melee support.
 
Draconian Shieldbearers, due to their dragon blood, have the ability to fly, fire breath (+3 Fire Breath), dragon-like hide (+1 Armor), and increased magical resistance (+1 Resistance) compared to shieldbearers of other races.
#UA High Elf Shieldbearers
*Units\u225x3_1.png
 SHIELDBEARERS
The Shieldbearers battalion is an advanced blade weapon infantry unit. Equipped with sword, armor, and shield, they advance swiftly towards enemies amid a hail of projectiles. Shieldbearers are well-trained soldiers capable of providing strong melee support.
 
High Elf Shieldbearers are skilled fighters due to their immense experience gained over their long lives (+10% To-Hit), more attuned to forest environments (Forester skill) and possess more resistance to poison and magical effects (+1 Resistance) than shieldbearers of other races.

 SHIELDBEARERS

Lizardman Shieldbearers can move across water freely and possess more robust endurance (+1 Health) but weaker constitution against poison and magical effects (-1 Resistance) compared to shieldbearers of other races.

#UA Barbarian Bowmen
*Units\u41x3_1.png
 BOWMEN
The Bowmen battalion is a basic physical ranged infantry unit equipped with bows and arrows, trained to engage enemies from a distance. Their small-sized physical ammunition cannot penetrate units with Missile Immunity.
 
Barbarian Bowmen are skilled fighters (+10% To-Hit), capable of hurling axes or javelins before engaging in melee (+1 Thrown), and adept at wilderness travel (Pathfinding skill) compared to bowmen of other races.
#UA Beastman Bowmen
*Units\u49x3_1.png
 BOWMEN

#UA Draconian Bowmen
*Units\u69x3_1.png
 BOWMEN
The Bowmen battalion is a basic physical ranged infantry unit equipped with bows and arrows, trained to engage enemies from a distance. Their small-sized physical ammunition cannot penetrate units with Missile Immunity.
 
Draconian Bowmen, due to their dragon blood, have the ability to fly, possess fire breath (+1 Fire Breath), dragon-like hide (+1 Armor), and increased magical resistance (+1 Resistance). However, their flying ability limits their arrow supply (4 ammo) compared to bowmen of other races.

 BOWMEN

High Man Bowmen have larger battalions (+2 Figures) but lack resistance to poison and magical effects (-1 Resistance) compared to bowmen of other races due to their sedentary lifestyle and limited exposure to magical threats in High Man society.

#UA Beastman Crossbowmen
*Units\u241x3_1.png
 CROSSBOWMEN
Crossbowmen battalion is an advanced physical ranged infantry unit equipped with war crossbows and pavises, capable of firing powerful missiles with strong penetrating power from behind the protection of pavise. However, their small physical projectiles cannot penetrate units with Missile Immunity.
 
Beastman Crossbowmen are aggressive fighters (+1 Melee) and possess more robust endurance (+1 Health) compared to crossbowmen of other races.

However, their small physical projectiles cannot penetrate units with Missile Immunity.
 
Dwarf Crossbowmen possess robust endurance (+1 Health), strong resistance to poison and magical effects (+2 Resistance), and are skilled in mountain hiking (Mountaineer skill) compared to crossbowmen of other races.

#UA Barbarian Cavalry
*Units\u42x3_1.png
 CAVALRY
The Cavalry brigade is a basic mounted unit. Lightly armored and armed mostly with swords on their saddles, the cavalry's main strength lies in its mobility, allowing them to gain a significant advantage on the battlefield by striking first in melee before their opponents can react.
 
Barbarian Cavalrymen are skilled fighters (+10% To-Hit), capable of hurling axes or javelins before engaging in melee (+3 Thrown), and adept at wilderness travel (Pathfinding skill) compared to cavalrymen of other races.

#UA Barbarian Heavy Cavalry
*Units\u214x3_1.png
 HEAVY CAVALRY
The Heavy Cavalry brigade is an advanced mounted unit. Well-equipped with both weapons and armor on their saddles, the heavy cavalry is stronger than basic cavalry but slightly slower than lighter cavalry yet still faster than infantry, enabling them to gain a significant advantage on the battlefield by striking first in melee before their opponents can react.
 
Barbarian Heavy Cavalrymen are skilled fighters (+10% To-Hit), capable of hurling axes or javelins before engaging in melee (+4 Thrown), and adept at wilderness travel (Pathfinding skill) compared to heavy cavalrymen of other races.

#UA Barbarian Shamans
*Units\u43x3_1.png
 SHAMANS
The Shamans congregation is a basic clergy unit specializing in folk magic and rituals. Primarily wandering faith healers, they also serve as field medics, military chaplains, and even magical artillery if required. They can travel and pilgrimage freely without hindrance due to wizard's pact.
 
Barbarian Shamans are skilled fighters (+10% To-Hit), capable of hurling axes or javelins before engaging in melee (+1 Thrown), and adept at wilderness travel (Pathfinding skill) compared to shamans of other races.
#UA Halfling Shamans
*Units\u92x3_1.png

#UA Orc Shamans
*Units\u142x3_1.png
 SHAMANS
The Shamans congregation is a basic clergy unit specializing in folk magic and rituals. Primarily wandering faith healers, they also serve as field medics, military chaplains, and even magical artillery if required. They can travel and pilgrimage freely without hindrance due to wizard's pact.
 
Orc Shamans are "officially" poorly paid (-1 gold Upkeep cost) compared to shamans of other races. However, in reality, Orc Shamans are generally wealthy due to their side business of selling amulets and religious services to the general populace. There is no competition or regulation from dominant religions in Orc society, as the Orc priesthood is purely political.

#UA Beastman Monks
*Units\u50x3_1.png
 MONKS
The Monks congregation is a unit of lower rank clerics who study and train in monasteries. Unlike shamans, monks serve organized religions and rarely travel outside their monastery. They sometimes act as field medics, military chaplains, or even participate in war as magical artillery. They can travel and pilgrimage freely without hindrance due to wizard's pact.
 
Beastman Monks are aggressive fighters (+1 Melee) and possess more robust endurance (+1 Health) compared to monks of other races.

#UA Dark Elf Priests
*Units\u61x3_1.png
 PRIESTS
The Priests congregation is a unit of higher rank clerics who complete their ordainment to bridge mortals and deities through approval in temple sanctuaries. Priests bring divine protection to believers and guide them in peace and war. Priests are allowed to travel and pilgrimage freely without hindrance due to wizard's pact.
 
Dark Elf Priests possess greater proficiency in arcane arts (+2 Magical Range Attack) and strong resistance to poison and magical effects (+2 Resistance) compared to priests of other races.

#UA Beastman Disciples
*Units\u51x3_1.png
 DISCIPLES
The Disciples battalion is a lower rank magician unit. The study of magic needs to begin somewhere, usually as a student apprentice under the tutorship of one or several magisters, proper magicians, with graduates earning the title "disciple". Institutions like the Sage's Guild make it easier to train many disciples to serve as magical artillery and cast basic spells on the battlefield.
 
Beastman Disciples are aggressive fighters (+1 Melee) and possess more robust endurance (+1 Health) compared to disciples of other races.

 DISCIPLES
The Disciples battalion is a lower rank magician unit. The study of magic needs to begin somewhere, usually as a student apprentice under the tutorship of one or several magisters, proper magicians, with graduates earning the title "disciple". Institutions like the Sage's Guild make it easier to train many disciples to serve as magical artillery and cast basic spells on the battlefield.
 
Nomad Disciples possess robust resistance against poison and magical effects (+3 Resistance) compared to disciples of other races.
#UA Orc Disciples
*Units\u240x3_1.png
 DISCIPLES
The Disciples battalion is a lower rank magician unit. The study of magic needs to begin somewhere, usually as a student apprentice under the tutorship of one or several magisters, proper magicians, with graduates earning the title "disciple". Institutions like the Sage's Guild make it easier to train many disciples to serve as magical artillery and cast basic spells on the battlefield.
 
Orc Disciples are poorly paid (-1 gold Upkeep cost) compared to disciples of other races, as part of their wages are mandated by law to be transferred to the institution that taught them.
#UA Beastman Magisters
*Units\u234x3_1.png
 MAGISTERS
The Magisters battalion is a higher rank magician unit. Not all graduated disciples can become Master Wizards, but they can aspire to become Magisters. Magisters are magicians who have proven their worth to Wizard's Guilds with strong spell power and spell casting ability. They often work as academics or operate their own workshops, but many also serve in the army as magical artillery and support casters of intermediate spells on the battlefield.
 
Beastman Magisters are aggressive fighters (+1 Melee) and possess more robust endurance (+1 Health) compared to magisters of other races.
#UA Draconian Magisters
*Units\u71x3_1.png
 MAGISTERS
The Magisters battalion is a higher rank magician unit. Magisters are magicians who have proven their worth to Wizard's Guilds with strong spell power and spell casting ability. They often work as academics or operate their own workshops, but many also serve in the army as magical artillery and support casters of intermediate spells on the battlefield.
 
Draconian Magisters, due to their dragon blood, have the ability to fly, fire breath (+2 Fire Breath), dragon-like hide (+1 Armor), and increased magical resistance (+1 Resistance) compared to magisters of other races.
#UA Halfling Magisters
*Units\u91x3_1.png
 MAGISTERS
The Magisters battalion is a higher rank magician unit. Magisters are magicians who have proven their worth to Wizard's Guilds with strong spell power and spell casting ability. They often work as academics or operate their own workshops, but many also serve in the army as magical artillery and support casters of intermediate spells on the battlefield.
 
Halfling Magisters lack ferocity (-1 Melee), but possess extraordinary luck (Lucky perk) compared to magisters of other races.
#UA High Man Magisters
*Units\u109x3_1.png
 MAGISTERS
The Magisters battalion is a higher rank magician unit. Magisters are magicians who have proven their worth to Wizard's Guilds with strong spell power and spell casting ability. They often work as academics or operate their own workshops, but many also serve in the army as magical artillery and support casters of intermediate spells on the battlefield.
 
High Man Magisters have larger battalions (+2 Figures) but lack resistance to poison and magical effects (-1 Resistance) compared to magisters of other races due to their sedentary lifestyle and limited exposure to magical threats in High Man society.

They often work as academics or operate their own workshops, but many also serve in the army as magical artillery and support casters of intermediate spells on the battlefield.
 
Nomad Magisters possess robust resistance against poison and magical effects (+3 Resistance) compared to magisters of other races.
#UA Orc Magisters

 MAGISTERS

They often work as academics or operate their own workshops, but many also serve in the army as magical artillery and support casters of intermediate spells on the battlefield.
