#UA Beastman Engineers
*Units\u52x3_1.png
 ENGINEERS
Engineers are non-combatant specialists trained to build roads and aid in toppling enemy walls. They can move freely in opponent wizard's territory with whom you have a Wizard's Pact.
 
Beastman Engineers are aggressive fighters (+1 Melee) and possess more robust endurance (+1 Health) than engineers of other races.
#UA High Man Engineers
*Units\u110x3_1.png
 ENGINEERS
Engineers are non-combatant specialists trained to build roads and aid in toppling enemy walls. They can move freely in opponent wizard's territory with whom you have a Wizard's Pact.
 
High Man Engineers have larger battalions (+2 Figures) but lack resistance to poison and magical effects (-1 Resistance) compared to engineers of other races due to their sedentary lifestyle and limited exposure to magical threats in High Man society.
#UA Klackon Engineers
*Units\u117x3_1.png
 ENGINEERS
Engineers are non-combatant specialists trained to build roads and aid in toppling enemy walls. They can move freely in opponent wizard's territory with whom you have a Wizard's Pact.
 
Klackon Engineers are sturdier (+2 Armor) compared to other races thanks to their heavy carapace and build roads twice as fast as engineers of other races due to their deep connection to the hive mind.
#UA Orc Engineers
*Units\u144x3_1.png
 ENGINEERS
Engineers are non-combatant specialists trained to build roads and aid in toppling enemy walls. They can move freely in opponent wizard's territory with whom you have a Wizard's Pact.
 
Orc Engineers are poorly paid (-1 gold Upkeep cost) compared to engineers of other races due to intense competition for civil engineering jobs from Orc universities.
#UA Xuanyuan Engineers
*Units\u292x3_1.png
 ENGINEERS
Engineers are non-combatant specialists trained to build roads and aid in toppling enemy walls. They can move freely in opponent wizard's territory with whom you have a Wizard's Pact.
 
Xuanyuan Engineers have more men in their battalion (+2 Figures) but are equipped with mass-produced armors that cuts corners in both quality and production processes (-1 Armor) compared to engineers of other races.
#UA Dark Elf Pioneers
*Units\u265x3_1.png
 PIONEERS
Pioneers are non-combatant volunteers trained to explore and clear paths for others. They may not build roads as fast as proper engineers but are skilled in certain situations. They can move freely in opponent wizard's territory with whom you have a Wizard's Pact.
 
Dark Elf Pioneers use magic to protect themselves in the wilderness (+1 Magical Range Attack, +4 Ammo) and possess strong resistance to poison and magical effects (+2 Resistance) compared to pioneers of other races.
#UA High Elf Pioneers
*Units\u266x3_1.png
 PIONEERS
Pioneers are non-combatant volunteers trained to explore and clear paths for others. They may not build roads as fast as proper engineers but are skilled in certain situations. They can move freely in opponent wizard's territory with whom you have a Wizard's Pact.
 
High Elf Pioneers are equipped with bows to protect themselves (+1 Missile Range Attack, +4 Ammo), are skillful fighters (+10% To-Hit), more attuned to forest environments (Forester skill), and possess more resistance to poison and magical effects (+1 Resistance) than pioneers of other races.
#UA Halfling Pioneers
*Units\u267x3_1.png
 PIONEERS
Pioneers are non-combatant volunteers trained to explore and clear paths for others. They may not build roads as fast as proper engineers but are skilled in certain situations. They can move freely in opponent wizard's territory with whom you have a Wizard's Pact.
 
Halfling Pioneers are equipped with slings and stones for protection in the wilderness (+1 Missile Range Attack, +4 Ammo), have more men in each battalion (+2 Figures), and possess extraordinary luck (Lucky perk) compared to pioneers of other races.
#UA Nomad Pioneers
*Units\u268x3_1.png
 PIONEERS
Pioneers are non-combatant volunteers trained to explore and clear paths for others. They may not build roads as fast as proper engineers but are skilled in certain situations. They can move freely in opponent wizard's territory with whom you have a Wizard's Pact.
 
Nomad Pioneers are equipped with bows and arrows for protection in the wilderness (+1 Missile Range Attack, +4 Ammo) and possess robust resistance against poison and magical effects (+3 Resistance) compared to pioneers of other races.
#UA Barbarian Berserkers
*Units\u45x3_1.png
 BERSERKERS
The Berserkers warband is a special barbarian melee unit. Barbarian blood runs hot and wild, and the berserkers tap into the blood rage, channeling it in battle. Friend or foe, all should fear them, for their ferocity and relentless fury make them unstoppable on the battlefield.
#UA Barbarian Gladiators
*Units\u87x3_1.png
 GLADIATORS
The Gladiators warband is a special barbarian melee unit. Gladiators are champions among the barbarians, standing tall in savage fights and holding their own against waves of enemies and showers of arrows. Their strength, resilience, and prowess in battle make them formidable adversaries, inspiring fear and respect in all who face them.
#UA Barbarian Spellserkers
*Units\u93x3_1.png
 SPELLSERKERS
The Spellserkers warband is a special barbarian melee/magician unit. Spellserkers are warrior-poets who weave spells as skillfully as they wield blades. They use their arcane power to protect themselves from small, underhanded projectiles, allowing them to fight and cast spells without interruption. Their unique blend of magic and martial prowess makes them both fearsome in close combat and formidable spellcasters on the battlefield.
#UA Barbarian Longships
*Units\u256x3_1.png
 LONGSHIPS
The Longships squadron is a special barbarian naval unit. Longships enable barbarians to dominate the savage seas. Their speed allows barbarian warriors to raid and battle across vast distances. When one longship is sighted, another is likely nearby. By the time anyone sees a Longship, it's often too late to flee, as the barbarians strike quickly and fiercely, leaving little time for defense.
#UA Beastman Centaurs
*Units\u54x3_1.png
 CENTAURS
The Centaurs battalion is a special Beastmen unit, both ranged and melee mounted. Beastmen who undergo artificial mutation transform into a form with the body of a bull and a humanoid upper body through a secret method. Once transformed, Centaurs are trained to utilize their new form to its fullest potential. They are exceptionally fast and proficient in both ranged and close combat. Once a Beastman undergoes the Centaur transformation, they cannot revert to their original bipedal humanoid form, embracing their new form as a powerful warrior on both land and battlefield.
#UA Beastman Minotaurs
*Units\u56x3_1.png
 MINOTAURS
The Minotaurs squadron is a special Beastmen elite melee infantry unit. Minotaurs embody bestial rage incarnate, transformed from Beastmen through a secret method involving the implantation of magical ore into their bodies. More beast than man, Minotaurs grow larger, stronger, and more aggressive. They are consumed by barely controllable rage and can withstand significant punishment before being brought down. Beastmen who transform into Minotaurs can gradually revert to their original form after the implanted magical ore is removed, though the transformation often leaves them with lingering echoes of their beastly nature.
#UA Beastman Gugalannas
*Units\u250x3_1.png
 GUGALANNAS
The Gugalannas squadron is a special Beastmen flying unit. Gugalannas, the bulls of heaven, are sentient bull-like beings among the Beastmen. They possess petrifying breath and the ability to fly. Gugalannas are believed to be the progenitor form of the Beastmen and are considered sacred within their society. Not all Beastmen can mutate into Gugalannas, and irreversible transformation into a Gugalanna is regarded as the greatest honor for a Beastman, marking them as revered warriors with unmatched power and prestige.
#UA Beastman Chironean Guards
*Units\u254x3_1.png
 CHIRONEAN GUARDS
The Chironean Guards battalion is a special Beastmen elite ranged and melee mounted unit. Chironean Guards are the elite among the Centaurs, selected from the finest and equipped with specially designed armor for their half-beast forms. The unit is named after Chiron the Sagittarius, the most honored Beastman warrior, who founded it and remains its greatest captain. Their skill in both ranged and melee combat, combined with their elite training and armor, makes them a fearsome force on the battlefield.
#UA Dark Elf Adepts
*Units\u62x3_1.png
 ADEPTS
The Adepts battalion is a special Dark Elf lower rank magician unit. While there is no official title of "Adept" among Dark Elves, outsiders use this term to refer to magicians who are on par with magisters but for various reasons do not hold that title. Due to the Dark Elves' natural affinity with arcane arts, most Dark Elf disciples possess skills comparable to magisters of other races, leading to them being colloquially called "Adepts" by outsiders. Despite their unofficial title, these Adepts are powerful spellcasters, capable of wielding potent magic on the battlefield.
#UA Dark Elf Nightblades
*Units\u63x3_1.png
 NIGHTBLADES
The Nightblades battalion is a special Dark Elf elite melee unit. Nightblades are enigmatic assassins among the Dark Elves, wielding poisoned blades and operating under a strict code of secrecy. They specialize in espionage, infiltration, and assassination both on and off the battlefield. The origins of the Nightblades are shrouded in mystery, but their existence seems to coincide with the arrival of the Xuanyuan people on Myrror, possibly learning martial arts from them or countering the perceived threat they posed. Their deadly precision and stealth make them formidable opponents in any covert operation.
#UA Dark Elf Warlocks
*Units\u64x3_1.png
 WARLOCKS
The Warlocks battalion is a special Dark Elf higher rank magician unit. Ancient Elves, driven by their thirst for power and hubris, discovered dark arts that granted them immense magical power at a great cost. This discovery led to a civil war between those who embraced these dark powers (the Dark) and those who opposed them (the High). While most modern Dark Elves cautiously dabble in these arts, Warlocks delve deepest, paying a great price to their bodies and souls for their mastery. Their powerful, forbidden magic makes them fearsome allies and dangerous foes, capable of wielding destructive forces at a great personal cost.
#UA Dark Elf Nightmares
*Units\u65x3_1.png
 NIGHTMARES
The Nightmares squadron is a special Dark Elf flying mounted unit. Nightmares are jet-black horse-like creatures that soar through the night sky, consuming the hopes and dreams of their victims, leaving only terror and despair behind. Riding a Nightmare requires extensive training and mastery of the arcane arts. Once bonded, the rider and Nightmare become one, granting the rider the ability to strike at enemies from their dreams, whether awake or asleep. Their fearsome presence in the sky is a harbinger of dread, capable of unsettling even the bravest of foes.
#UA Dark Elf Magic Knights
*Units\u249x3_1.png
 MAGIC KNIGHTS
The Magic Knights battalion is a special Dark Elf advanced mounted unit. Magic Knights are warriors adept in both magic and swordsmanship. They wear enchanted armor that enhances their magical abilities without hindering their combat prowess, wielding swords that double as wands. Their steeds are specially trained to withstand the dazzling magic they unleash, allowing these knights to strike with both blade and spell. Their combination of martial skill and arcane power makes them formidable opponents on the battlefield.
#UA Draconian Saints
*Units\u70x3_1.png
 SAINTS
The Saints congregation is a special Draconian cleric unit. Saints are Draconians chosen by "the One" to protect others from worldly and spiritual threats. They perform miracles like magic without using arcane arts. Their main power, the Miracle of Dragonheart, inspires believers to push their limits and grow stronger. The Saints act as protectors and symbols of faith, using divine power to uplift and defend others.
 
Draconians are a unique race among the followers of "the One," a deity who saved them from Chaos corruption. The awakening of Saints is seen as a divine blessing from their god, highlighting the Draconians' special role in protecting and guiding others.
#UA Draconian Doom Drakes
*Units\u74x3_1.png
 DOOM DRAKES
The Doom Drakes squadron is a special Draconian flying mounted unit. Doom Drakes are the last tamable drakes on Myrror, domesticated by Draconians who share a kinship with them due to their shared draconic blood. Though smaller than the wild drakes of the planes of magic, Doom Drakes still breathe fire and strike fear into their foes.
#UA Draconian Air Ship
*Units\u75x3_1.png
 AIR SHIP
The Air Ship is a special Draconian siege unit. A secretive innovation, the Air Ship is unmatched by any other civilization for achieving flight without relying on powerful magic. Armed with artillery, Air Ships act as mobile siege platforms, bombarding enemies from the skies. However, their reliance on non-magical flight limits their size, preventing them from serving as large-scale transports for armies.
The Air Ship is counted as ship and could only launch from the city tile or water tile closed to the city.
#UA Dwarf Combat Engineers
*Units\u78x3_1.png
 COMBAT ENGINEERS
The Combat Engineers battalion is a special Dwarf siege unit. Renowned for their expertise in siegecraft and engineering, Dwarves equip mortars capable of breaking enemy walls from a safe distance and handle alchemical fires with great skill. Their proficiency in military engineering and dangerous substances makes them invaluable in battle, though their specialized nature prevents them from freely traveling under Wizard's Pacts.
#UA Dwarf Hammerhands
*Units\u79x3_1.png
 HAMMERHANDS
The Hammerhands battalion is a special Dwarf advanced melee unit. Historically serving as vanguard warriors and war engineers before the age of gunpowder, Hammerhands excel at scaling enemy walls and clearing the way for fellow Dwarven warriors. In times of peace, their hammers are used to forge paths through mountains for commerce and transportation, showcasing their dual role as both formidable fighters and skilled engineers.
#UA Dwarf Steam Cannon
*Units\u80x3_1.png
 STEAM CANNON
The Steam Cannon is a special Dwarf siege unit. A proud innovation of Dwarven engineering, this heavy siege machine delivers powerful, precise bombardments over long distances. Mastery of the Steam Cannon is a key achievement for Dwarf engineers seeking recognition, though its stationary nature limits its mobility on the battlefield.
#UA Dwarf Golem
*Units\u81x3_1.png
 GOLEM
The Golem is a special Dwarf elite melee unit. These towering humanoid automata, crafted in imitation of legendary colossi, are impervious to fire and many magical effects. Golems are both fast and unwaveringly loyal, embodying the pinnacle of Dwarven craftsmanship and resilience on the battlefield.
#UA Dwarf Steam Tank
*Units\u202x3_1.png
 STEAM TANK
The Steam Tank is a special Dwarf siege unit. The pinnacle of Dwarven siege weaponry, it is armed with heavy steam mortars, flamethrowers, and thick armor, all powered by advanced steam engines. The Steam Tank strikes fear into enemies as it rolls inexorably across the battlefield, its powerful arsenal and resilience making it a formidable force in any siege.
#UA Dwarf Huskarls
*Units\u245x3_1.png
 HUSKARLS
The Huskarls battalion is a special Dwarf elite melee unit. Famed for their unbreakable resolve, formidable strength, and heavy armor, they wield specially forged axes capable of cleaving through steel. Huskarls are slow but unstoppable juggernauts on the battlefield, their sheer resilience and power making them a terrifying force in close combat.
#UA Dwarf Arquebusiers
*Units\u246x3_1.png
 ARQUEBUSIERS
The Arquebusiers battalion is a special Dwarf advanced firearms unit. Armed with handheld arquebuses, these weapons generate smoke and thunder, instilling fear in foes and delivering strong volleys at close range. Arquebusiers are proficient at defending against charges and engaging flying enemies, representing a newer and easier-to-train firearm technology for Dwarves.
#UA Dwarf Musketeers
*Units\u247x3_1.png
 MUSKETEERS
The Musketeers battalion is a special Dwarf elite firearms unit. Equipped with rifle muskets and bayonets, these muskets are more accurate than arquebuses and can deliver sustained volleys at range or in close combat. Thunderous musket fire strikes fear into enemies and provides versatile capabilities against both ground and aerial threats, making the Musketeers a powerful force on the battlefield.
#UA Gnoll Jackal Riders
*Units\u86x3_1.png
 JACKAL RIDERS
The Jackal Riders warband is a special Gnoll elite melee mounted unit. Trained at the Gnoll war college, these riders charge into battle atop jackals. While not as strong or fast as wolf riders' mounts, jackals are magically enchanted by Gnoll witchdoctors to induce fear in their opponents. Jackal Riders excel in traversing rough terrain and overwhelming enemies with their sheer numbers, making them a formidable force on the battlefield.
#UA Gnoll Wolf Riders
*Units\u88x3_1.png
 WOLF RIDERS
The Wolf Riders warband is a special Gnoll basic melee mounted unit. Mounted on wargs, a larger species of dire wolves known for their fierceness and tracking ability, Wolf Riders are among the fastest mounted units. They excel at maneuvering across various terrains and chasing down enemies without losing speed, making them highly effective in both pursuit and skirmishing.
#UA Gnoll Witchdoctors
*Units\u203x3_1.png
 WITCHDOCTORS
The Witchdoctors congregation is a special Gnoll lower rank magician unit. In Gnoll society, Witchdoctors act as mediators between the physical and spiritual realms, revered for their ability to commune with spirits and cast curses. Trained from a young age, they wield mystical powers to influence battles and uphold Gnoll traditions of spiritualism and magic, serving as both spiritual leaders and powerful magic users.
 
Witchdoctors are responsible for the prevalence of hexes in Gnoll society. Trained in the art of cursing, they use these powerful hexes without hesitation against their enemies.
#UA Gnoll Hunters
*Units\u210x3_1.png
 HUNTERS
The Hunters warband is a special Gnoll basic physical ranged infantry unit. Renowned for their tracking and archery skills, most Gnolls are expert hunters who excel at moving quickly across rough terrain. They are particularly adept at bringing down flying creatures before they can engage in melee combat.
#UA Gnoll Marauders
*Units\u222x3_1.png
 MARAUDERS
The Marauders warband is a special Gnoll advanced blade infantry unit. Embodying Gnoll warrior culture, Marauders are esteemed for their prowess in raiding neighboring communities for resources and glory. Those who prove themselves in battle earn the prestigious title of Marauder, the highest honor among Gnoll warriors, whether in times of peace or war.
#UA Halfling Slingers
*Units\u94x3_1.png
 SLINGERS
The Slingers battalion is a special Halfling advanced physical ranged infantry unit. Halflings are highly skilled with slings, capable of toppling giants under the right circumstances. Slingers are nimble skirmishers who can outrun enemies while maintaining distance to hurl projectiles. Their sling bullets are effective against most foes, though they cannot harm units with Missile Immunity.
#UA Halfling Scouts
*Units\u206x3_1.png
 SCOUTS
The Scouts battalion is a special Halfling basic mounted unit. Halflings, known for their pacifism, curiosity, and intrepid nature, ride ponies as light cavalry, adept at quietly traversing enemy territory. They specialize in exploring ruins and uncovering detailed information about monsters and their lairs.
#UA Halfling Rocs
*Units\u221x3_1.png
 ROCS
The Rocs squadron is a special Halfling flying mounted unit. Rocs are gigantic eagles that have formed bonds of friendship with Halflings. They soar high above the battlefield, beyond the reach of arrows and bullets, unmatched in aerial speed. Halflings view Rocs not merely as pets but as sentient beings, though their attempts to convince other races of this have met with limited success.
#UA High Elf Druids
*Units\u99x3_1.png
 DRUIDS
The Druids congregation is a special High Elf higher rank magician unit. Druids commune with nature, using their knowledge to purify the land and heal the sick. Unlike other races, High Elves do not have a priestly order, believing they do not need mediators between themselves and the "Power that Be."
#UA High Elf Longbowmen
*Units\u101x3_1.png
 LONGBOWMEN
The Longbowmen battalion is a special High Elf advanced physical ranged infantry unit. Renowned for their agility and mastery of archery, High Elf Longbowmen use specially designed longbows for stronger and longer-range shots with relatively less pull strength. Their skill, honed over centuries, makes their impressive abilities seem effortless.
#UA High Elf Elven Lords
*Units\u102x3_1.png
 ELVEN LORDS
The Elven Lords battalion is a special High Elf elite mounted unit. Clad in elegant armor and wielding the finest weapons, Elven Lords ride forest war horses well-suited to woodland environments. Despite their seemingly frail appearance, they are formidable in battle, unmatched in riding and combat due to centuries of experience and wisdom.
#UA High Elf Pegasus Riders
*Units\u103x3_1.png
 PEGASUS RIDERS
The Pegasus Riders battalion is a special High Elf flying mounted unit. Pegasi, known as heavenly horses by other Arcanian races, are flying equine creatures with long lifespans. Bonding with a Pegasus takes nearly a decade, making it impractical for other races. High Elves, with their skill, wisdom, and patience, are granted the rare opportunity to become Pegasus riders. This elite unit excels in ranged combat, melee, and scouting.
#UA High Elf Rangers
*Units\u135x3_1.png
 RANGERS
The Rangers battalion is a special High Elf elite physical ranged infantry unit. Unlike most High Elves, who are skilled fighters but not professional soldiers, Rangers are both agile and strong. They are fierce in melee combat and excellent archers. In peacetime, they patrol the wilderness and quietly handle threats. In wartime, they serve as scouts and fight on the frontlines and behind enemy lines. Their camouflage skills are often believed to be magical by lesser races, though they are simply highly trained techniques that can be learned in under a decade.
#UA High Man Crusaders
*Units\u111x3_1.png
 CRUSADERS
The Crusaders battalion is a special High Man elite blade weapon infantry unit. These warriors dedicate their martial skills to the cause of the High Man's church, receiving baptism and wearing blessed equipment. While lacking formal clerical training, their faith empowers them to protect the faithful, granting them a form of miracle armor.
#UA High Man Pikemen
*Units\u112x3_1.png
 PIKEMEN
The Pikemen battalion is a special High Man advanced polearm infantry unit. Known for their tight formations and excellent drilling, Pikemen wield longer pikes to pierce enemy armor. They excel at holding the line against charges, turning the tide of battle with their disciplined formations and formidable weapons.
#UA High Man Paladins
*Units\u113x3_1.png
 PALADINS
The Paladins battalion is a special High Man elite mounted unit. Trained from a young age by the High Man's church, their training includes both chivalric and warfare skills, along with clerical education. Only a few are ordained and recognized as Paladins, as they are able to bestow blessings upon those in need. Known for their impeccable honor and bravery, the Paladins' devotion grants them both protection and strength in battle.
#UA High Man Knights
*Units\u118x3_1.png
 KNIGHTS
The Knights battalion is a special High Man advanced mounted unit. Hailing from the landowning class, Knights embody chivalric ideals and excel in heavy cavalry tactics. Armed with shields to deflect missiles, they charge into combat swiftly, using their jousting skills to strike down enemies before they can mount a defense.
#UA High Man Squires
*Units\u212x3_1.png
 SQUIRES
The Squires battalion is a special High Man advanced blade weapon infantry unit. Not all landed gentries become knights immediately; those who train to be knights or have not yet achieved that status serve as squires. They are well-equipped, disciplined soldiers who fight as heavy infantry to support knights. Squires also act as shield and armor bearers and perform other tasks for the knights.
#UA High Man Inquisitors
*Units\u231x3_1.png
 INQUISITORS
The Inquisitors congregation is a special High Man higher rank cleric unit. Formed to combat heresies and supernatural threats, the Inquisitors are skilled in rooting out heresies and fighting Fantastic creatures. They use attack magic to exorcise undead and banish otherworldly beings. However, their zealous nature makes them unwelcome in foreign lands.
#UA Klackon Stag Beetle
*Units\u119x3_1.png
 STAG BEETLE
The Stag Beetle is a special Klackon elite mounted unit, named after a large insect. Despite its size, the Stag Beetle is fast and can breathe powerful flames, making it a formidable fighter. These giant creatures, exclusive to Klackon control, are thought to be linked to the Klackon hive mind.
#UA Klackon Antlions
*Units\u204x3_1.png
 ANTLIONS
The Antlions battalion is a special Klackon advanced mounted unit, named after a natural insect but much larger. Unlike their smaller counterparts, these giant Antlions can merge into the ground and appear unexpectedly, giving them a strategic advantage to surprise and flank enemies.
#UA Klackon Maiden Queens
*Units\u205x3_1.png
 MAIDEN QUEENS
The Maiden Queens battalion is a special Klackon higher rank magician unit. Unlike most Klackons, Maiden Queens, who are capable of flight and magic, serve as key leaders. They provide magical support and strengthen the hive mind bond among all creatures on their side. It is rumored that only the strongest Maiden Queens, able to form hive minds with non-Klackons, become Hive Queens.
#UA Klackon Mantises
*Units\u220x3_1.png
 MANTISES
The Mantises battalion is a special Klackon advanced blade infantry unit. In Klackon society, roles are assigned at birth, but only the most skilled warriors can become Mantises. These warriors use sharp reflexes and blade arms to quickly defeat enemies in the toughest battles for the hive mind.
#UA Klackon Stingers
*Units\u255x3_1.png
 STINGERS
The Stingers battalion is a special Klackon advanced polearm infantry unit. While similar to earlier warrior forms, Stingers are distinguished by their developed stinger tails, which carry potent poison for both offense and defense.
#UA Lizardman Carrack
*Units\u39x3_1.png
 CARRACK
The Carrack is a special Lizardman naval unit, featuring an oarless ship design made for Lizardman use. Built to navigate the high seas efficiently, Carracks harness wind and water currents effectively. These ships can also be beached and maintained by Lizardmen without the need for traditional shipyards.
#UA Lizardman Marines
*Units\u122x3_1.png
 MARINES
The Marines battalion is a special Lizardman advanced polearm infantry unit, renowned for their expertise in naval warfare. Lizardmen, skilled swimmers with a strong affinity for the sea, excel in disciplined combat, holding lines and striking unexpectedly. Their ability to swim swiftly and dive deep into the sea makes them impervious to fire during naval engagements.
#UA Lizardman Javelineers
*Units\u123x3_1.png
 JAVELINEERS
The Javelineers battalion is a special Lizardman advanced melee-physical ranged infantry unit. Javelins are revered as totem weapons in Lizardman culture, used in both tribal warfare and festival competitions. Javelineers are versatile warriors skilled in both melee combat and ranged attacks. They excel in hit-and-run tactics, using their ability to maintain distance while throwing missiles at their enemies.
#UA Lizardman Dragon Turtle
*Units\u126x3_1.png
 DRAGON TURTLE
The Dragon Turtle is a special Lizardman elite mounted unit, a fearsome secret weapon. These massive creatures, ridden exclusively by Lizardmen, are known for their tough skin, powerful melee attacks, and ability to breathe lightning. Resistant to fire, poison, and magic, Dragon Turtles are formidable on both land and sea, making them invaluable assets in Lizardman warfare.
#UA Lizardman Sea Hags
*Units\u207x3_1.png
 SEA HAGS
The Sea Hags battalion is a special Lizardman melee/magician unit. Despite their repulsive appearance, Sea Hags are revered as elderly Lizardman witches. Their arcane abilities are honed through deep-sea channeling, enhancing their physical and mental prowess. Sea Hags induce terror and madness in enemies, using venomous attacks and excelling in sea combat.
#UA Lizardman Reptile Riders
*Units\u219x3_1.png
 REPTILE RIDERS
The Reptile Riders battalion is a special Lizardman basic mounted unit. Originally limited to desert Lizardman tribes battling nomads, these reptiles are fast runners but cannot swim, restricting their use. However, the advent of the Carrack design allowed for their spread across Lizardman territories. Reptile riding has since become a common practice among upper-class Lizardmen.
#UA Nomad Horsebowmen
*Units\u133x3_1.png
 HORSEBOWMEN
The Horsebowmen battalion is a special Nomad basic mounted ranged unit. Skilled in horseback archery, they excel at hit-and-run tactics, outrunning enemies while firing arrows. Lightly equipped, they avoid melee combat, relying on speed and ranged attacks. Their arrows are effective against most foes but cannot penetrate missile immunity.
#UA Nomad Kardakes
*Units\u134x3_1.png
 KARDAKES
The Kardakes battalion is a special Nomad advanced polearm/ranged infantry unit. Trained as professional soldiers, they use hook spears and composite bows to pierce enemy armor and disrupt cavalry charges. However, their arrows are limited in number due to specialized piercing tips and cannot penetrate missile immunity.
#UA Nomad Griffin Riders
*Units\u136x3_1.png
 GRIFFIN RIDERS
The Griffin Riders squadron is a special Nomad flying mounted unit. Bonded with powerful griffins, half-lion and half-eagle, they offer unmatched speed and ferocity in combat. However, their wild nature makes them difficult to control, leaving Griffin Riders vulnerable to magical attacks despite their aerial advantage.
#UA Nomad Cataphracts
*Units\u201x3_1.png
 CATAPHRACTS
The Cataphracts battalion is a special Nomad elite mounted unit. Clad in heavy armor, they wield lances and composite bows, excelling in both ranged and melee combat. They use their bows effectively before engaging in close combat. Their versatility makes them formidable against all enemies, including flying foes, but their arrows cannot breach Missile Immunity.
#UA Nomad Sipahis
*Units\u213x3_1.png
 SIPAHIS
The Sipahis battalion is a special Nomad advanced mounted unit. Known as the backbone of the nomad army, Sipahis are armed with spears and bows, excelling in both melee and ranged combat. Their mobility and endurance allow them to engage flying enemies effectively while charging. However, like other Nomad units, their arrows cannot pierce Missile Immunity.
#UA Nomad Dervishes
*Units\u332x3_1.png
 Dervishes
The Dervishes congregation is a special Nomad lower-rank cleric unit. Ascetics of the desert, they train their spirits for communion with the gods. Skilled in tracking and wilderness travel, they guide lost travelers and help those struggling spiritually. In peacetime, they are helpful and often welcomed in foreign lands.
#UA Orc Hoplites
*Units\u72x3_1.png
 HOPLITES
The Hoplites battalion is a special Orc advanced polearm infantry unit. These heavily equipped militia come from the Orc slave-owning class, known for their quality gear and self-sufficiency. United by the need to protect their properties, they fight with disciplined ferocity in tight formations. However, their comfort and lack of hardship make them vulnerable to poison and curses.
#UA Orc Legionary
*Units\u139x3_1.png
 LEGIONARY
The Legionary cohort is a special Orc elite blade weapon infantry unit. Recruited from impoverished Orc bachelors, Legionaries undergo rigorous training, with promises of land, food, and a wife upon honorable discharge. They excel in methodical military tactics, capable of bringing down flying enemies, breaching fortifications, and providing medical aid after battle. Life as a Legionary is demanding and filled with responsibilities.
#UA Orc Wyvern Riders
*Units\u146x3_1.png
 WYVERN RIDERS
The Wyvern Riders squadron is a special Orc flying mounted unit. Mounted on venomous wyverns, these riders strike with deadly precision from the air. The wyverns' venomous attacks quickly incapacitate enemies, while Orcs use venom-coated weapons to ensure swift deaths for their foes. This mastery of taming wyverns allows them to rest while their enemies are permanently defeated.
#UA Troll Chieftains
*Units\u129x3_1.png
 CHIEFTAINS
The Chieftains warband is a special Troll elite support infantry unit. Troll society is held together by the efforts of these chieftains, who act as mediators between factions. When conflicts arise, chieftains step in to restore order and enforce discipline.
 
Trolls don't view death as humans do. They consider it a "deep nap" that can be ended by a chieftain. If there's an issue with someone in a "deep nap," they ask the chieftains to wake them up. Trolls don't understand why outlanders see it as a serious matter.
#UA Troll War Trolls
*Units\u132x3_1.png
 WAR TROLLS
The War Trolls warband is a special Troll elite melee infantry unit. War Trolls are fierce, tough, and vital to the troll army. To become a War Troll, a troll must fight one hundred angry trolls, provoking them until they either give up or fall into a "deep nap." If the troll survives, they earn the title of War Troll, but must give their teeth, the troll currency, as payment to the others.
#UA Troll War Mammoths
*Units\u145x3_1.png
 WAR MAMMOTH
The War Mammoths squadron is a special Troll elite mounted unit. Woolly mammoths are massive beasts with great strength and cold resistance. Initially tamed by the chief of the Frost Club trolls through wrestling, these mammoths were trained to bond with their riders through strength and respect. Frost Club trolls rode War Mammoths into battle with deadly force, forging the legend of the War Chief.
#UA Troll Medicinemans
*Units\u150x3_1.png
 MEDICINEMANS
The Medicinemans congregation is a special unit of Troll clerics. Serving as spiritual leaders and healers, they focus on boosting the spirits of sick trolls, often using motivation, rousing speeches, or insults. Known for their persuasive speech, Medicinemans excel at provoking others and lifting morale.
#UA Troll Rock Throwers
*Units\u248x3_1.png
 ROCK THROWERS
The Rock Throwers warband is a special Troll physical ranged infantry unit. Due to the scarcity of weapons, young trolls are only allowed to use sticks and stones in combat until they are old enough. Despite this, their boulder-throwing skills are formidable. Throwing large boulders is a popular pastime among troll youth, who earn respect by demonstrating their strength and accuracy in breaking things from a distance.
#UA Xuanyuan Conscripts
*Units\u287x3_1.png
 CONSCRIPTS
The Conscripts battalion is a special Xuanyuan basic polearm infantry unit. Unlike other races, Xuanyuan enforces conscription to train and arm soldiers, funded publicly, with draft dodging punishable by law. Conscripts undergo rigorous training with unique polearms, but their defensive equipment is minimal due to cost-cutting. Conscription, a practice from the ancient Xuanyuan Empire, continues as the standard for defending Xuanyuan polities.
#UA Xuanyuan Firelancers
*Units\u288x3_1.png
 FIRELANCERS
The Firelancers battalion is a special Xuanyuan advanced polearm infantry unit. These troopers wield halberds equipped with gunpowder weapons, producing loud sounds and distracting smoke. While not as advanced as dwarven firearms, their weaponry instills fear and boosts combat effectiveness. Gunpowder, originally developed by the Xuanyuan, led to innovations like firecrackers, fireworks, rockets, and bombs, which were later shared with their Dwarven neighbors upon settling in Myrror.
#UA Xuanyuan Dragon Guards
*Units\u291x3_1.png
 DRAGON GUARDS
The Dragon Guards squadron is a special Xuanyuan elite melee infantry unit. These warriors wield swords and powerful dragon shields that can throw fire. Originating from the ancient Xuanyuan Empire, the Dragon Guards were elite defenders against magical empires. The great dragon shields symbolize strength and courage, inspiring Xuanyuan warriors, even after the empire's fall, to defend their lords against countless foes.
#UA Xuanyuan Autocrossbowmen
*Units\u295x3_1.png
 AUTOCROSSBOWMEN
The Autocrossbowmen battalion is a special Xuanyuan elite physical ranged infantry unit. The Xuanyuan are renowned for their unique crossbow designs, especially the autocrossbow, a hand-held weapon with auto-drawing and auto-loading mechanisms for rapid, precise firing of explosive bolts. Only the best-equipped soldiers use these advanced weapons, allowing them to engage multiple targets quickly, even in close combat.
#UA Xuanyuan War Monks
*Units\u297x3_1.png
 WAR MONKS
The War Monks congregation is a special unit of Xuanyuan higher rank clerics. These monks combine martial arts with religious training, emphasizing strength and skill while following teachings that prohibit killing. In addition to combat, they serve as field medics, using mystical powers and medicinal knowledge to heal allies. Despite their warrior ethos, War Monks are exempt from wizard pacts due to their pacifist martial traditions.
#UA Xuanyuan Alchemists
*Units\u298x3_1.png
 ALCHEMISTS
The Alchemists battalion is a special Xuanyuan lower rank magician unit. Though not the originators of alchemy, the Xuanyuan have advanced its practical applications, including agricultural fertilizers, medicinal drugs, and gunpowder. In warfare, they serve as artillery, using mortars to launch poison cloud bombs. With spellcasting abilities equivalent to disciple-level magicians, they are valuable assets in both military and civic roles.
#UA Xuanyuan Elixir Alchemists
*Units\u299x3_1.png
 ELIXIR ALCHEMISTS
The Elixir Alchemists battalion is a special Xuanyuan higher rank magician unit. The Xuanyuan alchemists' ultimate goal is achieving everlasting life through elixirs, potent substances that enhance vitality and extend lifespans. Only those who can create these elixirs are considered true masters of alchemy. In battle, Elixir Alchemists serve as artillery, launching more powerful toxic cloud bombs with mortars. With spellcasting abilities akin to magister-level magicians, they combine formidable magic with their alchemical expertise.
#UA Xuanyuan Immortals
*Units\u300x3_1.png
 IMMORTALS
The Immortals squadron is a special Xuanyuan elite rank magician unit. After the fall of the Xuanyuan Empire, power shifted to immortal cultivators, mystical warriors who gain longevity and strength through a mix of alchemy, martial arts, and magic. Their rise coincided with the Xuanyuan's arrival on Myrror, where the magical environment boosts their regenerative abilities and enhances their vitality and supernatural powers.
#UA Xuanyuan Dragon Ship
*Units\u302x3_1.png
 DRAGON SHIP
The Dragon Ship is a special Xuanyuan naval unit. Once the ultimate warships of the ancient Xuanyuan Empire, Dragon Ships ruled the oceans of Arcanus. Now stationed in the seas of Myrror, these ships are crewed by magicians in separate compartments, allowing them to fire multiple magic bolts from protected sections. Equipped with flamethrowers for close combat, Dragon Ships are still formidable in naval battles.
#UA Xuanyuan War Wagons
*Units\u305x3_1.png
 WAR WAGONS
The War Wagons squadron is a special Xuanyuan siege unit, also known as carriage ballistae. Originating from conflicts with ancient Arcanian nomads, they feature small ballistae mounted on armored wagons for flexible missile deployment. Initially used against horsebowmen in the ancient Xuanyuan Empire's campaigns, these wagons have evolved to improve penetration against a variety of enemies on Myrror's battlefields.
#UA Xuanyuan Dragon Horses
*Units\u306x3_1.png
 DRAGON HORSES
The Dragon Horses battalion is a special Xuanyuan flying mounted unit. Originating from the Xuanyuan's fascination with dragons, these creatures were hybrids of sea horses and dragon-like amphibians, now extinct on Arcanus. Upon arriving in Myrror, they were bred with feral nightmares to give them flight capabilities. Elite Xuanyuan cavalrymen ride these creatures, representing the peak of Xuanyuan aerial combat prowess.
#UA Rakhshasa Manticores
*Units\u55x3_1.png
 MANTICORES
The Manticores squadron is a special Rakhshasa flying unit. These fierce beasts strike with deadly precision, originating from cursed Rakhshasa sinners who succumbed to bloodlust. Transformed into beastly forms with bat wings and scorpion tails, Manticores are driven by primal instincts, forsaking reason, morality, and spiritual redemption to feed their insatiable hunger for blood and flesh.
#UA Rakhshasa Wildhunters
*Units\u308x3_1.png
 WILDHUNTERS
The Wildhunters battalion is a special Rakhshasa advanced polearm infantry unit. As carnivores, Rakhshasa value game meat from traditional wild hunts and livestock. They charge through forests with hunting polearms, surrounding and slaying large beasts, demonstrating their skills in both hunting and wartime foraging.
#UA Rakhshasa Jaguar Warriors
*Units\u310x3_1.png
 JAGUAR WARRIORS
The Jaguar Warriors battalion is a special Rakhshasa advanced blade weapon infantry unit. Armed with flint blades designed to draw blood, these warriors charge fearlessly into enemy lines. They believe that consuming their foes' flesh and blood enhances their endurance and fulfills their duty, all while leaving no bodies behind.
#UA Rakhshasa Jungle Stalkers
*Units\u311x3_1.png
 JUNGLE STALKERS
The Jungle Stalkers battalion is a special Rakhshasa basic physical ranged infantry unit. Residing in Myrror's dense tropical jungles, they guard vital water sources with poison darts. They silently stalk intruders, either offering gifts or devouring them depending on their intentions, showcasing both stealth and lethal skill.
#UA Rakhshasa Blood Priests
*Units\u313x3_1.png
 BLOOD PRIEST
The Blood Priests congregation is a special Rakhshasa higher rank cleric unit. Following their creed of renouncing unnecessary violence, these elite clergy sustain themselves on blood and milk, avoiding the killing of their benefactors. In combat, they use blood siphoning spells to attack enemies while offering karmic redemption through blood donation.
#UA Rakhshasa Weretiger Mages
*Units\u314x3_1.png
 WERETIGER MAGES
The Weretiger Mages battalion is a special Rakhshasa lower rank magician unit. Known for their shapeshifting abilities, Rakhshasa mages can disguise themselves as animals or other races to infiltrate cities and mingle with people unnoticed. While their presence is known to the public, it often leads to paranoia, false accusations, and hunts for supposed predators, many of which are unfounded, resulting in innocent victims.
#UA Rakhshasa Rishi
*Units\u315x3_1.png
 RISHI
The Rishi congregation is a special Rakhshasa higher rank magician unit. These jungle sages are known for their wisdom and ability to see through illusions and falsehoods, earning respect from all races on Myrror. Using shapeshifting to conceal their true Rakhshasa forms, they sustain themselves by consuming enemy flesh and blood to rejuvenate.
#UA Rakhshasa Ogre Lords
*Units\u316x3_1.png
 OGRE LORDS
The Ogre Lords squad is a special Rakhshasa elite melee infantry unit. Ruling through strength and power, these leaders indulge in both carnal excess and martial prowess, inspiring bloodlust in their forces. Despite their tyrannical nature, they uphold noble duties, often serving as the last line of defense against overwhelming enemy forces.
#UA Hawkman Sky Lantern
*Units\u301x3_1.png
 SKY LANTERN
The Sky Lantern is a special Hawkman siege unit. Resembling a magical artifact, it serves as an altar to the powers of the sky, sun, lightning, and wind. Lifted by hot air and propelled by wind, it moves mechanically and enhances direct attack spells in combat. While it can discharge lightning bolts, it has little defense against melee attacks.
The Sky Lantern is counted as ship and could only launch from the city tile or water tile closed to the city.
#UA Hawkman Eagle Warriors
*Units\u318x3_1.png
 EAGLE WARRIORS
The Eagle Warriors battalion is a special Hawkman advanced polearm infantry unit. Chosen for their speed and sharp perception, they serve as couriers, scouts, and mobile defenders. They excel in speed, awareness, and preemptive strikes, often neutralizing enemy advantages with their quick reflexes.
#UA Hawkman Tomahawks
*Units\u320x3_1.png
 TOMAHAWKS
The Tomahawks battalion is a special Hawkman advanced blade weapon infantry unit. Selected for their diving skill and strength during coming-of-age ceremonies, these youths are trained at the Hall of Heavenly Axe to become Tomahawks warriors. Armed with heavy two-handed axes, they deliver swift, devastating attacks from the sky. Battles involving Tomahawks are often more like massacres than traditional combat.
#UA Hawkman Huichilobos
*Units\u321x3_1.png
 HUICHILOBOS
The Huichilobos battalion is a special Hawkman elite blade weapon infantry unit. Anointed by the Rite of the Sun, they serve as sacred warriors and intermediaries between the mortal world and the realm of death. Protected by the spirit of the Sun, they are immune to fire and unaffected by unnatural death. Armed with poison-coated weapons and shields, they are both deadly in attack and well-defended against ranged attacks and magic. With the aid of warrior spirits, they can summon projections of ancient warriors to assist in combat.
#UA Hawkman Harpies
*Units\u322x3_1.png
 HARPIES
The Harpies battalion is a special Hawkman basic physical ranged infantry unit. Female Hawkmen, while enjoying more privileges than their counterparts in other races, still share the duty of protecting their society. Adult females without special talents must fight alongside males when called to arms. Known as "harpies" by other races, they serve as light skirmishers, throwing javelins at close range while maintaining distance from enemies. They target vulnerable foes from the blind side and pursue fleeing enemies to prevent escape.
#UA Hawkman Holy Mother
*Units\u323x3_1.png
 HOLY MOTHER
The Holy Mother is a special Hawkman higher rank cleric. Hawkmen are considered by other races' religious authorities to be descendants of the heralds of the two opposing Primal Forces. However, Hawkman religious figures primarily serve to train and serve the Holy Mother, the most sacred and closest to the heavens. Many promising girls are trained from a young age, but only a few become Holy Mothers. Protected by divine grace from unnatural forces, the Holy Mother travels across the world with her followers, using her heavenly miracles to strengthen people's souls. Her miracles cannot be imitated by clerics of other races.
#UA Hawkman Enchantresses
*Units\u324x3_1.png
 ENCHANTRESSES
The Enchantresses battalion is a special Hawkman lower rank magician unit. Female Hawkmen generally have a stronger affinity for magic and supernatural power than their male counterparts. After their coming-of-age ceremony, those with strong magical affinity are trained to harness their powers. There is a rumor that a Hawkman's magical strength can be identified by their beauty alone. More powerful Enchantresses maintain their youthful appearance well beyond their years, as their higher magical capacity slows aging, and some use magic to enhance their beauty.
#UA Hawkman Sirens
*Units\u325x3_1.png
 SIRENS
The Sirens battalion is a special Hawkman higher rank magician unit. The beauty and allure of each female Hawkman are tied to their magical power, with the most powerful being the most enchanting, capable of charming others to their demise. As their magical abilities grow, many Enchantresses are drawn toward the dark path of the Siren, aligned with the left-hand side of the Primal Force. Their beauty can lead to the death and destruction of those around them, especially enemies who fall under their spell. Driven by their desires, many betray their allies and break their vows, only to meet death in the end.
#UA Hobgoblins
*Units\u349x3_1.png
 HOBGOBLINS
The Hobgoblins Warband is a special Goblin advanced polearm infantry unit. Goblins evolve into Hobgoblins by absorbing the essence of other creatures, particularly sentient ones, which makes them smarter and more social. Hobgoblins are larger and exhibit more mature, practical behavior, although they retain a childlike sense of fun. They are more responsible than regular goblins, taking on tasks such as gathering food, doing math, digging, and building. Outside the nest, they serve as both warriors and workers, often engaged in tasks like building roads. While generally friendlier and more helpful individually, they become more violent and aggressive in groups.
#UA Goblin Warbosses
*Units\u350x3_1.png
 GOBLIN WARBOSSES
The Goblin Warboss is a special Goblin elite specialist unit. Some Goblins evolve by absorbing the essence of large, powerful creatures, growing bigger and more dominant. These Warbosses bully smaller Goblins into submission and are known for their cunning, ambition, and unquenchable thirst for power, though they are often lazy. They derive pleasure from controlling a large number of henchmen, whom they treat as pawns in their game of war. Warbosses thrive on conquering enemies, pursuing them, plundering resources, and relishing the anguish of their defeated foes.
#UA Goblin Spider Riders
*Units\u351x3_1.png
 GOBLIN SPIDER RIDERS
The Goblin Spider Riders warband is a special Goblin basic melee mounted unit. Goblins have a natural fondness for animals, often taming and domesticating creatures with little regard for safety. One such creature is the large venomous spider, which they ride into battle. While smaller and weaker than the magical Giant Spiders summoned by wizards, these naturally occurring spiders are still considered untamable by other races. How Goblins manage to tame them remains a mystery to all.
The goblins require suitable environment such as swamp, or Nature Node for spores to develop into Spider Riders.
#UA Goblin Tricksters
*Units\u352x3_1.png
 GOBLIN TRICKSTERS
The Goblin Tricksters gang is a special Goblin specialist unit. Goblins delight in pranks and dark humor, and their pranks are rarely harmless. Hobgoblin Tricksters specialize in setting traps and skillfully evading attacks on the battlefield. They entertain younger goblins and Warbosses while turning enemies into unwitting fools, breaking down walls, and causing meticulously laid plans to fall apart.
The goblins require suitable environment such as grassland, or desert, or hill for spores to develop into Tricksters.
#UA Goblin Rabblerousers
*Units\u353x3_1.png
 GOBLIN RABBLEROUSERS
The Goblin Rabblerousers gang is a special Goblin support unit. Goblins enjoy mimicking other sentient races, especially their politicians and clergy, often focusing more on the excitement and emotion stirred than the message itself. Goblin Rabblerousers use this talent to deliver rousing speeches that incite fanaticism, provoking their kin to take sacrificial and violent actions.
The goblins require suitable environment such as river, or desert, or Sorcery Node for spores to develop into Rabblerousers.
#UA Goblin Hexers
*Units\u354x3_1.png
 GOBLIN HEXERS
The Goblin Hexers gang is a special Goblin lower rank magician unit. Goblins start learning magic after their progenitor spores land on the twin planes. As they absorb the essence of magical creatures and mana-rich minerals, some develop the ability to wield magic. While most Goblins lack enough magical power to fulfill their desires, a few can wield it, though they focus more on causing chaos and agony than on efficiency or effectiveness.
The goblins require suitable environment such as Chaos Node, or Nature Node, or Sorcery Node for spores to develop into Hexers.
#UA Goblin Arsonists
*Units\u355x3_1.png
 GOBLIN ARSONISTS
The Goblin Arsonists warband is a special Goblin advanced melee infantry unit. Goblins have a deep fascination with flames, finding comfort in watching things burn, and some even liken it to the warmth of a mother they never had. When they briefly acquired dwarven flamethrowers and Xuanyuan dragon shields, chaos ensued. Though the items were reclaimed, goblins began crafting their own crude flamethrowers, using them for everything from curing skin rashes to burning down cities. This innovation quickly spread through Goblin nests, reaching even those who had never encountered dwarves or Xuanyuan.
The goblins require suitable environment such as tundra, or volcano, or Chaos Node for spores to develop into Arsonists.
#UA Night Goblins
*Units\u356x3_1.png
 NIGHT GOBLINS
The Night Goblins warband is a special Goblin advanced missile infantry unit. Born from spores in dark caves, Night Goblins are more comfortable in darkness than daylight. They have excellent night vision, allowing them to excel at hiding, stalking enemies, and striking from the shadows. Occasionally, they infiltrate other races' settlements to observe and mimic their nighttime activities. Despite being biologically asexual, they are driven by a strong desire to imitate these actions.
The goblins require suitable environment such as hill, or mountain, or Nature Node for spores to develop into Night Goblins.
#UA Goblin Mechaniacs
*Units\u357x3_1.png
 GOBLIN MECHANIACS
The Goblin Mechaniacs gang is a special Goblin mechanical specialist unit. Goblins are naturally curious and inventive, often disregarding self-preservation in their pursuits. Those with a deep passion for mechanics are known as Mechaniacs. They enjoy tinkering with devices and have a talent for turning scrap into makeshift, functional war machines that are just as dangerous to themselves as to their enemies. Their reckless nature allows them to repair machines in the heat of battle, undeterred by enemy fire or personal risk.
The goblins require suitable environment such as river, or mountain for spores to develop into Mechaniacs.
#UA Goblin Poxbearers
*Units\u358x3_1.png
 GOBLIN POXBEARERS
The Goblin Poxbearers ward is a special Goblin specialist unit. Goblins, though unfamiliar with sanitation, enjoy playing “doctor and patient” and are particularly fascinated by the role of nurses. The Poxbearers emerged from their chaotic attempts to imitate illness and "cure" each other, with goblins competing to be the “sickest” for attention. Eventually, they discovered that their self-induced illnesses, manageable for them, were devastating to other races, a fact they quickly weaponized.
The goblins require suitable environment such as swamp, or Sorcery Node for spores to develop into Poxbearers.
#UA Doom Wheels
*Units\u359x3_1.png
 DOOM WHEELS
The Doom Wheels squad is a special Goblin mechanical mounted unit. The Doom Wheel is a motorized monowheel operated by goblins, equipped with scythe-like blades that cut through everything in its path. Its engine uses a volatile mixture of molten Quark and Crysx, converting energy into propulsion through intense agitation. This cutting-edge but dangerous technology is avoided by other races due to its scorching radiation, toxic gases, and high risk of explosion. Goblins, however, push these machines into overdrive, making the Doom Wheel a deadly hazard for everyone alike.
Cost of the Doom Wheels could be reduced by 20% in city with plenty of Quork crystal and by 40% in the city with plenty of Crysx crystal.
#UA Goblin Gliders
*Units\u360x3_1.png
 GOBLIN GLIDERS
The Goblin Gliders squadron is a special Goblin flying unit. Goblins, driven by wild imagination, have always dreamed of manned flight. As their nest's fungal network grows, making them smarter, their attempts at flying become more feasible. Starting from crude wings and catapult launches, they have developed small, stable gliders that combine mechanical and magical features. Goblin Gliders soar through the skies, carrying bombs, each uniquely decorated by its pilot. Piloting a glider is a great honor and a thrilling experience, but one that most will only get to enjoy once.
#UA Midget Submarines
*Units\u361x3_1.png
 MIDGET SUBMARINES
The Midget Submarines flotilla is a special Goblin naval unit. Driven by curiosity, Goblins seek to explore the deepest and most uncharted waters. To reach these depths, they created the Midget Submarine, a vessel powered by a miniature goblin nest with its own fungal network, encased in a waterproof shell. Its operations rely on goblin biological features that other races can't replicate. While primarily for exploration, Midget Submarines also serve as effective underwater weapons, though they lose their advantage on the surface.
Cost of the Midget Submarines could be reduced by 20% in city with plenty of Quork crystal and by 40% in the city with plenty of Crysx crystal.
#UA Magic Spirit
*Units\u154x3_1.png
 MAGIC SPIRIT
The Magic Spirit is a common Arcane realm Fantastic creature. Resembling a ghost-like entity, the Magic Spirit manifests as a non-corporeal form surrounded by a glowing aura, capable of melding with Power nodes and scouting swiftly through any terrain or obstacles.
#UA Clockwork Tinmen
*Units\u363x3_1.png
 CLOCKWORK TINMEN
The Clockwork Tinman is an Uncommon Arcane realm Fantastic creature uniquely created by an Artificer wizard. Created with synergy and harmony between mechanic and magic, clockwork tinmen are helping hands and industrous labour for its creator. Always work tirelessly with precision and mechanical skill, they could build road better than any dwarves engineers and repair and optimize any war machines better than the most reckless mechaniacs. They also on the field with survey mechanical critters that could be using for sabotage enemy's mechanical unit effectively in combat.
#UA Boar
*Units\u152x3_1.png
 BOAR
The Boar is a common Nature realm Fantastic creature. Grand old boars, possessed by nature spirits, grow larger and sturdier as they answer the call of Gaia to fight. After combat, the nature spirits depart, and the boars return to the wilderness, resuming their normal lives.
 
The Conjurer could study how to summon Boars with Conjuring Pact if has at least 2 Nature Books.
#UA Water Elemental
*Units\u158x3_1.png
 WATER ELEMENTAL
The Water Elemental is an uncommon Nature realm Fantastic creature. Water Elementals, originating from the elemental realm of water as Undines, are invisible and formless. When bound to the material world, they take on a physical water form. Water Elementals attack by shooting magical water and can easily move through oceans or other water terrains. They cannot be truly killed, if their physical form is destroyed or disconnected from their essence, it disintegrates, returning the Undine to their realm.
 
The Conjurer could study how to summon Water Elemental with Conjuring Pact if has at least 4 Nature Books.
#UA War Bears
*Units\u179x3_1.png
 WAR BEAR
The War Bear is a common Nature realm Fantastic creature. War Bears are powerful creatures that answer the call of Nature. Larger and stronger than ordinary bears, they possess incredible strength, durability, and excel in melee combat. According to legend, War Bears are ascended from wild bears by Gaia, the will of Nature, who bestows her power upon the worthy to transform them into her agents. War Bears are known to lead troops through forest terrain, serving as formidable allies in battle.
 
The Conjurer could study how to summon War Bears with Conjuring Pact if has at least 2 Nature Books.
#UA Sprites
*Units\u180x3_1.png
 SPRITE
The Sprite is a common Nature realm Fantastic creature. Sprites are tiny humanoid creatures found in areas where the power of Nature is strong. They have large butterfly wings on their backs, allowing them to fly, leaving behind a shimmering blue trail that is likely magical. Known for their mischievous and independent nature, Sprites are capable of magical ranged attacks. While they may serve Gaia's will, they do not willingly serve any wizard.
 
The Conjurer could study how to summon Sprites with Conjuring Pact if has at least 2 Nature Books.
#UA Cockatrices
*Units\u181x3_1.png
 COCKATRICE
The Cockatrice is an uncommon Nature realm Fantastic creature. A Cockatrice is a strange creature with the head of a rooster and the body of a reptile, complete with dragon-like wings. Though not particularly strong, it possesses the deadly ability to petrify enemies upon contact, ending their existence with a single blow.
 
The Conjurer could study how to summon Cockatrices with Conjuring Pact if has at least 4 Nature Books.
#UA Great Lizard
*Units\u182x3_1.png
 GREAT LIZARD
The Great Lizard is an uncommon Nature realm Fantastic creature. The Great Lizard, also known as the Lizard King, is the largest species of lizard and possesses almost all abilities of lesser lizards, including regeneration, camouflage in the wilderness, the ability to swim, and toxic saliva. Lizardmen view these creatures as their mythical forefathers, believing that the Lizard King, who married the Naga Queen, gave birth to the eggs of their first ancestors.
 
The Conjurer could study how to summon Great Lizard with Conjuring Pact if has at least 4 Nature Books.

 GIANT SPIDER

The Conjurer could study how to summon Giant Spiders with Conjuring Pact if has at least 4 Nature Books.
#UA Stone Giant
*Units\u184x3_1.png
 STONE GIANT
The Stone Giant is a rare Nature realm Fantastic creature. Stone Giants are reclusive and peaceful, preferring solitude. Despite their immense size and strength, they are surprisingly lithe and graceful. Skilled rock throwers, they treat boulder tossing as a favored pastime. When summoned by Nature, Stone Giants emerge from the mountains, wielding powerful melee attacks and deadly ranged boulder strikes.
 
The Conjurer could study how to summon Stone Giant with Conjuring Pact if has at least 6 Nature Books.

 COLOSSUS
The Colossus is a very rare Nature realm Fantastic creature. Born where adamantium veins merge with the heart of orihalcon, the Colossus is clad in golden-hued adamantium. This mighty guardian strikes with powerful melee attacks and deadly ranged boulders, making it one of Nature's most formidable protectors.
 
The Conjurer could study how to summon Colossus with Conjuring Pact if has at least 8 Nature Books.
#UA Gorgon
*Units\u186x3_1.png
 GORGON
The Gorgon is a rare Nature realm Fantastic creature. The Gorgons are female creatures with serpentine lower bodies and snake-like hair, serving Gaia and her will. Often called "witches of Gaia," they are sentient and wield Nature magic. While generally cordial, those who provoke them are turned to stone by their gaze. Villagers sometimes seek out friendlier Gorgons, offering farm produce in exchange for good weather and bountiful harvests.
 
The Conjurer could study how to summon Gorgons with Conjuring Pact if has at least 6 Nature Books.
#UA Earth Elemental
*Units\u187x3_1.png
 EARTH ELEMENTAL
The Earth elemental is a rare Nature realm Fantastic creature. Originating from the elemental realm of Earth, known as Gnomi, Earth Elementals take on physical forms made of solid material when bound to the material world. Though slow, they possess high strength and endurance, capable of delivering powerful melee strike and crushing enemy fortifications. Earth Elementals cannot be truly killed; once their physical body is destroyed or disconnected from the Gnomi essence, they disintegrate and return to their realm.
 
The Conjurer could study how to summon Earth Elemental with Conjuring Pact if has at least 6 Nature Books.
#UA Behemoth
*Units\u188x3_1.png
 BEHEMOTH
The Behemoth is a very rare Nature realm Fantastic creature. The Behemoth is a massive amphibious reptilian creature, covered in thick red stony scales and with spiny plates protruding from its back. This unstoppable juggernaut is incredibly strong in melee combat, capable of crushing through any obstacle or armor in its path. Victims within its deadly sight are petrified before being crushed. Even if seemingly slain, the Behemoth can rise again unless its corpse is completely destroyed.
 
The Conjurer could study how to summon Behemoth with Conjuring Pact if has at least 8 Nature Books.
#UA Great Wyrm
*Units\u189x3_1.png
 GREAT WYRM
The Great Wyrm is a very rare Nature realm Fantastic creature. The Great Wyrm is a mysterious serpent-like creature covered in thick scales. Most of its massive body remains hidden underground, with only its head and neck emerging to strike from unexpected angles on the battlefield. Its subterranean body is an enigma, and the assumption of its serpentine nature is only based on its visible parts. The Wyrm delivers devastating melee strikes, and lethal venom to finish any victims.
 
The Conjurer could study how to summon Great Wyrm with Conjuring Pact if has at least 8 Nature Books.
#UA Killer Wasp
*Units\u252x3_1.png
 KILLER WASP
The Killer Wasp is common Nature realm Fantastic creatures. Empress Wasps are predatory eusocial insects, like bees, wasps, and hornets, that live in forest and jungle hives ruled by queens. Occasionally, these queens are empowered by Nature, transforming into Fantastic creatures with enhanced hive mind abilities. Under an Empress Wasp's rule, multiple hives unite into massive, aggressive swarms. These insects grow larger and fiercer, becoming fiercely protective of their empress. Normal behavior returns once the Empress Wasp is slain.
 
The Conjurer could study how to summon Killer Wasps with Conjuring Pact if has at least 2 Nature Books.
#UA Lesser Gaia Lord
*Units\u260x3_1.png
 LESSER GAIA LORD
The Lesser Gaia Lord is a legendary Nature realm Fantastic creature. Gaia, the collective will of Nature, is often seen as a single entity, but in reality, it is fragmented due to failed attempts at spells of mastery across both realms. These fragmented aspects occasionally manifest as powerful offshoot beings called 'Gaia Lords.' Known as the daughters of Gaia, these beings possess immense supernatural power and can wield Nature’s energy at will.
 
The Conjurer could study how to summon Lesser Gaia Lord with Conjuring Pact if has at least 10 Nature Books.
#UA Great Gaia Lord
*Units\u261x3_1.png
 GREAT GAIA LORD
The Great Gaia Lord is a forbidden Nature realm Fantastic creature. Gaia, the collective will of Nature, is often seen as a single entity, but in truth, it has been broken as result from several failed attempts at Spells of Mastery. The Great Gaia Lords, the eldest among Gaia's daughters, are among the most powerful fragments of Gaia. The arrival of a Great Gaia Lord signifies Gaia herself enforcing her will.
 
The Conjurer could study how to summon Great Gaia Lord with Conjuring Pact if has at least 12 Nature Books.
#UA Sacred Ancient
*Units\u270x3_1.png
 SACRED ANCIENT
The Sacred Ancient is an rare Nature realm Fantastic creature. Sacred Ancients are ancient great trees that serve as homes for spirits. Revered by animists of various races, these trees are considered sacred due to the protective spirits within. While immobile in combat, Sacred Ancients possess spiritual defenses against deception, and their faeries can cast fairy dust. These trees also act as natural sources of magical power, but binding them permanently to a wizard's will is challenging.
 
The Conjurer could study how to summon Sacred Ancient with Conjuring Pact if has at least 6 Nature Books.

 THUNDERBIRD

Their arrival signals dark skies and powerful storms. Capable of soaring through tempests and lightning without harm, the sighting of a Thunderbird is seen as a positive omen, often heralding rain that nourishes the land.

#UA Warg
*Units\u326x3_1.png
 WARG
The Warg is a common Nature realm Fantastic creature. Wargs, also known as Fenrir by northern barbarians, are giant spirit wolves found primarily in the frozen north, though they can be encountered elsewhere. These wolves travel in packs, sharing a strong kinship. Wargs are exceptional trackers, able to navigate forests and mountains with ease. Known for their agility and leaping attacks, they often catch their enemies off guard in combat.

#UA Floating Island
*Units\u190x3_1.png
 FLOATING ISLAND
The Floating Island is a common Sorcery realm Fantastic creature. Floating Islands are crafted from water, salt, and air, stabilized by magic. These islands float effortlessly on the ocean, moving with the tides and winds controlled by their wizard owners. While they lack self-will and cannot defend themselves, the islands will dissipate if attacked without units onboard, as the stabilizing magic is disrupted.
#UA Phantom Beast
*Units\u191x3_1.png
 PHANTOM BEAST
The Phantom Beast is an uncommon Sorcery realm Fantastic creature. Phantom Beasts are large, humanoid illusions created by sorcery. To the untrained eye, they appear as shimmering blue lights with transparent bodies, but this is simply an illusion powered by magic. Skilled in melee combat, they can move across water and deliver illusionary attacks that bypass physical defenses, targeting the mind. However, against those with Illusion Immunity, their attacks are significantly weakened.
 
The Conjurer could study how to summon Phantom Beast with Conjuring Pact if has at least 4 Sorcery Books.
#UA Phantom Warrior
*Units\u192x3_1.png
 PHANTOM WARRIOR
The Phantom Warrior is a common Sorcery realm Fantastic creature. These translucent humanoids appear as soldiers wielding long pikes, their glowing magical outlines distinguishing them from mortal warriors. They move freely, ignoring geographical obstacles, and strike with illusionary power that bypasses defenses. As sorcerous illusions, they typically dissipate after combat. Against those immune to illusions, their attacks are significantly weaker.
 
The Conjurer could study how to summon Phantom Warriors with Conjuring Pact if has at least 2 Sorcery Books.

 STORM GIANT
The Storm Giant is a rare Sorcery realm Fantastic creature. Clad in blue plate armor and helmets that conceal their faces, Storm Giants are large, intelligent, and prideful beings. They wield lightning as both a melee and ranged weapon, enhanced by magical properties. Capable of controlling wind to shield themselves from small projectiles, they are selective about responding to summoning calls, only heeding those from worthy wizards.

#UA Djinn

 DJINN
The Djinn is a very rare Sorcery realm Fantastic creature. Djinns are powerful elemental spirits from the realm of aether, known for their ability to form physical bodies by binding their magical power at will. Unlike other elemental spirits, they could communicate easily with mortals. While generally wild, Djinn are often tolerant of servitude, provided the deal is fair, and temporary. They can transport troops overland. In combat, they could perform several kinds of powerful sorcery.

#UA Sky Drake
*Units\u196x3_1.png
 SKY DRAKE
The Sky Drake is a very rare Sorcery realm Fantastic creature. Sky Drakes are lightning-breathing wind dragons from the realm of air. While smaller and less resilient than Great Drakes from the realm of fire, they are much wiser. Sky Drakes possess the ability to see through illusions and are completely immune to magic. Their lightning breath is a deadly weapon capable of vaporizing most opponents, regardless of their armor.
 
The Conjurer could study how to summon Sky Drake with Conjuring Pact if has at least 8 Sorcery Books.
#UA Naga
*Units\u197x3_1.png
 NAGA
The Naga is a common Sorcery realm Fantastic creature. Nagas are sentient, half-humanoid serpentine beings from an advanced underwater civilization. While not skilled in spellcraft, they are renowned for their mercenary services, wielding tridents and toxins with great precision. Originating from a distant mortal plane across the realm of Aether, Nagas have spread across various planes due to careless summoners. They sustain themselves through magical sources, with physical food serving only for recreation.
 
The Conjurer could study how to summon Nagas with Conjuring Pact if has at least 2 Sorcery Books.
#UA Coatl
*Units\u208x3_1.png
 COATL
The Coatl is an uncommon Sorcery realm Fantastic creature. Coatls are feathered serpents with rainbow-feathered wings and venomous breath, combining intellect surpassing humans with powerful psionic abilities. It is uncertain whether their flight is due to wings or psionics. In combat, they can unleash lightning breath and venomous strikes, and their psionics enhance their sorcery. Primarily found in the elemental realm of air, Coatls are also worshipped by rainforest inhabitants on material planes where they roam.
 
The Conjurer could study how to summon Coatl with Conjuring Pact if has at least 4 Sorcery Books.
#UA Cloud Giant
*Units\u251x3_1.png
 CLOUD GIANT
The Cloud Giant is a rare Sorcery realm Fantastic creature. Cloud Giants, residing in the clouds of the air realm or ethereal lands, are powerful, handsome, and wealthy giants. They enjoy grand entrances and often masquerade as gods for amusement. Known for their refined tastes, trickery, cunning, and love of gambling, Cloud Giants frequently toy with mortals using illusions. While their damage is illusory, dispelling the illusion doesn't negate its full effects. They are skilled at seeing through trickery.
 
The Conjurer could study how to summon Cloud Giant with Conjuring Pact if has at least 6 Sorcery Books.
#UA Lesser Aether Lord
*Units\u262x3_1.png
 LESSER AETHER LORD
The Lesser Aether Lord is a legendary Sorcery realm Fantastic creature. Aether Lords are enigmatic beings from the realm of Aether. In the primordial past, the Aether sky was clear, known as the "True Cosmic Sky," until attempts to cast the Spell of Mastery created portals linking mortal minds to Aether. These disturbances gave rise to monstrous Aether Lords. While the portals closed when the casting attempts ceased, Aether Lords continue to persist, terrorizing those who interfere with the Aether.
 
The Conjurer could study how to summon Lesser AEther Lord with Conjuring Pact if has at least 10 Sorcery Books.
#UA Great Aether Lord
*Units\u263x3_1.png
 GREAT AETHER LORD
The Great Aether Lord is a forbidden Sorcery realm Fantastic creature. Great Aether Lords are ancient beings existed in the primordial Cosmic True Sky since time immemorial, predate mortal disturbances. Aligned with the will of Aether, they were awakened by attempts to cast the Spell of Mastery, becoming guardians against mortal interference. They cannot return to slumber due to the irreversible state of the Aether causes by mortal disturbance, resulting in their hostility toward powerful wizards.
 
The Conjurer could study how to summon Great AEther Lord with Conjuring Pact if has at least 12 Sorcery Books.

 KRAKEN
The Kraken is a rare Sorcery realm Fantastic creature. Krakens are massive ocean-dwelling magical beasts from the abyssal depths but can dry land when necessary. With thick, shell-like plating that makes them resistant to most attacks, especially long-range projectiles, Krakens wield powerful claws and can shoot high-pressure water at close range. Primarily hunting in the ocean, they excel in combat in aquatic environments and could channel their power as if they were in their abyssal home in Sorcery node.
 
The Conjurer could study how to summon Kraken with Conjuring Pact if has at least 6 Sorcery Books.

 HELL HOUND
The Hell Hound is a common Chaos realm Fantastic creature. Known as the "Hell Chaser," the Hell Hound is a twisted canine from the Chaos realm. These beasts are much larger than typical wolves and possess the ability to breathe fire. Hell Hound packs consist of unrelated members, with the most ruthless alpha in charge. Occasionally, they coerce ordinary dogs into servitude, which would soon mutate into Hell Hounds by Chaos's influence and become full members of the pack.

#UA Gargoyle
*Units\u156x3_1.png
 GARGOYLE
The Gargoyle is an uncommon Chaos realm Fantastic creature. Gargoyles are born from the corruption of the realm of fire by Chaos, taking on humanoid forms made of magma, granite, and obsidian. As creatures made entirely of stone, their thick exteriors make them highly resistant to destruction. Chaos grants them the ability to fly, defying the laws of physics. They are immune to biological weaknesses like poison, and being turned to stone has no effect on them since they are already made of stone.
 
The Conjurer could study how to summon Gargoyles with Conjuring Pact if has at least 4 Chaos Books.
