#UA Chaos Spawn
*Units\u159x3_1.png
 CHAOS SPAWN
The Chaos Spawn is a rare Chaos realm Fantastic creature. Chaos Spawns are the true children of Chaos, born from endless mutations within the Chaos realm. Created during the Chaos Calamity from failed attempts to cast the Spell of Mastery, they are twisted versions of creatures from different planes. Their identities are lost, each one a unique yet distorted reflection of its former self. Those who meet their gaze risk falling into madness, cursed by the same fate that transformed the Chaos Spawns.
 
The Conjurer could study how to summon Chaos Spawn with Conjuring Pact if has at least 6 Chaos Books.
#UA Chimera
*Units\u160x3_1.png
 CHIMERA
The Chimera is an uncommon Chaos realm Fantastic creature. Chimeras are creatures formed from stable mutations of various animals, with traits of a lion, goat, snake, and bat-like wings that grant them flight. They also possess the ability to breathe fire, a common feature among Chaos creatures. Emerging during the Chaos Calamity, Chimeras were created when creatures fused and mutated from the chaotic power. While some became uncontrollable Chaos Spawns, others stabilized into the distinct form of the Chimera.
 
The Conjurer could study how to summon Chimeras with Conjuring Pact if has at least 4 Chaos Books.
#UA Doom Bat
*Units\u161x3_1.png
 DOOM BAT
The Doom Bat is a rare Chaos realm Fantastic creature. Doom Bats are massive, unnatural black bats from the realm of Chaos. They use powerful sonic attacks to hunt their victims, which cannot be blocked or defended against. Due to their high metabolism, Doom Bats emit intense heat waves from their skin, burning anything nearby. Their speed is extraordinary, enabling them to travel like shooting stars. Once they detect their prey, evading them becomes nearly impossible.
 
The Conjurer could study how to summon Doom Bat with Conjuring Pact if has at least 6 Chaos Books.
#UA Efreet
*Units\u162x3_1.png
 EFREET
The Efreet is a rare Chaos realm Fantastic creature. Efreets are djinns transformed by Chaos during the Chaos Calamity, when part of the Aether realm and many djinns sank into the primordial void. Tainted by entropic fire and Chaos, Efreets lack the space-time attunement of djinns but gain destructive powers. The influence of Chaos has made them emotionally unstable, with frequent mood swings and anger issues. Despite these difficulties, Efreets are more passionate than djinns, leading to a higher birth rate among them since the Chaos Calamity.
 
The Conjurer could study how to summon Efreet with Conjuring Pact if has at least 6 Chaos Books.
#UA Hydra
*Units\u163x3_1.png
 HYDRA
The Hydra is a very rare Chaos realm Fantastic creature. Hydras are massive, nine-headed amphibious creatures from the primordial sea, residing in the realm of Chaos. Each head has its own will, is venomous, breathes lightning, and acts unpredictably. With chaotic vitality, the Hydra constantly molts, healing injuries almost instantly. Originally serpentine, their form evolved into a reptilian shape with legs, reflecting the transformation of the primordial void from a cosmic sea to a chaotic, burning spawning pool influenced by fire and Aether.
 
The Conjurer could study how to summon Hydra with Conjuring Pact if has at least 8 Chaos Books.
#UA Great Drake
*Units\u164x3_1.png
 GREAT DRAKE
The Great Drake is a very rare Chaos realm Fantastic creature. Great Drakes are fire-breathing dragons from the realm of fire, originally known as fire drakes and similar in size to other great dragon kinds. However, the Chaos Calamity mutated them into much stronger and larger beings, their scales now irradiated and capable of burning everything they touch. Their fire breath generates heat far beyond that of normal flames, incinerating anything in its path.
 
The Conjurer could study how to summon Great Drake with Conjuring Pact if has at least 8 Chaos Books.

 LESSER CHAOS LORD

 GREAT CHAOS LORD
The Great Chaos Lord is a forbidden Chaos realm Fantastic creature. Great Chaos Lords are the oldest and most powerful among their kind, born during the Chaos Calamity. Their status has been solidified through eons of mutations, fusions, and countless battles fought to survive within the chaotic realm of Chaos. The appearance of a Great Chaos Lord in the mortal realm signals impending conflict and often marks the approach of the time when the Spell of Mastery will be cast again.

#UA Fire Drake

The Fire Drake is a rare Chaos realm Fantastic creature. Fire Drakes, cousins of the massive Great Drakes, migrated to the mortal planes of Arcanus and Myrror long ago. They originate from the realm of fire, escaping just as it was engulfed by Chaos. While they retain many of their original traits, such as breathing fire and casting fireballs, they no longer possess the inherent resistance to fire or lightning. Unlike their Great Drake relatives, Fire Drakes are not surrounded by impenetrable flames.

Symbolizing purity and grace, they are immune to poison and possess the power to ward off curses and cleanse corrupted lands. Elusive and rarely seen, unicorns can teleport away from those with wicked intentions. According to legend, only maidens can tame them, though no mortal maiden has ever succeeded in riding one.

These non-corporeal beings can move through solid objects and are dedicated to aiding those in need. Serving as messengers of Life, they protect divinities and their followers. On the battlefield, Angels bless their allies and wield swords of justice to strike down evil.
 
The Conjurer could study how to summon Angel with Conjuring Pact if has at least 6 Life Books.

Wielding swords of justice imbued with holy flame, Archangels inspire their allies with heavenly glory. They embody mortals' faith and ideals, leading crusades against forces aligned with the opposite aspect of the Primal Force.

#UA Phoenix
*Units\u200x3_1.png
 PHOENIX
The Phoenix is a very rare Life realm Fantastic creature. Phoenixes are majestic, fire-bird creatures blessed with the power of Life. Originally from the realm of fire, they were spared from Chaos corruption and ascended to the realm of Life. Phoenixes can bring life back to the mortal plane, are immune to fire and unnatural death, and heal allies with their aura on the battlefield. Upon death, they are reborn from their own ashes within a short period of time.
 
The Conjurer could study how to summon Phoenix with Conjuring Pact if has at least 8 Life Books.
#UA Ethereal Knight
*Units\u211x3_1.png
 ETHEREAL KNIGHT
The Ethereal Knight is a very rare Life realm Fantastic creature. The ethereal knights are legendary and enigmatic figures who appear to protect those in need. Their true nature remains a mystery. Some believe they are flawed heroes given a chance at redemption in the afterlife, while others think they are embodiments of knightly ideals shaped by the faith and hope of believers in the right-hand aspect of the Primal Force. What they truly are remains unknown, perhaps even to the knights themselves.
 
The Conjurer could study how to summon Ethereal Knight with Conjuring Pact if has at least 8 Life Books.
#UA Valkyrie
*Units\u269x3_1.png
 VALKYRIE
The Valkyrie is a rare Life realm Fantastic creature. Valkyries are divine battle maidens and choosers of the slain, serving gods by granting exaltation to chosen warriors and escorting heroic souls to the Hall of Valor. They ride celestial steeds resembling winged unicorns into combat. While myths of Valkyries as brides exist, they are simply the daydreams of unwitting admirers.
 
The Conjurer could study how to summon Valkyries with Conjuring Pact if has at least 6 Life Books.
#UA Seraph
*Units\u286x3_1.png
 SERAPH
The Seraph is a forbidden Life realm Fantastic creature. Seraphs are the highest angels in the angelic hierarchy, with six wings, and are the closest beings to the Life aspect of the Primal Force. Too exalted to serve any divinity or mortal wizard master, their appearance in the mortal world signals a cosmic threat that requires the intervention of the Primal Force.
 
The Conjurer could study how to summon Seraph with Conjuring Pact if has at least 12 Life Books.
#UA Simurgh
*Units\u327x3_1.png
 SIMURGH
The Simurgh is an uncommon Life realm Fantastic creature. Simurghs, also known as celestial griffins, are powerful and wise leonine birds aligned with the right-hand aspect of the Primal Force. They are immune to poison and unnatural death, and have healing abilities for those they deem harmless. As heralds of divine miracles, Simurghs can amplify magical effects to greater potency. They are also known for their preference for eating coatls.
 
The Conjurer could study how to summon Simurgh with Conjuring Pact if has at least 4 Life Books.
#UA Skeleton
*Units\u165x3_1.png
 SKELETON
The Skeleton is a common Death realm Fantastic creature. Skeletons are animated remains of mortal beings, brought to life by the power of the Death aspect of the Primal Force. They are not living creatures and lack biological functions, emotions, or a soul. Their hard tissue may keep moving, but they are driven only by the magic that animates them, continuing until they eventually crumble and return to dust. Skeletons are impervious to cold, poison, and small projectiles.
 
The Conjurer could study how to summon Skeletons with Conjuring Pact if has at least 2 Death Books.
#UA Ghoul
*Units\u166x3_1.png
 GHOUL
The Ghoul is a common Death realm Fantastic creature. Ghouls are servants of the left-hand aspect of the Primal Force, appearing as creepy humanoid creatures with green skin and gnarled faces. They have the power to raise the deceased as undead servants, bringing those who die by their hand back to life as undead. This grants the deceased another chance to exist in the material world, albeit in a transformed, lifeless form. Ghouls dwell in death, wielding the powers of the left-hand aspect.
 
The Conjurer could study how to summon Ghouls with Conjuring Pact if has at least 2 Death Books.
#UA Night Stalker
*Units\u167x3_1.png
 NIGHT STALKER
The Night Stalker is an uncommon Death realm Fantastic creature. Night Stalkers are stealthy and mysterious hunters aligned with the left-hand aspect of the Primal Force. Their true form remains unseen by most, as they are invisible, only detectable by their glowing red eyes in the darkness. These eyes foretell imminent death for anyone who encounters them.
 
The Conjurer could study how to summon Night Stalker with Conjuring Pact if has at least 4 Death Books.
#UA Werewolf
*Units\u168x3_1.png
 WEREWOLF
The Werewolf is an uncommon Death realm Fantastic creature. Werewolves are humanoid creatures with wolf-like traits, including elongated heads, sharp teeth, claws, and fur. Known for their feral nature and frenzied behavior, they are driven by a primal hunger. Originating from mortals exposed to the chaotic power of the left-hand aspect mixed with beast essence, they retain some of their humanity but gradually lose their minds.
 
The Conjurer could study how to summon Werewolves with Conjuring Pact if has at least 4 Death Books.
#UA Demon
*Units\u169x3_1.png
 DEMON
The Demon is a rare Death realm Fantastic creature. Demons are a race seeking domination over the left-hand aspect of the Primal Force. Often used as a colloquial term for lesser members of the demonic hierarchy, demons are powerful spellcasters and leaders of the undead, capable of raising fallen enemies as undead servants. Contrary to popular belief, demons did not originate from the realm of Death, but were once beings of Life who became consumed by desires for material power and eternal existence.
 
The Conjurer could study how to summon Demon with Conjuring Pact if has at least 6 Death Books.
#UA Wraith
*Units\u170x3_1.png
 WRAITH
The Wraith is a rare Death realm Fantastic creature. Wraiths are restless spirits of the dead, preserved by the power of the left-hand aspect of the Primal Force. Non-corporeal and lacking a physical form, wraiths can fly and pass through walls without hindrance. They drain life force from the living to sustain themselves, turning their victims into cursed undead who share their fate. Though they may retain emotions, wraiths cannot hold onto them permanently or change their state.
 
The Conjurer could study how to summon Wraiths with Conjuring Pact if has at least 6 Death Books.
#UA Shadow Demon
*Units\u171x3_1.png
 SHADOW DEMON
The Shadow demon is an uncommon Death realm Fantastic creature. Shadow demons are demonic creatures made entirely of shadows and dark energy. They float through the sky, using blasts of dark energy to attack mortals. While they can travel freely across most planes, their movement is restricted by the power of wizard towers. Shadow demons cannot die easily; if destroyed, they quickly reform in their original state.
 
The Conjurer could study how to summon Shadow Demons with Conjuring Pact if has at least 4 Death Books.
#UA Death Knight
*Units\u172x3_1.png
 DEATH KNIGHT
The Death Knight is a very rare Death realm Fantastic creature. Death knights are powerful champions of the left-hand aspect of the Primal Force, reapers of souls raised from fallen, once powerful mortals. Riding supernatural black steeds, they are known as riders of the apocalypse. While they retain memories and personalities, they lack emotions that could interfere with their mission to enforce the left-hand aspect's order, and restore and maintain the Balance.
 
The Conjurer could study how to summon Death Knights with Conjuring Pact if has at least 8 Death Books.
#UA Demon Lord
*Units\u173x3_1.png
 DEMON LORD
The Demon Lord is a very rare Death realm Fantastic creature. Demon Lords are powerful beings that rule over lesser demons in the demonic hierarchy. Originally graceful denizens of Life, their obsession with dominating the left-hand aspect of the Primal Force transformed them into grotesque abominations. While they lost their beauty, they gained immense power, commanding legions of demons and undead. Demon Lords are known to negotiate with powerful wizards to further their goals.
 
The Conjurer could study how to summon Demon Lord with Conjuring Pact if has at least 8 Death Books.
#UA Zombie
*Units\u174x3_1.png
 ZOMBIE
The Zombie is a common Death realm Fantastic creature. Zombies are reanimated corpses driven by an insatiable hunger for flesh. Though decaying, they possess surprising strength and are controlled by necromancers. Mindless and instinct-driven, they serve as undead minions. Victims of zombies may be transformed into functional undead under the control of their necromantic masters.
 
The Conjurer could study how to summon Zombies with Conjuring Pact if has at least 2 Death Books.
#UA Vampire Lord
*Units\u199x3_1.png
 VAMPIRE LORD
The Vampire Lord is a rare Death realm Fantastic creature. Vampire Lords are powerful vampires who rule over lesser vampires, undead, and sometimes mortals. Once mortals who sought eternal life and power through the left-hand aspect of the Primal Force, they possess timeless beauty and strength at the cost of a bloodthirsty nature. Known for their wealth, beauty, and social influence, Vampire Lords live opulent yet dark lives.
 
The Conjurer could study how to summon Vampire Lord with Conjuring Pact if has at least 6 Death Books.
#UA Ghost Ship
*Units\u253x3_1.png
 GHOST SHIP
The Ghost Ship is a rare Death realm Fantastic creature. Ghost Ships are non-corporeal vessels crewed by undead spirits. More a phenomenon than a creature, these ships transport lost souls unable to find rest in the afterlife. Damned to sail eternally, they traverse land, water, and sky, attacking any unfortunate souls in their path.
 
The Conjurer could study how to summon Ghost Ship with Conjuring Pact if has at least 6 Death Books.
#UA Arch Demon Lord
*Units\u282x3_1.png
 ARCH DEMON LORD
The Arch Demon Lord is a forbidden Death realm Fantastic creature. Arch Demon Lords are the sovereigns at the top of the demonic hierarchy, ruling over demon lords and lesser demons. Once among the highest beings of Life, their relentless desire to dominate the left-hand aspect of the Primal Force turned them into malevolent abominations. Although their attempt to seize control failed, their corruption tainted the left-hand aspect, and the struggle for dominance continues to this day.
 
The Conjurer could study how to summon Arch Demon Lord with Conjuring Pact if has at least 12 Death Books.
#UA Arch Lich
*Units\u330x3_1.png
 ARCH LICH
The Arch Lich is a rare Death realm Fantastic creature, also known as dark priests or priests of Death. Once powerful priests or magicians, they undergo self-mortification rituals to transform into undead beings while retaining their mental faculties. These beings, known as liches, tap into the power of the left-hand aspect of the Primal Force without the usual consequences. Arch Liches can commune with the dead and gather followers seeking spiritual salvation and a tailored afterlife.
 
The Conjurer could study how to summon Arch Liches with Conjuring Pact if has at least 6 Death Books.
